§ Exile Beyond Fact and Fiction 事实与虚构消亡的流放地
An Ontology of Cults 邪教本体论

An Exile Beyond Fact and Fiction 事实与虚构消亡的流放地

The ideal subject of totalitarian rule is not the convinced Nazi or the convinced Communist, but people for whom the distinction between fact and fiction (i.e., the reality of experience) and the distinction between true and false (i.e., the standards of thought) no longer exist. Hannah Arendt, The Origins of Totalitarianism (1951)
There are three powers, three powers alone, able to conquer and to hold captive forever the conscience of these impotent rebels for their happiness — those forces are miracle, mystery, and authority. Fyodor Dostoevsky, The Brothers Karamazov, "The Grand Inquisitor" (1880)
The thought-reform program is a milieu in which everyone speaks in the language of redemption, but no one is permitted to ask, "redemption from what?" Robert Jay Lifton, Thought Reform and the Psychology of Totalism (1961)
极权统治的理想对象不是坚定的纳粹或坚定的共产党人,而是事实与虚构的区分(即经验之实在性)与真假的区分(即思想之标准)对他们而言不复存在的人。 汉娜·阿伦特《极权主义的起源》(1951)
三种力量,惟此三种力量,足以永远征服并俘虏这些无能反叛者的良心——为了他们的幸福——这些力量是:神迹、神秘与权威。 陀思妥耶夫斯基,《卡拉马佐夫兄弟》"宗教大法官"(1880)
思想改造之程序所在之环境是这样的:其中每个人都说着救赎的语言,但没有人被允许问:"从什么之中救赎?" 罗伯特·杰伊·利夫顿《思想改造与极权主义心理学》(1961)

§ Preface 导论

On What Makes a Cult 邪教之"邪"

In contemporary religious studies and the sociology of religion, the word cult has been largely displaced by the term New Religious Movement (NRM). The displacement has institutional history and stated reasons. The reasons include: that cult carries pejorative connotation incompatible with scholarly neutrality; that early anti-cult activism (1970s–1980s) used the word to justify abusive practices such as forcible deprogramming; that there is no clean ontological line between a "cult" and the more respectable religions which were themselves heterodox movements once; and that applying the term primarily to non-Western or non-mainstream groups encodes an unexamined cultural asymmetry.

These reasons are not without merit, and the methodological literature defending them — chiefly Eileen Barker, J. Gordon Melton, Massimo Introvigne — represents serious scholarship. The argument here is not that the methodological worries were fabricated, but that the response to them has been disproportionate: the field has handled a problem of nuance by abandoning the category altogether. The result is a vocabulary in which Samuel Bateman's organisation, in which a 9-year-old child was given as a "wife" in exchange for two bags of chips and fifty dollars, is grouped under the same generic kind as Mormonism, Reform Judaism, and Zen Buddhism in America.

The flattening matters for two reasons, one conceptual and one ethical.

Conceptually, the move repeats a mistake that the ontology of vague boundaries has done much to expose: the absence of a sharp line does not entail the absence of a distinction. A mountain and a hill have no precise boundary, but mountains and hills are different things. Morning and noon shade into one another, but they are different times. The fact that there are borderline cases between a strict religious order and a destructive cult does not show that the categories collapse into one another; it shows only that the categories have a fuzzy boundary, like almost every other social ontological category. The NRM framework treats vagueness as if it required obliteration of the distinction. It does not.

Ethically, the abandonment of cult produces what Miranda Fricker has called hermeneutic injustice: the deprivation of a group's capacity to name its own experience. A person harmed by Samuel Bateman's organisation does not have, within the NRM vocabulary, an adequate word for what was done to her. "I am a survivor of a new religious movement" is a grammatical sentence and a semantically empty one. The structural fact of the violence done to her requires structural vocabulary, which NRM, designed to be neutral, deliberately refuses to provide.

The working assumption throughout is that cult names a real ontological kind, that the kind admits of a structural definition observable without prior moral judgement, and that the kind is distinguishable — vaguely but reliably — from religion as such. The chapters that follow construct that definition, identify its theoretical antecedents, examine paradigm cases, mark the genuine difficulties, and end with the question of how legal and institutional systems have responded to a phenomenon that the academic study of religion has, in significant part, refused to name.

A second avoidance, distinct from the NRM-school's avoidance, must also be addressed up front. The clinical anti-cult school — Lifton, Singer, Hassan, Lalich — retains the term cult, but locates the disorder in the cult leader and in the organisational machinery of thought reform, methodologically prescinding from the question of doctrinal content. On this prescinding view, the cult is what the leader does to the members; the doctrine is interchangeable filler. Against this prescinding: cult-susceptibility has a doctrinal substrate as well as an organisational one, and the failure to face this substrate is a second hermeneutic injustice done to cult survivors — the first being the NRM-school's withdrawal of the term itself. Chapter I develops the organisational layer of the ontology; Chapter II develops the doctrinal layer.

在当代宗教研究与宗教社会学中,邪教一词已大体被新兴宗教运动(NRM)所取代。这种取代有其制度史与所声明的理由,包括:邪教一词所携带的贬义色彩不符合学术中立性的要求;早期反邪教运动(1970–80 年代)曾使用此词来为强制"去编程"等虐待性实践辩护;在所谓"邪教"与那些更受尊敬的宗教(它们自身也曾是异端运动)之间不存在清晰的本体论界线;且将该术语主要应用于非西方或非主流群体,会编码一种未被审视的文化不对称。

这些理由并非毫无根据,为其辩护的方法论文献——主要是 Eileen Barker、J. Gordon Melton、Massimo Introvigne 等人——亦属严肃学术。问题不在这些方法论关切纯属虚构,而在回应失衡:学界以放弃整个范畴的方式来处理本应是细节区分的问题。其结果是一种词汇体系,在其中,Samuel Bateman 的组织——一个 9 岁孩子被以"两袋薯片加 50 美元"作为"妻子"交付的组织——被归入与摩门教、改革派犹太教、美国禅宗同一个通用种类之下。

这种扁平化重要,有两个原因:概念上的,以及伦理上的。

概念上,这一术语转移重蹈了模糊边界本体论已大力揭示的一个错误:清晰界线的缺失,并不蕴涵区分的缺失。山与丘之间没有精确的边界,但山与丘是不同的事物。早晨与正午彼此过渡,但它们是不同的时刻。在严格的宗教秩序与破坏性邪教之间存在边缘案例,这并不表明这两个范畴坍缩为同一个,它只表明这两个范畴之间存在模糊边界——一如几乎所有其他社会本体论范畴。NRM 框架将模糊性视为足以消除区分的根据。它不是。

伦理上,放弃邪教一词造成了 Miranda Fricker 所谓的诠释学不正义(hermeneutic injustice):剥夺一个群体命名自身经验的能力。在 NRM 词汇内,一位被 Samuel Bateman 组织所伤害的人,缺乏一个充分的词来命名她所遭遇之事。"我是一个新兴宗教运动的幸存者"是一个语法上合法、语义上空洞的句子。她所遭暴力的结构性事实,要求结构性的词汇;而 NRM——由于其有意为之的"中立"——拒绝提供这一词汇。

据此：邪教是一个真实的本体论种类,这一种类可被结构性地定义(其特征可被观察,无需先做道德判断),且这一种类可与宗教本身区分——边界模糊但可靠。后续各章将构建这一定义、辨识其理论先驱、考察典范案例、标注真实困难,并以"法律与制度系统如何回应一个学界宗教研究在相当程度上拒绝命名的现象"作结。

还有第二种回避,与 NRM 学派之回避不同,亦需在开头予以面对。临床反邪教学派——Lifton、Singer、Hassan、Lalich——保留了邪教一词,却将病灶定位于邪教首要分子与思想改造的组织机制,在方法论上悬置教义内容的问题。在此种悬置之视角下,邪教即首领对成员所为之事;教义则是可互换之填充物。反对此种悬置:邪教易感性既有组织层底层,亦有教义层底层;未能正视教义层底层,即对邪教幸存者所做的第二重诠释学不正义——第一重即 NRM 学派对该词本身的撤销。第一章开展本体论之组织层;第二章开展教义层。

I. Chapter One 第 一 章

Heresy and Cult: A Formal Distinction 异端与邪教:形式性区分

Two judgements that are routinely conflated must be held apart. Heresy is a doctrinal-layer judgement passed by a host tradition on a branch deviating from its orthodox standards. Cult is an organisational-layer judgement determined by four structural conditions independent of doctrinal content. The two can combine in any of four ways. This chapter sets out the formal system in which every subsequent chapter operates: definitions, axioms, theorems, diagnostic matrix, notation.

两个常被混淆的判断须分开:异端是教义层判断,由母传统按其正统标准对偏离分支作出;邪教是组织层判断,由四个独立于教义内容之结构性条件决定。二者之组合有四种可能。本章建立后续各章所运行之形式系统:定义、公理、定理、诊断矩阵、记号。

§ 1 — Definitions § 1 — 定义
Def 1 Heresy 异端

Heresy is a doctrinal-layer predicate. A branch B is heretical relative to host tradition T just in case B holds doctrinal positions deviating from T's orthodox standards (creed, canon, authoritative interpretation). Notation: Heretic(B, T).

异端是教义层谓词。分支 B 相对于母传统 T 为异端,当且仅当 B 持有偏离 T 正统标准(信经、正典、权威诠释)之教义立场。记为 Heretic(B, T)。

Def 2 Cult 邪教

Cult is an organisational-layer predicate. An organisation G is a cult just in case it satisfies all four conditions O1–O4 listed in Def 3. Notation: Cult(G).

邪教是组织层谓词。组织 G 为邪教,当且仅当其同时满足下文 Def 3 所列之全部四条件 O1–O4。记为 Cult(G)。

Def 3 Organisational Conditions 组织条件

The four conditions whose conjunction defines Cult(G):

  • O1 — Epistemic Closure (认识论闭合): members are systematically deprived of capacity to evaluate the organisation's claims by independent standards; external information is pre-filtered, internal dissent is reframed as pathology or sin.
  • O2 — Authority Centralisation (权威单一化): doctrinal and operational authority is concentrated in a single living person or a small unaccountable body; that authority is not subject to revision by external reference.
  • O3 — Metaphysicalised Exit-Cost (出口成本形而上学化): leaving the organisation is constructed within the system as carrying infinite cost — damnation, ontological annihilation, loss of all that makes life intelligible — such that exit becomes unthinkable from within the frame.
  • O4 — Comprehensive Frame-Coverage (概念框架全覆盖): the organisation's conceptual framework adjudicates over every domain of experience (work, family, sexuality, diet, dress, friendship, art, illness, death), leaving no domain in which the member can stand outside the frame.

合取定义 Cult(G) 之四条件:

  • O1 — 认识论闭合(Epistemic Closure):成员被系统性地剥夺以独立标准评估组织主张之能力;外部信息被预先过滤,内部异议被重述为病理或罪。
  • O2 — 权威单一化(Authority Centralisation):教义与运作权威集中于单一在世之人或一无问责之小团体;该权威不接受外部参照之修订。
  • O3 — 出口成本形而上学化(Metaphysicalised Exit-Cost):离开组织在系统内被构造为承担无限代价——永罚、本体论消亡、丧失一切使生活可被理解者——以致离开在框架内成为不可设想。
  • O4 — 概念框架全覆盖(Comprehensive Frame-Coverage):组织之概念框架裁定一切经验领域(工作、家庭、性、饮食、衣着、友谊、艺术、疾病、死亡),无任何领域使成员能站在框架之外。

Detailed elaboration in Chapter II §2.

详细阐述见第二章 §2。

Def 4 Doctrinal Susceptibility 教义易感性

A doctrinal structure d is cult-susceptible just in case its combination with the O-set in Def 3 makes Cult(G) more probable. The six recurrent susceptibility structures are:

  • D-a — Continuing Revelation (持续启示): living person authorised to receive new revelation overriding prior doctrine.
  • D-b — End-Times Eschatology (末世论): imminent, this-worldly, human-action-requiring eschatology; especially in date-setting form.
  • D-c — Gnostic Dualism (灵知二元论): salvation through esoteric knowledge accessible only via the tradition's inner pathway.
  • D-d — Esoteric Initiation (密法授受): tiered membership with the highest teachings secret, transmitted only through master-disciple lineage.
  • D-e — Mystical Theosis / Divine Embodiment (神化 / 在世神身): a specific living individual identified as divine or above ordinary human conditions.
  • D-f — Sacralised Marriage and Sexuality (神圣化的婚姻与性): marital or sexual configuration as bearing soteriological function under tradition's authority.

教义结构 d 为邪教易感,当且仅当其与 Def 3 之 O 集合取时使 Cult(G) 更可能。本页识别六个反复出现之易感结构:

  • D-a — 持续启示(Continuing Revelation):在世人物被授权接受新启示以废止过往教义。
  • D-b — 末世论(End-Times Eschatology):临近、此世、需人之行动之末世论;尤其在设日期化形式。
  • D-c — 灵知二元论(Gnostic Dualism):救赎通过仅经传统之内部路径所及之秘传知识。
  • D-d — 密法授受(Esoteric Initiation):分层成员制,最高教导保密,仅通过师徒法脉传递。
  • D-e — 神化 / 在世神身(Mystical Theosis):具体在世个体被认定为神或超越普通人类状态。
  • D-f — 神圣化的婚姻与性(Sacralised Marriage and Sexuality):婚姻或性之配置在传统权威之下承载救赎论功能。

Detailed elaboration in Chapter III §2.

详细阐述见第三章 §2。

§ 2 — Axioms § 2 — 公理
Ax 1 Independence 独立性

The predicates Heretic(B, T) and Cult(G) are logically independent: the truth-value of either does not entail the truth-value of the other. The conflation of them is the root error of both NRM-school and clinical-school cult studies.

谓词 Heretic(B, T) 与 Cult(G) 在逻辑上独立:任一者之真值不蕴涵另一者之真值。二者之混淆是 NRM 学派与临床学派邪教研究双方之根本错误。

Ax 2 Host-Tradition Relativity 母传统相对性

The heresy predicate is always indexed to a host tradition T. When no host tradition applies — i.e., when G derives from no religious tradition — Heretic(G, T) is undefined. Written Heretic(G, ⊥) = undef.

异端谓词总是相对某一母传统 T 而被索引。当无适用母传统时——即 G 不源自任何宗教传统时——Heretic(G, T) 未定义。记为 Heretic(G, ⊥) = undef。

Ax 3 Organisational Absoluteness 组织绝对性

The cult predicate Cult(G) is absolute: it does not depend on any host tradition, only on G's own organisational properties (the O-set of Def 3). A secular organisation can satisfy Cult(G) without any reference to religious doctrine.

邪教谓词 Cult(G) 是绝对的:它不依赖于任何母传统,仅依赖于 G 自身之组织属性(Def 3 之 O 集)。一个世俗组织可在不涉及任何宗教教义之情况下满足 Cult(G)。

Ax 4 Susceptibility ≠ Realisation 易感性 ≠ 实现

Satisfying a subset of the D-set (Def 4) implies only that G is cult-susceptible — not that G is a cult. The full O-set (Def 3) must also hold. Doctrinal susceptibility is necessary but not sufficient for organisational cult-emergence.

满足 D 集(Def 4)之子集仅蕴涵 G 邪教易感——而非 G 为邪教。须 O 集全部(Def 3)亦成立。教义易感性是组织性邪教浮现之必要而非充分条件。

§ 3 — Theorems § 3 — 定理
Th 1 Heresy ≠ Cult 异端非邪教

By Ax 1 and Ax 3: there exist branches B such that Heretic(B, T) ∧ ¬Cult(B). Examples: mainline LDS relative to Nicene Christianity; Bahá'í Faith relative to Shia Islam; Unitarian Universalists relative to Trinitarian Christianity; Christadelphians relative to Nicene Christianity. These are New Religious Movements in the strict sense — heretical from their host traditions but not organisationally cultic.

由 Ax 1 与 Ax 3:存在分支 B 使得 Heretic(B, T) ∧ ¬Cult(B)。例:主流 LDS 相对尼西亚基督教;巴哈伊信仰相对什叶派伊斯兰;Unitarian Universalist 相对三位一体基督教;Christadelphian 相对尼西亚基督教。此等为严格意义之新兴宗教运动——对其母传统而言为异端但在组织上非邪教。

Th 2 Cult ≠ Heresy 邪教非异端

By Ax 1 and Ax 2: there exist organisations G such that Cult(G) ∧ Heretic(G, ⊥) = undef. Examples: NXIVM, Synanon, the Manson Family, the Kim cult of personality (DPRK), Khmer Rouge. The cult predicate applies; the heresy predicate is undefined because no host tradition supplies the orthodoxy standard.

由 Ax 1 与 Ax 2:存在组织 G 使得 Cult(G) ∧ Heretic(G, ⊥) = undef。例:NXIVM、Synanon、Manson Family、朝鲜金氏个人崇拜、红色高棉。邪教谓词适用;异端谓词未定义,因无母传统提供正统标准。

Th 3 Both 两者皆是

There exist organisations G such that Heretic(G, T) ∧ Cult(G). This is the strongest negative diagnosis. Examples: FLDS, Aum Shinrikyo, Church of Almighty God, Branch Davidians, Heaven's Gate, Peoples Temple (post-1973). These cases are the proper objects of Chapter V case studies.

存在组织 G 使得 Heretic(G, T) ∧ Cult(G)。此为最强负面诊断。例:FLDS、奥姆真理教、全能神教会、Branch Davidians、天堂之门、人民圣殿教(1973 年后)。此类案例是第五章案例研究之恰当对象。

Th 4 Susceptibility Transfer 易感性传递

By Ax 4: if G satisfies at least one element of Def 4's D-set, then G is cult-susceptible; if G further satisfies all four elements of Def 3's O-set, then Cult(G). Mainline LDS satisfies D-a + D-e + D-f, but not the full O-set, hence cult-susceptible but not cult. FLDS satisfies the same D-elements plus the full O-set, hence Cult(FLDS). The doctrinal door opened by mainline LDS is walked through by FLDS.

由 Ax 4:若 G 满足 Def 4 之 D 集至少一元,则 G 邪教易感;若 G 复满足 Def 3 之 O 集全部,则 Cult(G)。主流 LDS 满足 D-a + D-e + D-f,但不满足 O 集全部,故为邪教易感但非邪教。FLDS 满足相同 D 元素加上 O 集全部,故 Cult(FLDS)。主流 LDS 所开启之教义之门,被 FLDS 跨过。

Th 5 Twofold Avoidance 双重回避

No mainstream academic faction operates the full diagnostic space Def 1–4 + Ax 1–4 + Th 1–4. (i) NRM-school cult studies retracts the legitimacy of Cult(·). (ii) Clinical anti-cult studies retains Cult(·) but retracts the legitimacy of Heretic(·, ·). (iii) Mainstream religious studies operates Heretic(·, ·) for its own tradition only, and outsources Cult(·) to a separate subfield. The full 2-D diagnostic space is operated nowhere in the institutional academy.

无主流学术阵营运行完整诊断空间 Def 1–4 + Ax 1–4 + Th 1–4。(i)NRM 派邪教研究撤回 Cult(·) 之合法性。(ii)临床反邪教研究保留 Cult(·) 但撤回 Heretic(·, ·) 之合法性。(iii)主流宗教学只对自身传统运行 Heretic(·, ·),将 Cult(·) 外包给独立子领域。完整之二维诊断空间在制度性学界无处被运行。

§ 4 — The Diagnostic Matrix § 4 — 诊断矩阵
§ 5 — Notational Conventions § 5 — 符号约定
N 1 Naming 命名

Throughout the remainder of the page:

  • Organisational conditions are referenced as O1, O2, O3, O4.
  • Doctrinal susceptibility structures are referenced as D-a, D-b, D-c, D-d, D-e, D-f.
  • The cult predicate is written Cult(G); the heresy predicate, Heretic(G, T); cult-susceptibility, CultSusceptible(G).
  • Complete diagnoses combine the two systems. Example:
    CAG: Heretic(CAG, mainstream evangelical Christianity) ∧ Cult(CAG) ∧ (D-a + D-b + D-e + O1 + O2 + O3 + O4).

本页其余各章皆遵此记号:

  • 组织条件以 O1, O2, O3, O4 引用。
  • 教义易感结构以 D-a, D-b, D-c, D-d, D-e, D-f 引用。
  • 邪教谓词记为 Cult(G);异端谓词记为 Heretic(G, T);邪教易感性记为 CultSusceptible(G)。
  • 完整诊断为两系统之组合。例:
    CAG: Heretic(CAG, 主流福音派基督教) ∧ Cult(CAG) ∧ (D-a + D-b + D-e + O1 + O2 + O3 + O4)。
II. Chapter Two 第 二 章

A BFO-Based Ontology of Cults 基于 BFO 的邪教本体论

A cult is, in the first instance, a kind of organisation. It is not a kind of belief (cults do not share a doctrine), not a kind of feeling (joining a cult does not feel any one way), not a measure of group intensity (high-intensity groups need not be cults, and low-intensity groups occasionally are). The definition that follows distinguishes the kind by four structural conditions. It is Aristotelian in form (genus plus differentia) and BFO-compatible in execution (each clause picks out a specifiable disposition realised through specifiable processes); it should classify clear cases correctly and identify borderline cases as borderline. This is the organisational layer; Chapter II takes up the doctrinal substrate.

邪教首先是一种组织。它不是一种信念(邪教并不共享同一教义);不是一种感受(加入邪教并无固定的感受方式);也不是群体强度的度量(高强度群体未必是邪教,低强度群体偶尔是邪教)。下面的定义以四个结构性条件来标定这一种类。其形式是亚里士多德式(属加种差),其执行与 BFO 兼容(每一条款挑出一种可被指明的 disposition,通过可被指明的 processes 得以实现);它应能正确分类清晰案例,并将边缘案例标识为边缘。此处是组织层;第二章处理教义底层。

I · 1 Existing Definitions and Their Failures 现有定义及其失败 +

The Legal-Political Definition (PRC)

法律-政治定义(中华人民共和国)

The People's Republic of China defines a cult, in its judicial interpretation accompanying Articles 300 and 301 of the Criminal Law (《关于办理组织和利用邪教组织犯罪案件具体应用法律若干问题的解释》, 1999, revised 2017), as an illegal organisation that (i) appropriates the name of a religion, qigong, or other body of thought, (ii) deifies its principal members, (iii) employs the fabrication and dissemination of superstitious beliefs to bewitch and deceive others, (iv) develops and controls its membership, and (v) endangers society. The strengths of this definition are operational: it allows police, prosecutors, and courts to identify a class of organisations and prosecute them under positive law. Its weaknesses, considered as ontology, are several. Clause (v) — the endangerment-of-society requirement — is a downstream consequence, not a constitutive feature. A cult that did not endanger society (if any exists) would not, on this definition, be a cult, which is the wrong result. Clause (iii) — the fabrication-of-superstition requirement — embeds a metaphysical judgement (that the beliefs are false) which a structural definition should not require. And clause (i) — appropriation of an existing name — rules out the cult that invents its own vocabulary from the start.

中华人民共和国在《关于办理组织和利用邪教组织犯罪案件具体应用法律若干问题的解释》(1999 年,2017 年修订)中,与《刑法》第 300、301 条配套地将邪教定义为:(一)冒用宗教、气功或者其他名义,(二)神化首要分子,(三)利用制造、散布迷信邪说等手段蛊惑、蒙骗他人,(四)发展、控制成员,(五)危害社会的非法组织。此定义的长处在于其可操作性:它使公安、检察与法院得以识别一类组织并依法追诉。但作为本体论考察,它有若干弱点。第(五)条——"危害社会"——是下游后果,非构成性特征;一个不危害社会的邪教(若存在),按此定义将不是邪教,这是错误结果。第(三)条——"制造迷信邪说"——内嵌一个形而上学判断(即认定信念为假),而结构性定义不应要求此。第(一)条——"冒用既有名义"——则排除了从一开始就自创话语的邪教。

Lifton's Eight Criteria

利夫顿的八项标准

Robert Jay Lifton, in Thought Reform and the Psychology of Totalism (1961), proposed eight features of totalist thought reform systems: milieu control, mystical manipulation, demand for purity, cult of confession, sacred science, loading the language, doctrine over person, and dispensing of existence. As a clinical heuristic, Lifton's list is unsurpassed; as ontology, it is a list without a theory of itself. The eight features are not derived from a unifying principle; their interrelations are not specified; the question of which combinations are necessary or sufficient is left open. The list treats cults as Wittgensteinian family resemblance, which is a defensible position but one that forfeits the explanatory power of a structural definition.

罗伯特·杰伊·利夫顿在《思想改造与极权主义心理学》(1961)中提出极权式思想改造系统的八个特征:环境控制、神秘操纵、纯粹性要求、忏悔崇拜、神圣科学、语言改装、教义高于人、存在的赐予与剥夺。作为临床启发,利夫顿之清单无可超越;但作为本体论,它是一份没有自身理论的清单。八个特征不是从一个统一原则中推导出的;它们彼此之间的关系未被言明;哪些组合是必要的、哪些是充分的,问题悬而未决。该清单将邪教视作维特根斯坦式的家族相似——这是一个可辩护的立场,但放弃了结构性定义所具备的解释力。

Hassan's BITE Model

哈森的 BITE 模型

Steven Hassan's BITE Model — control of Behavior, Information, Thought, and Emotion — is a measurement framework rather than a definition. It tells one along which axes a group exerts control, but does not specify thresholds, nor distinguish cultic control from the high but legitimate control exercised by, for example, a military unit or a residential medical training programme. As an assessment tool the BITE Model is valuable; as a definition it under-discriminates.

Steven Hassan 的 BITE 模型——对行为(Behavior)、信息(Information)、思想(Thought)、情感(Emotion)的控制——是一个测量框架而非一个定义。它告诉人们一个群体在哪些轴线上施加控制,但未指明阈值,亦未区分邪教式控制与那些高度但合法的控制(如军队单位或住院医师培训)。作为评估工具,BITE 模型有价值;作为定义,它区分力不足。

Lalich's Bounded Choice

拉里奇的有界选择

Janja Lalich's Bounded Choice: True Believers and Charismatic Cults (2004) approaches the question from the side of the member's experience: a cult is a system within which members make decisions that are internally rational given the constructed information environment, but from outside appear unintelligible. Lalich's framework is the closest to ontology among the leading approaches because it identifies an experiential structure rather than a feature list. Building on Lalich, the four-condition definition specifies the organisational structure on the other side of the member's bounded choice — that is, what an organisation must be like in order to produce bounded choice in its members.

Janja Lalich《有界的选择:真信徒与魅力型邪教》(2004)从成员经验侧切入:邪教是一个系统,其中成员所做之决定,在被建构出的信息环境内是内在地理性的,而从外部看却难以理解。在主流路径中,Lalich 框架最接近本体论,因为它识别出一种经验结构而非特征清单。在 Lalich 之上,可进一步刻画"成员有界选择"另一侧的组织结构——即一个组织必须具备何种性质,才能在其成员中产生有界选择。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • Robert Jay Lifton, Thought Reform and the Psychology of Totalism (W. W. Norton, 1961).
  • Steven Hassan, Combating Cult Mind Control (Park Street Press, 1988; 25th-anniversary edn., 2015).
  • Janja Lalich, Bounded Choice: True Believers and Charismatic Cults (University of California Press, 2004).
  • Margaret Thaler Singer, Cults in Our Midst: The Continuing Fight Against Their Hidden Menace (Jossey-Bass, 1995; revised 2003).
  • 最高人民法院、最高人民检察院,《关于办理组织和利用邪教组织犯罪案件具体应用法律若干问题的解释》 (法释〔2017〕3 号)。
I · 2 A Four-Condition Structural Definition 四个结构条件的定义 +

The Definition

定义

A cult is an ideological community possessing the following four structural features in combination:

(1) Epistemic Closure. The community establishes an internal truth-adjudication mechanism such that no external reference point — science, other religious traditions, secular common sense, individual experience — is admissible as a legitimate ground for disagreement.

(2) Authority Centralisation. The terminus of truth-adjudication is located in a specific, living person or in agents directly appointed by him, rather than in a text, a tradition, or a community consensus.

(3) Exit-Cost Metaphysicalisation. Leaving the community is constructed not merely as a social loss but as a metaphysical loss (damnation, annihilation, loss of one's soul, ontological cessation), such that any rational decision-procedure conducted within the community's epistemic framework cannot recommend departure.

(4) Conceptual-Frame Comprehensiveness. The community's conceptual scheme claims jurisdiction over the totality of the member's experience — ethics, kinship, sexuality, the body, the future, suffering, doubt — such that thinking outside the community's frame becomes conceptually difficult.

邪教是一种意识形态共同体,具备以下四个结构性特征的组合:

(一)认识论闭合(Epistemic Closure)。共同体确立一种内部真理判定机制,使任何外部参照点——科学、其他宗教传统、世俗常识、个人经验——都不能作为合法异见之根据。

(二)权威单一化(Authority Centralisation)。真理判定的终点被定位于一个具体的、活着的人,或他直接任命的代理人身上,而非文本、传统或共同体共识。

(三)出口成本的形而上学化(Exit-Cost Metaphysicalisation)。离开共同体被建构为不仅是社会损失,更是形而上学损失(永罚、灭绝、灵魂之失、本体论上的消失),从而在共同体认识论框架内进行的任何理性决策程序,皆不可能推荐离开。

(四)概念框架的全覆盖(Conceptual-Frame Comprehensiveness)。共同体的概念体系宣称对成员经验之全部领域具有管辖权——伦理、亲属、性、身体、未来、痛苦、怀疑——从而在共同体框架之外进行思考,在概念上变得困难。

Diagrammatic Form

图示

Why These Four, and Why Together

为何是这四条,为何须合并

The four conditions are co-necessary, not independent. (1) alone is found in certain closed academic traditions (some strands of Lacanian psychoanalysis, certain hard-line Marxist schools), but in those cases the authority resides in a text or method, not a living person — so (2) is absent and exit is conceptually possible by appeal to the same texts. (2) alone is found in many religious traditions with charismatic leadership; absent (1), such leadership remains accountable to external reference points (scripture, tradition, the broader community). (3) alone is found in certain organised crime structures, which threaten metaphysical or material annihilation for departure but make no doctrinal claim. (4) alone is found in certain ideological commitments (some forms of identity politics, certain political ideologies) that claim totalising explanatory scope without an enforcement mechanism behind them.

Only the conjunction of all four produces what the term cult picks out: a community in which the member's epistemic, ethical, and existential life is administered by a single living authority, from which there is no rationally available exit. This is what the four-condition definition is meant to capture, and what the NRM framework is unable to articulate.

四条彼此互为必要,非相互独立。仅有(一)者,见于某些封闭的学术传统(某些拉康精神分析支脉、某些强硬马克思主义学派),但其权威居于文本或方法,而非在世之人——因此(二)不在,且经由对同一文本之诉求,出口在概念上仍可能。仅有(二)者,见于许多具魅力型领导的宗教传统;若无(一),此种领导仍对外部参照点(经文、传统、更广共同体)负责。仅有(三)者,见于某些有组织犯罪结构,它们以形而上学或物质消灭威胁离开者,但不作教义性宣称。仅有(四)者,见于某些意识形态承诺(某些身份政治、某些政治意识形态),它们宣称具备全覆盖之解释范围,却无后置的强制机制。

唯有四条之合取才产生"邪教"一词所指之物:一个共同体,其成员的认识、伦理与存在生活,由一个在世之单一权威所管辖,从中没有理性上可得之出口。这是四条定义意欲捕捉者,亦是 NRM 框架无法言说者。

I · 3 A BFO Reconstruction BFO 重构 +
BFO 2020 entity hierarchy · with cult-ontology extension BFO 2020 实体层级 · 邪教本体论扩展

Adapted from the BFO 2020 reference diagram in the BFO User's Guide. 图 II.1。BFO 2020 实体层级(深色)及其邪教本体论扩展(绿色虚线)。点击 +/− 圆按钮折叠或展开子树。滚轮缩放;鼠标拖动平移;触屏双指缩放。改编自《BFO 用户指南》中 BFO 2020 参考图。

Cult-Ontology Class Definitions 邪教本体论类定义
Cult (subkind of Object Aggregate)
Cult / 邪教(Object Aggregate 之子类)

An Object Aggregate whose constituent objects — members, premises, financial holdings, documentary records — collectively bear all four organisational dispositions O1, O2, O3, O4 (Def 3, Chapter I). The aggregate persists as long as it bears the four dispositions; ceasing to bear any one is sufficient for the kind to dissolve, even though the constituent members may remain.

一个对象聚合体,其构成对象(成员、场所、财务资产、文档记录)集体承载全部四个组织 dispositions O1、O2、O3、O4(第一章 Def 3)。该聚合体只要承载此四 dispositions 即持续存在;丧失其中任一即足以使该种类消解,即便构成成员仍可保留。

Religious Community (sibling subkind of Object Aggregate)
Religious Community / 宗教共同体(Object Aggregate 之同级子类)

A sibling kind to Cult: an Object Aggregate of persons and supporting material entities bound by a shared doctrinal or ritual tradition, but not bearing the full O1–O4 conjunction. Mainline religious denominations, new religious movements proper (LDS, Bahá'í, Unitarian Universalist), and most local congregations belong here.

Cult 之同级种类:由具体的人与支持性物质实体构成、被共同教义或仪式传统所束缚的对象聚合体,但不承载 O1–O4 全部合取。主流宗教宗派、严格意义之新兴宗教(LDS、巴哈伊、Unitarian Universalist)、以及多数地方会众属于此类。

Cult Compound (subkind of Site)
Cult Compound / 邪教聚居地(Site 之子类)

A Site at which a cult's processes are realised — characteristically isolated (Jonestown, Guyana), enclosed (FLDS Short Creek), or hardened (Aum's Mt. Fuji complex). The Site's spatial isolation co-realises O1 (the physical absence of external information sources) and O3 (physical distance from the prior world as part of the metaphysicalised exit cost).

一场所,邪教之 processes 在其中得到实现——具有典型的孤立性(琼斯敦)、封闭性(FLDS 短溪)或加固性(奥姆富士山院落)。该 Site 之空间孤立共同实现 O1(外部信息源之物理缺席)与 O3(与先前世界之物理距离作为形而上学出口成本之一部分)。

O1–O4 (subkinds of Disposition)
O1–O4(Disposition 之子类)

Each of the four organisational conditions is a Disposition borne by the cult-as-aggregate, realised through corresponding families of Processes: epistemic-disputation processes for O1; revelation, pronouncement, and revocation processes for O2; disfellowshipping and apostate-construction processes for O3; daily reportage, confession, and frame-extension processes for O4. Dispositions are Realizable Entities in BFO: they can be borne without being realised (a dormant cult), and are realised only through their characteristic processes.

四个组织条件之每一者皆是由邪教(作为聚合体)承载之 Disposition,通过相应 Processes 家族得到实现:O1 通过教义争辩 processes;O2 通过启示、宣告与撤销 processes;O3 通过逐出团契与叛教者建构 processes;O4 通过日常汇报、忏悔与框架扩展 processes。在 BFO 中,Disposition 是 Realizable Entity:它可被承载而未被实现(休眠之邪教),仅通过其特征性 processes 得以实现。

D-a through D-f (subkinds of Information Content Entity)
D-a 至 D-f(信息内容实体之子类)

Each cult-susceptible doctrinal structure is a Generically Dependent Continuant — specifically, an Information Content Entity (ICE) in the IAO extension of BFO. A doctrine depends generically on some carrier (scripture, oral transmission, members' minds) but is not bound to any particular carrier; the same doctrine can be instantiated in any number of carriers. This is why doctrinal substrates persist across centuries and migrate across organisational hosts (continuing revelation persists from Joseph Smith 1843 into FLDS 2022 without losing identity).

每一邪教易感教义结构皆是一类依赖持续存在体——具体说,BFO 之 IAO 扩展中的信息内容实体(ICE)。教义在类的意义上依赖于某载体(经文、口传、成员心智),但不专属于任何特定载体;同一教义可在任意数量之载体中被实例化。这正是教义底层何以能跨越数世纪持续存在,并在不同组织宿主间迁移之原因(持续启示从 Joseph Smith 1843 持续至 FLDS 2022,而不失同一性)。

Cult Leader / Cult Member / Apostate Role (subkinds of Role)
Cult Leader / Cult Member / Apostate Role(Role 之子类)

Three subkinds of Role. Each role is a Specifically Dependent Continuant borne by a specific person, and externally grounded in the existence of the cult organisation. The Apostate Role is BFO-distinctive: it persists for ex-members, often for years after physical departure, because it is constructed by the cult and continues to attach to the person from the cult's standpoint. This explains the floating phenomenology documented in cult-recovery literature — the ex-member's social-ontological position has not yet fully detached from the role.

Role 之三种子类。每一角色皆是由具体人承载之种依赖持续存在体,且外部依附于邪教组织之存在。Apostate Role 在 BFO 上具独特性:它对前成员持续存在,常在物理离开后数年仍存,因其由邪教所建构,并继续从邪教之立场附着于该人。这解释了邪教康复文献中所记录之"漂浮"现象——前成员之社会本体论位置尚未完全脱离该角色。

Recruitment / Thought-Reform / Disfellowshipping Processes (subkinds of Process)
招募 / 思想改造 / 逐出团契 Processes(Process 之子类)

Three families of Process. Each is an Occurrent unfolding in time, realising one or more of the O-dispositions, and may also serve as the vehicle by which Information Content Entities (the doctrines D-a through D-f) are instantiated in members. Lifton's eight conditions of thought reform (Chapter IV.1) are a fine-grained classification of the Thought-Reform Process family; Hassan's BITE model gives operational markers for the same family.

Process 之三种家族。每一者皆为时间中展开之 Occurrent,实现一或多个 O-disposition,并可作为信息内容实体(教义 D-a 至 D-f)在成员中被实例化之载体。Lifton 关于思想改造之八条件(第四章 IV.1)是思想改造 Process 家族之细粒度分类;Hassan 之 BITE 模型给出同一家族之操作性标识。

Cult as a Material Entity with Specifiable Dispositions

作为具有可指明 dispositions 的物质实体的邪教

Basic Formal Ontology (BFO) provides a vocabulary in which the four-condition definition can be re-expressed without remainder. A cult, as an organisation, is a material entity (an object aggregate with continuant parts, including members, premises, financial holdings, and documentary records). It bears several characteristic dispositions, each of which is realised through a corresponding family of processes:

Disposition of epistemic closure is realised in processes of doctrinal disputation, in which external claims are systematically reframed within the community's vocabulary or rejected as marks of spiritual failure. Disposition of authority centralisation is realised in processes of revelation, pronouncement, and revocation, by which the living authority issues and amends doctrine. Disposition of exit-cost metaphysicalisation is realised in processes of disfellowshipping, the casting-out ritual, and the construction of the apostate as a category of being. Disposition of conceptual coverage is realised in processes of daily reportage, confession, scheduling, ritual, and the production of community vocabulary for previously unnamed domains of experience.

Members of a cult are parts of the organisation, but not as instances of a generic role. Their roles within the cult — wife, prophet, elder, suppressive person, true believer, apostate — do not exist outside the organisation; they are externally grounded roles whose existence requires the continuing presence of the organisation. This is the BFO-level expression of what Lalich means by bounded in bounded choice: the choosing agent is constituted as a choosing agent only within the bounds of the organisation, because the categories of person available to her are categories supplied by the organisation.

基本形式本体论(BFO)提供一套词汇,可以无残余地重新表达四条定义。邪教,作为组织,是一种物质实体(material entity)——一个对象聚合体(object aggregate),其连续部分(continuant parts)包括成员、场所、财务资产与文档记录。它承载若干特征性dispositions,每一种都通过相应的processes家族得以实现:

认识论闭合 disposition 通过教义争辩 processes 实现——外部主张被系统地重述于共同体词汇中,或被驳斥为灵性失败之标记。权威单一化 disposition 通过启示、宣告与撤销 processes 实现——在世权威由此发布与修订教义。出口成本形而上学化 disposition 通过逐出团契、放逐仪式、以及将"叛教者"建构为一种存在范畴等 processes 实现。概念覆盖 disposition 通过日常汇报、忏悔、日程安排、仪式、以及为先前未被命名之经验领域生产共同体词汇等 processes 实现。

邪教成员是组织的部分(parts),但不是某种通用角色之实例。他们在邪教内的角色——妻子、先知、长老、抑制性人物、真信徒、叛教者——不在组织之外存在;它们是外部依附的(externally grounded)角色,其存在依赖于组织的持续存在。这是 BFO 层面上 Lalich 所谓"有界选择"之"有界"的表达:选择主体被建构为选择主体,只在组织之界内成立,因为其所能选择之"人之范畴",由组织所提供。

Ontological Significance of the BFO Move

BFO 重构的本体论意义

The BFO reconstruction does two things. First, it removes the residual normativity from the four-condition definition: each clause refers to an observable structural feature of an organisation, not to a moral judgement about it. The harm produced by cults follows mechanically from the structure (a member whose roles depend on the organisation cannot leave without ontological loss), but the definition does not need to mention harm to identify the kind. Second, it places the ontology of cults within a wider ontological vocabulary used in clinical, biological, and information-systems research. This makes the definition cross-disciplinarily portable: a clinical psychologist, a sociologist, and a legal scholar working with BFO can refer to the same entity-type without disciplinary translation.

BFO 重构做两件事。其一,它从四条定义中去除残余规范性:每一条款都指向组织的可观察结构性特征,而非对其的道德判断。邪教所致之危害,从结构机械地推导而出(其角色依赖组织之成员,无法在不承担本体论损失的条件下离开),但定义本身不必提及危害,即可识别该种类。其二,它将邪教本体论置于临床、生物学与信息系统研究所共享的更宽本体论词汇之内。这使该定义具备跨学科可携带性:运用 BFO 的临床心理学家、社会学家与法学者,可指称同一实体类型,而无需跨学科翻译。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • Robert Arp, Barry Smith, Andrew D. Spear, Building Ontologies with Basic Formal Ontology (MIT Press, 2015).
  • Barry Smith et al., "The OBO Foundry: Coordinated Evolution of Ontologies to Support Biomedical Data Integration" Nature Biotechnology 25 (2007): 1251–55.
  • Janja Lalich, Bounded Choice: True Believers and Charismatic Cults (University of California Press, 2004).
I · 4 Testing the Definition: Boundary Cases 检验定义:边界案例 +

Clear Positive Cases

清晰阳性案例

FLDS under Warren Jeffs and again under Samuel Bateman: all four conditions satisfied in their strong form. Authority is centralised in a living "prophet"; external Mormonism, secular law, and member doubt are all reframed as spiritual failure; departure is configured as eternal damnation in the celestial hierarchy of the Mormon afterlife; and the conceptual frame covers reproductive arrangements, dress, speech, finance, and movement.

Peoples Temple under Jim Jones: all four. Authority in Jones; closure achieved by a syncretic vocabulary that absorbed external critique as evidence of conspiracy; exit construed as betrayal of "the cause," with members trained for the eventual "revolutionary suicide"; frame covers everything down to the schedule of meals and the wording of letters home.

Aum Shinrikyo under Shoko Asahara: all four, with the additional escalation to physical violence; exit-cost included literal murder of departing members. Scientology: all four, satisfied by different mechanisms; closure through the doctrine that critics are "Suppressive Persons" whose speech is by definition suspect; centralisation in the office of Chairman of the Board, Religious Technology Center; exit through the policy of "Disconnection" and the metaphysical category of being "out-ethics"; frame extends to "thetan" identity across multiple lifetimes.

杰夫斯与贝特曼时期之 FLDS:四条以强形式悉数满足。权威集中于在世"先知";外部摩门教、世俗法律与成员怀疑皆被重述为灵性失败;离开被配置为天体层级中的永罚;概念框架覆盖生育安排、衣着、言说、财务与行动。

琼斯领导下之人民圣殿教:四条悉数满足。权威在琼斯;闭合通过混合词汇达成,该词汇吸纳外部批评为阴谋之证据;离开被理解为对"事业"之背叛,成员被训练以备最终之"革命性自杀";框架覆盖一切,包括饮食日程与给家人书信之措辞。

麻原彰晃领导下之奥姆真理教:四条悉数满足,并升级为物理暴力;出口成本包括对离开者的实际谋杀。山达基:四条以不同机制满足;闭合通过"批评者皆为'抑制性人物'(SP),其言说按定义不可信"之教义;集中在宗教技术中心董事长办公室;离开通过"切断"政策与"伦理失常"的形而上学范畴;框架延伸至多生多世之"theta"身份。

Clear Negative Cases

清晰阴性案例

Mainline LDS (Mormon Church): satisfies (2) (a living prophet) and partly (4) (extensive scope), but fails (1) — modern science is officially embraced, including evolution — and fails (3) — leaving the Church incurs social and familial loss but is not officially constructed as eternal damnation. Not a cult.

The United States Marine Corps: high control over behaviour, information, thought, and emotion, but fails (2) (authority is structural, not personal) and fails (4) (no jurisdiction over religion, kinship, or worldview outside service). Not a cult.

A Trappist monastery: high coverage of daily life (4) and significant authority of the abbot (2), but the abbot's authority is internal to a larger tradition (Catholic Church) that supplies an external reference point (1), and departure, while spiritually weighted, is not constructed as damnation (3). Not a cult.

主流摩门教(LDS):满足(二)(有在世先知),部分满足(四)(覆盖广),但不满足(一)——现代科学(包括演化论)被正式接受——且不满足(三)——离开教会会带来社会与家庭损失,但官方并未将其构造为永罚。不是邪教。

美国海军陆战队:对行为、信息、思想、情感施加高度控制,但不满足(二)(权威是结构性的,非个人的),亦不满足(四)(对服役之外的宗教、亲属、世界观无管辖权)。不是邪教。

特拉普会修道院:日常生活覆盖度高(四),院长权威显著(二),但院长权威内嵌于一个更大的传统(天主教会)之中,后者提供了一个外部参照点(一);离开虽有灵性分量,但未被建构为永罚(三)。不是邪教。

Borderline Cases

边缘案例

Some MLM organisations: partial (1) (internal vocabulary that reframes external skepticism as "failure mindset"); partial (2) (charismatic founder); partial (3) (departure constructed as evidence of personal weakness rather than damnation, but the metaphysics is thinner); partial (4) (covers business, mindset, social life, sometimes more). Borderline — best classified as cult-like or quasi-cultic.

Certain extreme political cells: a Maoist cell of the Cultural Revolution period in its most intense phase, certain North Korean institutional substructures, certain extremist cells in the contemporary far right. These often satisfy (1), (3), and (4); whether they satisfy (2) depends on whether authority is properly understood as residing in a living person or in a textual canon. Where (2) is met, the four-condition definition applies; where (2) is unmet, the structure is better described by an adjacent term such as totalist or totalitarian cell.

Some intense charismatic Pentecostal churches: high (4), strong (2), but variable on (1) (often interfaces with mainstream Christianity) and (3) (often allows departure with social cost only). Most such churches are not cults on the four-condition definition, but some specific congregations have drifted across the threshold.

某些多层次直销(MLM)组织:部分满足(一)(内部词汇将外部怀疑重述为"失败心态");部分满足(二)(有魅力型创始人);部分满足(三)(将离开建构为个人软弱之证据而非永罚,形而上学较薄);部分满足(四)(覆盖业务、心态、社交,有时更多)。属边缘案例——最好归类为"邪教式"(cult-like)或"准邪教"(quasi-cultic)。

某些极端政治小组:文革最激烈阶段之某些毛主义小组、朝鲜某些机构子结构、当代极右某些极端小组。它们常满足(一)、(三)、(四);是否满足(二)取决于权威是否被恰当地理解为居于一个在世之人或居于一个文本经典之中。当(二)成立,四条定义适用;当(二)不成立,该结构最好以"极权式"(totalist)或"极权小组"(totalitarian cell)等邻近术语描述。

某些激烈的灵恩派五旬节教会:(四)高,(二)强,但(一)上不一(常与主流基督教接口),(三)上可变(常仅以社会成本允许离开)。按四条定义,大多数此类教会非邪教,但某些具体会众已漂移过阈值。

The Vagueness Is Not a Bug

模糊性不是缺陷

That the definition produces a continuous gradation between paradigm cults and clear non-cults, with borderline cases in between, is not a failure of the definition. It is what a correct definition should produce for a social ontological category whose instances vary along multiple structural dimensions. The mistake of the NRM framework is not its recognition of vagueness; it is the inference from vagueness to category dissolution. The four-condition definition models the vagueness without dissolving the category.

该定义在典型邪教与清晰非邪教之间产生一种连续分级,边缘案例居中——这不是定义之失败。对一个社会本体论范畴而言,其实例沿多个结构维度变化,正确的定义应产生此种结果。NRM 框架的错误,不在它对模糊性之承认,而在它从模糊性推出范畴消解。四条定义为模糊性建模,而不消解范畴。

Unresolved Tensions 未解张力

Difficulties Internal to the Four-Condition Definition 四条定义自身的困难

  1. The threshold problem. The four conditions admit of degree. At what intensity does a feature "count" as satisfied? The honest answer is that there is no sharp threshold, only a continuous gradation — which is what the boundary-case analysis tries to handle. But this means that any prescription based on the definition (legal, clinical, journalistic) will inherit the threshold problem.
  2. The first-generation problem. The definition is built around features that mature cults exhibit. A nascent organisation may possess these features only in inchoate form, and the question of when it crosses the threshold is itself underdetermined. Was Bateman's group a cult before he openly declared himself prophet? When?
  3. The textual-authority edge case. Some organisations centralise authority in a deceased founder's text rather than a living person, but operate functionally identically. The definition's clause (2) excludes them strictly; is this the right call, or should the definition be generalised to "concentrated, unaccountable authority, whether textual or personal"? If generalised, the definition becomes broader and risks capturing more legitimate religious traditions.
  4. The secular-cult problem. Some organisations satisfy all four conditions but make no religious or metaphysical claim (certain therapeutic communities, certain political-totalist cells, certain corporate cults). The exit-cost in such cases is secular rather than metaphysical. Should the definition be expanded to admit secular forms of exit-cost (loss of self, loss of meaning, social annihilation) as functionally equivalent to metaphysical loss? The expansion has plausibility but weakens the specificity of clause (3).
  5. The verification problem. Whether a community satisfies the four conditions requires testimony from inside, which is precisely what cultic structure makes unreliable. Members in good standing will under-report features (because the community's vocabulary reframes them); exited members will over-report features (because of post-exit reinterpretation). The definition is testable in principle but the evidence is structurally compromised.
  6. 阈值问题。四条均允许程度变化。一个特征以何种强度才"算"满足?诚实的答案是:并无明确阈值,只有连续分级——这正是边界案例分析所欲处理者。但这意味着,任何基于此定义的规范性主张(法律、临床、新闻)都将继承阈值问题。
  7. 初代问题。定义围绕成熟邪教所展现之特征建立。一个新生组织或仅以雏形展现这些特征,而它何时跨越阈值,本身处于未定状态。Bateman 组织在他公开自封先知之前是邪教吗?何时开始?
  8. 文本权威边缘案例。某些组织将权威集中于已故创始人之文本而非在世之人,但功能上与邪教等同。定义之第(二)条严格排除此类;这是否为正确判断?抑或定义应推广为"集中、不受问责的权威,无论是文本性的还是个人性的"?若推广,定义变宽,有捕捉更多合法宗教传统之风险。
  9. 世俗邪教问题。某些组织满足四条,却不作宗教或形而上学宣称(某些治疗共同体、某些政治极权小组、某些公司邪教)。在此类案例中,出口成本是世俗的而非形而上学的。定义是否应扩展,以接纳世俗形式的出口成本(自我之失、意义之失、社会消亡)作为形而上学损失的功能等价物?此扩展可被论证,但削弱第(三)条的特异性。
  10. 验证问题。判断一个共同体是否满足四条,需来自内部之证言,而邪教结构恰使内部证言不可靠。在职成员将低报特征(因共同体词汇将其重述);离开者将高报特征(因离开后之再诠释)。定义原则上可检验,但证据在结构上受损。
III. Chapter Three 第 三 章

The Doctrinal Substrate 教义底层

The organisational layer developed in Chapter I describes what a cult is; it does not yet describe why some traditions produce cults more readily than others. The four structural conditions are formal, in the sense that any ideological content can in principle fill them. But empirically, cults do not arise with equal probability from all doctrinal soils. Certain teachings — continuing revelation, end-times eschatology, gnostic dualism, esoteric initiation, mystical theosis, sacralised marriage — are repeatedly the soil in which cults grow. The aim of this chapter is to identify those doctrinal structures, trace specific cults to specific teachings within their host traditions, and address the scholarly avoidance that has, until now, kept this question off the table.

The thesis is uncomfortable, because it implicates not only the rogue prophet but the host tradition: it says that mainline Mormonism bears partial responsibility for the FLDS, that mainstream Mahāyāna esotericism bears partial responsibility for Aum Shinrikyo, that Pentecostal end-times schema bears partial responsibility for Peoples Temple. These are claims that no serious scholar of religion wants to make in print, because each one offends a constituency. They are stated here directly. The claim is in each case partial, not total — Joseph Smith did not foresee Samuel Bateman, but he established the doctrinal machinery that made Samuel Bateman a legible figure within his tradition. The cult emerges where the doctrinal door has been left open; the host tradition is responsible, in part, for having installed the door.

第一章所开展之组织层描述邪教是什么;它尚未描述为何某些传统比另一些更易产出邪教。四个结构性条件是形式的——任何意识形态内容原则上皆可填充其中。但经验上,邪教并不以同等概率从所有教义土壤中生长。某些教义——持续启示论、末世论、灵知二元论、密法授受、神秘合一与神化、神圣化婚姻——反复地成为邪教生长之土壤。本章之意图在于识别这些教义结构,将具体邪教溯源至其母传统中具体之教导,并面对学界至今对该问题之回避。

此命题不舒服,因为它牵连的不仅是流氓先知,亦是母传统:它说主流摩门教对 FLDS 负有部分责任;主流大乘密宗对奥姆真理教负有部分责任;五旬节末世论对人民圣殿教负有部分责任。这些是任何严肃的宗教学者皆不愿在刊物上做出的主张,因为每一项皆冒犯一个群体。在此径直陈述。每一项主张皆为部分而非全部——Joseph Smith 未能预见 Samuel Bateman,但他确立了使 Samuel Bateman 在其传统内成为一个可被理解之人物的教义机制。邪教生长于教义之门被留开之处;母传统对该门之安装负有部分责任。

II · 1 The Symmetry Argument: No Tradition Is Immune 对称性论证:无传统具豁免 +

A Common Rhetorical Trap

一种常见的修辞陷阱

When someone observes that a particular tradition has produced cults or terrorism — say, that Islam has produced ISIS, AQ, and Boko Haram — the standard response in liberal-academic discourse is to point out that other traditions have produced comparable things too, and therefore that the original observation is unfair, racist, or culturally chauvinist. This response is rhetorically effective and logically defective. If it is true that the original observation can only be reinforced by extending the sample (Christianity has produced Münster, Branch Davidians, Peoples Temple, FLDS; Buddhism has produced White Lotus, Ikkō-ikki, Aum; Hinduism has produced RSS violence and Aghori extremism; Sikhism has produced Bhindranwale's movement; secular ideologies have produced Khmer Rouge and the cult around Pol Pot), then the correct response is not to retract the original observation but to extend it: no major religious or ideological tradition is cult-immune.

当有人指出某一特定传统产出过邪教或恐怖主义——比如,说伊斯兰教产出了 ISIS、AQ、博科圣地——自由主义学术话语中之标准回应,是指出其他传统也产出过相当之物,因此原观察是不公平的、种族主义的、或文化沙文主义的。此回应修辞上有效,逻辑上有缺陷。若扩展样本反而强化了原观察(基督教产出过明斯特、Branch Davidians、人民圣殿、FLDS;佛教产出过白莲教、一向一揆、奥姆;印度教产出过 RSS 暴力与 Aghori 极端分支;锡克教产出过宾德兰瓦勒运动;世俗意识形态产出过红色高棉与围绕波尔布特的崇拜),则正确的回应不是撤回原观察,而是扩展它:没有任何主要宗教或意识形态传统是邪教-免疫的。

Symmetry Without Equivalence

对称而不等同

The symmetry argument does not say all traditions produce cults at the same rate or for the same reasons. It says: each major tradition has produced cults, and the cults each tradition has produced are traceable to specific doctrinal structures within that tradition. The FLDS is not "the dark side of religion in general"; it is the specific product of Mormon continuing-revelation theology combined with the doctrine of plural celestial marriage. Aum is not "religion gone wrong"; it is the specific product of Mahāyāna esoteric structures (guru-as-vehicle, transgressive antinomianism justified by realisation, mappō / latter-day-Dharma eschatology) combined with a doomsday science-fiction overlay. Each cult requires its own specific genealogy of doctrinal cause. The symmetry is that every tradition has such a genealogy to give.

对称性论证并非声称所有传统以相同速率、出于相同理由产出邪教。它声称:每一主要传统皆产出过邪教,而每一传统所产出之邪教,可追溯至该传统内具体的教义结构。FLDS 不是"宗教普遍之阴暗面";它是摩门教持续启示神学与天体多妻教义结合之具体产物。奥姆不是"宗教走错路";它是大乘密宗结构(上师作为媒介、由证悟所授权的越轨反律法主义、末法时代之末世论)与一种末日科幻外衣结合之具体产物。每一邪教皆需自身具体的教义因果谱系。所对称者,在于每一传统皆有此种谱系可被给出。

A Visual Matrix

视觉矩阵

II · 2 Six Cult-Susceptible Doctrinal Structures 六个邪教易感的教义结构 +

The following six doctrinal structures recur across cult-producing traditions. None of them is, by itself, evidence that a tradition is a cult; many mainline religions hold one or more of them in moderated form. The claim is that where the four organisational conditions of Chapter I are present, these doctrinal structures are the most common content filling those conditions; and that traditions whose mainstream theology contains one or more of these structures in a strong form are the traditions from which cultic offshoots most readily emerge.

以下六个教义结构反复出现于产出邪教的传统之中。其中任何一个本身皆非"该传统是邪教"之证据;许多主流宗教皆以缓和形式持有其中之一或多个。所要说的是:当第一章之四个组织条件存在时,这些教义结构是最常被用以填充该条件的内容;而其主流神学以强形式持有其中之一或多个的传统,即邪教式分支最易从中浮现的传统。

D-a — Continuing Revelation

D-a — 持续启示论

A tradition that licenses an authoritative living person — prophet, imam, master — to receive new revelation and to modify or supersede prior doctrine is structurally undefended against a new prophet appearing and doing exactly that. Mormonism opened this door in 1830 (Joseph Smith); it partially closed the door in 1890 (the Manifesto renouncing plural marriage), but it closed the door using the same mechanism — a new revelation overriding an old one — and therefore left the mechanism itself fully available for any subsequent claimant. Warren Jeffs and Samuel Bateman are not deviations from Mormon doctrine; they are continuations of one of its core mechanisms, applied with the same internal logic by which the 1890 mainstream itself acted. By contrast, Orthodox Judaism closes the door theologically (the age of prophecy has ended); Sunni Islam closes it through the doctrine of the seal of the prophets (khātam an-nabiyyīn); Reformation Protestantism closes it through sola scriptura. These closures are not perfect — schismatic movements have arisen within all three — but the doctrinal door is, at least, deliberately bolted.

一个授权某一权威性在世人物——先知、伊玛目、上师——接受新启示并可修订或废止过往教义的传统,在结构上无法防御一位新先知出现并恰恰如此行。摩门教 1830 年开启此门(Joseph Smith);1890 年部分封堵(放弃多妻之《宣言》),但封堵之方式正是利用同一机制——以新启示废止旧启示——因此使该机制本身对任何后续主张者完全可用。Warren Jeffs 与 Samuel Bateman 不是摩门教教义之偏离;他们是其核心机制之一的延续,以 1890 主流自己行动时所运用之同一内部逻辑加以应用。相反,正统犹太教在神学上封堵此门(先知时代已结束);逊尼派伊斯兰教通过"先知之印"(khātam an-nabiyyīn)之教义封堵;改革新教通过sola scriptura 封堵。这些封堵并不完美——三者内部皆出现过分裂运动——但教义之门至少是被有意上锁的。

D-b — End-Times Eschatology

D-b — 末世论

A tradition that locates the present moment as the last moment before historical termination — and that licenses, during this final moment, the suspension of ordinary moral and epistemic rules — is structurally vulnerable to cult formation. The mechanism is simple: when ordinary rules are suspended for emergency reasons, whoever defines the emergency controls what is permitted. Jim Jones operated in Pentecostal eschatology; David Koresh in Seventh-day Adventist eschatology; Aum Shinrikyo in a syncretic mappō / apocalyptic-science-fiction fusion; Heaven's Gate in a UFO-Christian end-times schema; the Mahdist rebellion in Sudan in Islamic eschatology; the Taiping in a Chinese millenarianism overlaid with Protestant tropes. The vulnerability is most acute in traditions whose eschatology is imminent rather than remote, this-worldly rather than other-worldly, and requires human action rather than awaiting divine action. Mainstream Catholicism mitigates the vulnerability by displacing the eschaton to ecclesial time and institutional sacrament; mainstream Theravāda Buddhism by displacing it across kalpas; mainstream Sunni Islam by deferring the Mahdi without clear human role. Where the deferral is removed, the door is opened.

一个将当下时刻定位为历史终结之前的最后时刻——并授权在此最终时刻中悬置普通道德与认识论规则——的传统,在结构上易于邪教形成。其机制简单:当普通规则因紧急理由而被悬置,定义紧急者即控制何为可被允许。Jim Jones 在五旬节末世论中运作;David Koresh 在复临安息日会末世论中运作;奥姆真理教在融合末法与末日科幻的混合中运作;天堂之门在 UFO–基督教末世图式中运作;苏丹的马赫迪起义在伊斯兰末世论中运作;太平天国在叠加新教元素之中国千禧年主义中运作。此种脆弱性在末世论为临近而非遥远、此世而非他世、需要人之行动而非等待神之行动的传统中最为尖锐。主流天主教通过将末世位移至教会时间与制度性圣礼来缓和此脆弱;主流上座部佛教通过将其位移至诸劫之间;主流逊尼派伊斯兰教通过推迟马赫迪且不赋予人类清晰角色。当推迟被移除,门即被打开。

Date-Setting as the Specific Heresy of D-b
设日期化:D-b 之具体异端形式

Mainstream Christianity holds that Christ will return imminently but that the date is not knowable. The position has hard scriptural foundation. Matthew 24:36: "But of that day and hour knoweth no man, no, not the angels of heaven, but my Father only." Acts 1:7, the risen Christ's final words to disciples asking about timing: "It is not for you to know the times or the seasons, which the Father hath put in his own power." 1 Thessalonians 5:1–2 makes the same point to a congregation actively expecting return. Augustine in De Civitate Dei 18:53 attacks date-calculation explicitly, citing Acts 1:7. The patristic heresiological corpus from Irenaeus through Epiphanius treats Montanus's "new prophecy" — which had a specific time-frame — as paradigmatic heresy on this ground.

The rule formalises as: date-setting is itself a heresy, independently of any other doctrinal feature. Any movement announcing a specific year, form, or identifying sign of Christ's return crosses the line by that act alone. This converts D-b from a vague "imminent eschatology" disposition into a sharp diagnostic. Movements that have set dates and qualify as date-setting heresy: William Miller's 1844 ("Great Disappointment", founding event of Adventism); Charles Taze Russell's 1914 (Watchtower Society, parent of Jehovah's Witnesses, with successive failed dates 1925, 1975); Branch Davidians under David Koresh; Heaven's Gate (Hale-Bopp 1997); Family Radio under Harold Camping (21 May 2011, then 21 October 2011); Korean Dami Mission (28 October 1992); the Mahdist movements of 19th-century Sudan; Taiping Tianguo's specific chronology (1851 onward); World Mission Society Church of God's various calculations.

By this criterion, Adventism's lineage — Miller → Seventh-day Adventists → various splinters (Branch Davidians, the Worldwide Church of God under Armstrong, Christadelphians via Thomas) — carries the date-setting gene as a structural inheritance, even where descendant denominations have publicly retreated from specific dates. Catholicism, Orthodoxy, mainstream Sunni and Shia Islam, mainstream Mahāyāna and Theravāda Buddhism all maintain the eschatological deferral and thereby close this door. Pentecostalism varies: most denominations refuse explicit dating but operationalise imminence in ways that can shade into the heresy under high-charisma leadership.

主流基督教持守:基督将迫近再临,但日期不可知。此立场有硬经文基础。《马太福音》24:36:"但那日子,那时辰,没有人知道,连天上的使者也不知道,子也不知道,惟独父知道。"《使徒行传》1:7,复活基督对询问时间之门徒之最后话语:"父凭着自己的权柄所定的时候、日期,不是你们可以知道的。"《帖撒罗尼迦前书》5:1-2 对一个正主动期待再临之会众做出同样的强调。奥古斯丁在《上帝之城》18:53 明确攻击日期推算,引《使徒行传》1:7。从 Irenaeus 至 Epiphanius 之教父异端学全集,将 Montanus 之"新预言"(具体时间表)视为此基础上之典范异端。

该规则形式化为:设日期化本身即异端,独立于任何其他教义特征。任何运动宣告基督再临之具体年份、形式、或识别标志,即凭此行为本身跨越界线。这将 D-b 从一个模糊的"迫近末世论" disposition,转化为一种尖锐的诊断。设日期且符合"设日期化异端"之运动:William Miller 之 1844 年("大失望",复临运动之奠基事件);Charles Taze Russell 之 1914 年(守望塔社,即耶和华见证人之母会,后续失败日期 1925、1975);David Koresh 之 Branch Davidians;天堂之门(海尔-波普彗星 1997);Harold Camping 之家庭电台(2011 年 5 月 21 日、后改 10 月 21 日);韩国 Dami Mission(1992 年 10 月 28 日);十九世纪苏丹之马赫迪运动;太平天国之具体年历(1851 起);世界传道会上帝教会之各种推算。

按此标准,复临运动谱系——Miller → 七日复临会 → 各分裂派(Branch Davidians、Armstrong 之世界基督教会、Thomas 经创立之 Christadelphians)——作为结构性继承携带"设日期"基因,即便其后裔宗派公开后退离具体日期。天主教、东正教、主流逊尼派与什叶派伊斯兰、主流大乘与上座部佛教,皆维持末世推迟之立场,因而封堵此门。五旬节派变异较大:多数宗派拒绝明确日期,但以可在高魅力型领袖之下滑入异端之方式操作化迫近性。

D-c — Gnostic Dualism

D-c — 灵知二元论

A tradition that builds its soteriology on a sharp polarisation of two realms — the material/fallen and the spiritual/saved — and that locates salvation in esoteric knowledge (gnosis) accessible only through the tradition's special channels, produces an internal logic by which members are "those who know" and outsiders are "those still asleep." The structure goes back to ancient Gnostic Christianity (Valentinians, Sethians) and Manichaeism; it surfaces in Christian Cathar dualism, in some Sufi bāṭinī ("inner") schools, in Russian Orthodoxy's heterodox sectarian fringe (Khlysty, Skoptsy), and — most importantly for modern cult studies — in the secular-spiritual hybrids of the twentieth century. Scientology's thetan-versus-MEST cosmology is overtly Gnostic in structure; NXIVM's distinction between "integrated" persons and ordinary humans is a Gnosticism without metaphysics; the New Age movement's "ascended masters" and "5D consciousness" frameworks repeat the same form. The doctrinal door is the proposition that ordinary epistemic access is insufficient and only the tradition's inner pathway suffices. Where this proposition is held strongly, the tradition is structurally pre-loaded with epistemic closure (Chapter I, condition 1).

一个将其救赎论建立于两个领域之尖锐对立——物质/堕落与灵性/被拯救——并将救赎定位于秘传知识(灵知)只能通过该传统之特殊渠道获取的传统,产出一种内部逻辑:成员是"已知者",外人是"仍沉睡者"。此结构可追溯至古代灵知派基督教(瓦伦丁派、塞特派)与摩尼教;它浮现于基督教卡特里二元论、某些苏菲bāṭinī("内在")派、俄罗斯东正教异端宗派边缘(鞭笞派、阉割派)中,以及——对现代邪教研究最重要的——二十世纪世俗-灵性混合体中。山达基的 theta-MEST 宇宙论在结构上明显是灵知派;NXIVM 对"已整合者"与普通人之区分,是去形而上学的灵知主义;新时代运动的"扬升大师"与"五维意识"框架重复同一形式。教义之门在于"普通认识论途径不足,唯传统之内部路径足够"这一命题。当此命题被强力持有,该传统已在结构上预装载认识论闭合(第一章条件 1)。

D-d — Esoteric Initiation

D-d — 密法授受

Closely related to (c), but mechanically distinct. A tradition that reserves its highest teachings for initiated members, transmitted only through direct master-to-disciple lineage and forbidden to publish, structurally produces a tiered membership in which the upper tiers know things the lower tiers do not — and the highest tier (the master, the guru, the chief operator) defines what counts as advancement. Tibetan Buddhist tantra is the most theologically developed instance: the master-disciple relationship (samaya) is sacralised to a degree that obedience to the master is itself a soteriological virtue, and breaking samaya is metaphysically punished. This structure has produced numerous abusive Tibetan-Buddhist groups in the West (Chögyam Trungpa's Shambhala, Sogyal Rinpoche's Rigpa, and others), and at full strength it produced Aum Shinrikyo. Mahāyāna esotericism in East Asia (Shingon, certain strands of Korean and Vietnamese Buddhism) is more institutionally constrained but retains the same doctrinal element. The Western analogues are Theosophy (Madame Blavatsky's "Masters"), Gurdjieff's Fourth Way schools, and the entire family of mystery-tradition revival movements (OTO, modern Rosicrucianism). The doctrinal door is the legitimation of asymmetric information as soteriologically necessary.

与(c)密切相关,但机制上有别。一个将其最高教导保留给已受戒成员、仅通过直接师徒法脉传授、禁止公开出版的传统,在结构上产出分层之成员制,其中上层知道下层所不知之事——而最上层(上师、古鲁、首要操作者)定义何为进阶。藏传佛教密宗是神学上最发展之实例:师徒关系(三昧耶)被神圣化至于"对上师之顺从本身即救赎之美德",而破坏三昧耶则受形而上学之惩罚。此结构在西方产出了诸多施虐性藏传佛教团体(Chögyam Trungpa 的香巴拉、Sogyal Rinpoche 的 Rigpa 等),而以最强形式则产出奥姆真理教。东亚之大乘密宗(真言宗,某些朝鲜与越南佛教支脉)在制度上更受限,但保留同一教义元素。西方对应者为通神学(布拉瓦茨基的"大师")、葛吉夫的第四道学派,以及神秘传统复兴运动整个家族(OTO、现代玫瑰十字会)。教义之门是对"不对称信息作为救赎所必需"的合法化。

D-e — Mystical Theosis / Divine Embodiment

D-e — 神秘合一与神化

A tradition that allows for the possibility that a specific living individual has, in this present life, achieved union with the divine, become an incarnation of the divine, or attained a state above ordinary human conditions, opens a door through which a living person can claim — and have his community accept — that he is to be treated as superhuman. Shōkō Asahara claimed to be the "final liberated one"; Jim Jones declared himself the incarnation of God; Sun Myung Moon claimed to be the True Father completing what Christ began; Bhagwan Shree Rajneesh / Osho positioned himself as an enlightened master whose conduct, by definition, expressed enlightenment. The doctrinal door is the proposition that the gap between the human and the divine can be closed by a living individual. Where the tradition keeps this gap absolute (orthodox Sunni Islam, Reformed Calvinism, certain strands of Orthodox Judaism), the door is closed. Where the tradition allows degrees of divinisation (Mahāyāna's tathāgatagarbha doctrine, Christian mystical theology of theosis, Hindu jīvanmukti, Sufism's fanā), the door is at least theologically reasoned about; but in proportion as the tradition allows the gap to be closed in this life by a specific living person, the door is opened.

一个允许"某一具体在世个体在此生中已达成与神之合一、成为神之化身、或达到超越普通人之状态"之可能性的传统,开启一道门,通过此门,一个在世之人可以宣告——并使其共同体接受——他将被视作超人。麻原彰晃宣称自己为"最终解脱者";Jim Jones 自称神之化身;Sun Myung Moon 宣称自己为完成基督所开启之事的"真父";Bhagwan Shree Rajneesh / Osho 将自己定位为开悟之师,其行为按定义即开悟之表达。教义之门是"人与神之间的鸿沟可被一在世个体所跨越"这一命题。当传统将此鸿沟保持为绝对(正统逊尼派伊斯兰、改革宗加尔文主义、某些正统犹太教支脉),门是关闭的。当传统允许神化之程度(大乘的如来藏教义、基督教神化之神秘神学、印度教解脱者、苏菲之消融),门至少在神学上有过推理;但与此传统允许此鸿沟在此生由某一在世之具体人所跨越的程度成正比,该门是被打开的。

D-f — Sacralised Marriage and Reproduction

D-f — 神圣化的婚姻与生育

A tradition that constructs marriage, sexuality, or reproduction not as a worldly social arrangement but as bearing salvific function — such that the right marital configuration is itself a soteriological act — opens a door to prophet-directed sexual exploitation. Joseph Smith's 1843 revelation (D&C 132) is the canonical case: plural celestial marriage was not merely permitted but soteriologically required for the highest tier of post-mortem exaltation, and a woman who refused her husband's plural marriages was warned she would be "destroyed." From this doctrinal structure, the FLDS practice of child marriage is not a deviation; it is a continuation of one of the doctrine's internal logics. The Unification Church's "Blessing" ceremonies, in which Sun Myung Moon personally arranged marriages with soteriological consequences, operate on the same doctrinal structure. The Children of God / Family International's "flirty fishing" doctrine — that members were spiritually obligated to use sex as a recruitment tool — operates on a related structure. The doctrinal door is the construction of sexual and marital arrangement as having metaphysical rather than merely social weight, with the tradition's authority defining what configuration is salvific.

一个将婚姻、性、或生育不构建为世俗社会安排、而是构建为承载救赎功能——以致正确的婚姻配置本身即一救赎行为——的传统,开启一道通往先知主导之性剥削之门。Joseph Smith 1843 年之启示(教义与圣约 132)即典范:天体多妻不仅被允许,且为死后高阶之"提升"所救赎论上必要,而拒绝丈夫多妻之妻子被警告将"被毁灭"。从此教义结构出发,FLDS 之童婚实践不是偏离;它是该教义内部某条逻辑之延续。统一教之"祝福"仪式——其中 Sun Myung Moon 亲自安排具救赎后果之婚姻——以同一教义结构运作。神之子女/家庭国际的"调情垂钓"教义——成员被精神性地义务以性作为招募工具——以相关结构运作。教义之门是"将性与婚姻安排构建为具形而上学而非仅社会分量,并以传统之权威定义何种配置具救赎性"。

Combinations Are More Dangerous Than Individuals

组合比个别更危险

No single one of these six doctrinal structures suffices to make a tradition cult-producing. Most mainline religions hold one or more of them in some form. What converts doctrinal potential into actual cult production is the combination of two or more, plus the four organisational conditions of Chapter I. The FLDS satisfies D-a + D-e + D-f, plus the full O-set (O1, O2, O3, O4) in strong form. Aum satisfies D-b + D-d + D-e, plus the full O-set. Scientology satisfies D-c + D-d + partial D-e, plus the full O-set. NXIVM satisfies D-c + D-d + D-f, plus the full O-set. Peoples Temple satisfies D-b + D-e, plus the full O-set. The doctrinal substrate analysis is, in this sense, complementary to the organisational analysis: it tells us which doctrinal soils are likely to grow which cults, but the cult only fully emerges when the organisational conditions are also met.

六个教义结构中之任何一个,单独皆不足以使一个传统成为邪教-产出性的。多数主流宗教皆以某种形式持有其中之一或多个。将教义潜能转化为实际邪教产出者,是其中两个或多个之组合,加上第一章之四个组织条件。FLDS 满足 D-a + D-e + D-f,加 O 集全部(O1、O2、O3、O4)以强形式。奥姆满足 D-b + D-d + D-e,加 O 集全部。山达基满足 D-c + D-d + 部分 D-e,加 O 集全部。NXIVM 满足 D-c + D-d + D-f,加 O 集全部。人民圣殿满足 D-b + D-e,加 O 集全部。教义底层分析在此意义上,与组织分析互补:它告诉我们何种教义土壤可能生长何种邪教,但邪教只有在组织条件亦被满足时才完整浮现。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • D. Michael Quinn, The Mormon Hierarchy: Origins of Power (Signature Books, 1994).
  • Jon Krakauer, Under the Banner of Heaven: A Story of Violent Faith (Doubleday, 2003).
  • Ian Reader, Religious Violence in Contemporary Japan: The Case of Aum Shinrikyo (Curzon, 2000).
  • Kurt Rudolph, Gnosis: The Nature and History of Gnosticism (HarperOne, 1987).
  • Hugh B. Urban, Tantra: Sex, Secrecy, Politics, and Power in the Study of Religion (University of California Press, 2003).
  • Norman Cohn, The Pursuit of the Millennium (Oxford University Press, 1957; revised 1970).
II · 3 Case Tracing: From Tradition to Cult 案例溯源:从传统到邪教 +

FLDS as Mormon Continuation

FLDS 作为摩门教之延续

The case for "FLDS is mainstream Mormonism's deviant offshoot, externally produced" is the standard LDS apologetic position; it is held with sincerity by most contemporary Mormons and has the institutional advantage of preserving mainstream LDS's respectability. It is also false in its strong form. Joseph Smith received D&C 132 in 1843; he himself married women already married to other men, married teenage girls (Helen Mar Kimball, 14, in 1843), and instituted plural marriage as a soteriological requirement for the highest tier of post-mortem glory. Brigham Young expanded the practice openly in Utah. The 1890 Manifesto was a political act under federal pressure, not a theological repudiation; even after 1890, plural marriages continued under church authority into the early 1900s, and the official theological justification for plural marriage was never withdrawn: the LDS Church teaches that it remains valid in the celestial realm, only suspended from earthly practice.

Given this, Warren Jeffs's position is theologically coherent: if plural marriage was a divine ordinance, and if the prophetic office can receive revelation overriding earlier revelation, then a new prophet can re-authorise the earthly practice. The FLDS reading is not external to Mormon doctrine; it is one of the readings the doctrine licenses. Mainline LDS responds by claiming exclusive prophetic authority, but it cannot do so on principled grounds — its own founding logic gives every prophet equal claim to revelation. The structural responsibility for the FLDS lies in the doctrinal architecture Joseph Smith built; the proximate responsibility lies with Jeffs and Bateman. The two are not in competition.

"FLDS 是主流摩门教的偏离分支,外在产生"——这是标准的 LDS 护教立场;大多数当代摩门教徒真诚地持有此立场,且它有保留主流 LDS 体面之制度便利。其强形式亦是错的。Joseph Smith 于 1843 年接受 教义与圣约 132;他本人娶了已婚于他人之女子、娶了少女(Helen Mar Kimball,1843,14 岁),且将多妻确立为死后最高荣耀阶层的救赎要求。Brigham Young 在犹他公开扩展此实践。1890 年《宣言》是在联邦压力下的政治行为,非神学撤销;即便 1890 年后,多妻在教会权威下继续延续至 1900 年代初,而对多妻之官方神学辩护从未被撤回:LDS 教会教导多妻在天界仍有效,只是从尘世实践中被暂停。

鉴于此,Warren Jeffs 的立场在神学上一致:若多妻是神圣法令,且先知职位可接受废止较早启示之启示,则新先知可重新授权尘世实践。FLDS 之读法不外在于摩门教教义;它是该教义所授权的读法之一。主流 LDS 通过宣称排他性先知权威加以回应,但它在原则上无法如此——其自身奠基性逻辑赋予每位先知对启示之同等主张。FLDS 之结构性责任在于 Joseph Smith 所建造之教义架构;近端责任在于 Jeffs 与 Bateman。二者并不竞争。

Aum Shinrikyo as Mahāyāna Esoteric Extension

奥姆真理教作为大乘密宗之延伸

The standard reading of Aum — particularly in Western Buddhist circles — is that Asahara's organisation distorted Buddhist teachings beyond recognition. This is comforting and partially true. It is also strategically incomplete. The four-condition definition is filled in Aum by specifically Mahāyāna esoteric materials, not by random ideological filler. The guru-as-vehicle structure that Aum exploited is canonical in Tibetan tantra (samaya obedience to the root lama is taught as a soteriological precondition for tantric practice). The doctrine of transgressive antinomianism authorised by realisation — the idea that a sufficiently realised practitioner can perform acts that would be ethically wrong for an unrealised practitioner, because the realised practitioner acts from emptiness rather than from delusion — is canonical (it is the structure of the trülshik and siddha traditions; it is what makes Padmasambhava's biography possible; it appears in Vajrayāna texts that any educated Tibetan practitioner has encountered). The mappō / latter-day Dharma framework — the doctrine that we live in a degenerate era in which ordinary religious practice is insufficient and extraordinary measures are required — is canonical Mahāyāna East Asian Buddhism.

Asahara did not invent any of these doctrinal elements. He combined them, weighted them in a particular way, added an apocalyptic-science-fiction overlay, and applied them to his community with the four organisational conditions in place. Each of the elements he used can be found in living, mainstream forms of Mahāyāna esoteric practice today. Robert Jay Lifton, in Destroying the World to Save It, comes very close to making this point — he writes about Asahara's "guru bond" and about how Aum tapped into authentic Vajrayāna structures — but he stops short of saying that mainstream Vajrayāna therefore shares partial responsibility for what Aum became. That step is taken here.

对奥姆之标准读法——尤其在西方佛教圈——是麻原之组织扭曲佛教教导至不可辨认。此说舒适且部分为真。它亦在策略上不完整。奥姆中之四条件被具体的大乘密宗材料填充,非由随机意识形态填充物。奥姆所利用之上师-作为媒介结构,在藏传密宗中是经典(对根本喇嘛之三昧耶顺从被教导为密法修行之救赎前提)。"由证悟所授权之越轨反律法主义"之教义——即一位充分证悟之修行者可行使对未证悟者而言道德上错误之行为,因证悟者由空性行事而非由迷妄行事——是经典(它是瑜伽士与成就者传统之结构;它使莲花生大士之传记成为可能;它出现在任何受过教育之藏传修行者所遭遇之金刚乘文本中)。末法框架——我们生活于一退化之时代,普通宗教修行不足,需非常手段——是经典之东亚大乘佛教。

麻原未发明这些教义元素中之任何一个。他将它们组合、以特定方式赋权、加上一末日科幻外衣,并在四组织条件就位之情境下应用于其共同体。他所使用之每一元素,皆可在今日活生生的、主流的大乘密宗实践中被发现。Robert Jay Lifton 在《摧毁世界以救赎之》中非常接近做出此点——他写到麻原之"上师关系"以及奥姆如何接入真实的金刚乘结构——但他止步于不去说"主流金刚乘因而对奥姆所成之物负有部分责任"。此处迈出该步。

Scientology and NXIVM as Modern Gnostic Revivals

山达基与 NXIVM 作为现代灵知派复兴

Scientology and NXIVM are both, despite their public self-presentation as scientific or rational, structurally Gnostic systems. Scientology's thetan-versus-MEST cosmology recapitulates the central Gnostic move: the true self (the thetan) is trapped in matter (MEST = Matter, Energy, Space, Time); salvation consists in liberation through esoteric knowledge progressively revealed only to initiated members; the highest knowledge (the OT levels, including the Xenu material) is kept secret and is metaphysically dangerous to those not prepared. NXIVM's structure is a Gnosticism without metaphysical theology: "rational inquiry method" replaces gnosis; "integration" replaces salvation; the master-disciple lineage of "stripes" and master-slave bonds replaces initiation. In both cases, the doctrinal substrate is the Gnostic combination of (c) and (d): esoteric knowledge as soteriologically necessary, transmitted in tiers. These structures are not invented by Hubbard or Raniere; they are reactivations, in twentieth-century vocabulary, of a religious form with a 1,800-year history.

山达基与 NXIVM,尽管对公众自我呈现为科学的或理性的,在结构上皆是灵知派系统。山达基的 theta-MEST 宇宙论重演了灵知派之核心移动:真我(theta)被困于物质(MEST = 物质、能量、空间、时间);救赎在于通过仅渐进地向已受戒成员揭示之秘传知识所达成之解脱;最高知识(OT 等级,包括 Xenu 材料)被保密,且对未准备者形而上学地危险。NXIVM 之结构是无形而上学神学的灵知派:"理性探究方法"取代灵知;"整合"取代救赎;"条纹"之师徒法脉与主奴关系取代受戒。两者中,教义底层皆是(c)与(d)之灵知派组合:秘传知识作为救赎所必需,以等级传递。这些结构非由 Hubbard 或 Raniere 所发明;它们是在二十世纪词汇中,对一种具 1800 年历史的宗教形式之再激活。

Peoples Temple as Pentecostal End-Times Realisation

人民圣殿教作为五旬节末世论之实现

Jim Jones started in mainstream Pentecostalism. His move toward divinisation, the construction of an external enemy (American capitalism / fascism), and the eventual ritualised "revolutionary suicide" did not require him to leave Pentecostal eschatology; they required him to operationalise it. The Pentecostal schema — that we live in the last days, that the world is fundamentally fallen, that the faithful constitute a remnant community in tension with a hostile world, that martyrdom for the faith is salvific — gave Jones the doctrinal scaffolding within which his organisational extremes became internally legible. His syncretic blending with socialist political vocabulary did not break Pentecostal eschatology; it gave it a contemporary political object (capitalist America as the world from which the faithful must separate). The Jonestown end-state was, from inside the operationalised Pentecostal frame, a coherent act. From outside the frame, it was unintelligible. The doctrinal door that opened it was the Pentecostal emphasis on the imminent end and the salvific value of separation from the fallen world.

Jim Jones 起于主流五旬节派。他朝向神化、对外部敌人(美国资本主义/法西斯主义)之建构、以及最终仪式化之"革命性自杀",并未要求他离开五旬节末世论;它们要求他将其操作化。五旬节图式——我们生活于末日、世界根本上是堕落的、信徒构成与敌对世界处于张力中之余民共同体、为信仰殉道具救赎价值——给予 Jones 一教义脚手架,在其内其组织极端化在内部成为可理解。他与社会主义政治词汇之混合,不打破五旬节末世论;它给予后者一个当代政治对象(资本主义美国作为信徒必须分离之世界)。琼斯敦之终态,在被操作化之五旬节框架内部,是一融贯之行为。在该框架外部,它是不可理解的。开启此门的教义,是五旬节派对临近终结与"自堕落世界分离"之救赎价值之强调。

II · 4 The Threefold Scholarly Avoidance 学界的三重回避 +

First Avoidance: The NRM School Withdraws the Word

第一重回避:NRM 学派撤回该词

The first avoidance has already been identified in the Preface and is developed at length in Chapter VIII. The New Religious Movements school, since the 1980s, has substituted the term cult with terms whose neutrality is purchased precisely by their inability to mark the structural distinction. The withdrawal of the word effects a hermeneutic injustice on those harmed by what the word names. This is the avoidance that contemporary anti-cult scholars (Singer, Hassan, Lalich) have correctly identified and resisted.

第一重回避已在前言中识别,并在第八章中详细开展。新兴宗教运动学派自 1980 年代起,以中立性恰恰由"无法标记结构性区分"之能力购得之术语,取代邪教一词。该词之撤销对被其所名命之物所伤害者构成诠释学不正义。此乃当代反邪教学者(Singer、Hassan、Lalich)所正确识别并抵制之回避。

Second Avoidance: The Clinical School Contracts the Causal Chain

第二重回避:临床学派收缩因果链

The second avoidance has not, so far, been identified by name. It is the avoidance practiced by the very scholars who resist the first. Lifton, Singer, Hassan, and Lalich retain the term cult — and this is essential and right — but they locate the causal source of cultic harm in the cult leader and the organisational machinery of thought reform, and they methodologically prescind from the question of doctrinal content. On their view, what Jeffs did to FLDS members is the kind of thing a charismatic authoritarian leader does to dependents within a high-control group; the specifically Mormon doctrinal substrate (continuing revelation plus celestial marriage plus 1843 D&C 132) is treated as the interchangeable filler within which the universal pattern played out.

This contraction of the causal chain has at least three motivations, in order of decreasing innocence. First, it is clinically useful: a survivor of FLDS abuse can be treated for the trauma without the therapist being required to take a position on Mormon theology, which preserves the therapist's professional neutrality and avoids alienating clients who wish to retain religious identities. Second, it is academically safer: a clinical psychologist who treats Mormon-affiliated patients cannot afford to be seen indicting Mormon theology, since to do so would mean losing referrals and the cooperation of mainstream Mormon institutions in research. Third, it preserves a more general institutional comfort: the implicit suggestion that mainstream religion is fundamentally healthy and only "high-control offshoots" are sick, which is congenial to a broad American liberal-religious establishment.

The cost of this contraction is borne by survivors. A young woman who leaves the FLDS but retains belief in "the restored gospel" — i.e., in the Joseph Smith founding revelations including D&C 132 — is not, on the clinical school's framing, in conceptual error. She has merely left a deviant offshoot and returned to legitimate religion. But on the doctrinal-substrate view, she has left only the operational extension; the doctrinal door through which her abuse became theologically authorised remains open in the tradition she continues to inhabit. She needs structural vocabulary that lets her name not only what Jeffs did but what the doctrinal architecture allowed Jeffs to do. The clinical school's contraction of the causal chain denies her this vocabulary. It is a second hermeneutic injustice, parallel in form to the NRM school's first, although less visible because committed by scholars who think of themselves as the survivors' allies.

第二重回避至今未被点名识别。它是抵抗第一重回避的同一批学者所行之回避。Lifton、Singer、Hassan、Lalich 保留邪教一词——此乃必要且正确——但他们将邪教伤害之因果源头定位于邪教首要分子与思想改造的组织机制,并在方法论上悬置教义内容之问题。在他们看来,Jeffs 对 FLDS 成员所为之事,是一位魅力型独裁领袖对一高控制群体内依附者所做之事的一种;具体之摩门教教义底层(持续启示加天体婚姻加 1843 年 教义与圣约 132)被视作普遍模式在其中上演之可互换填充物。

此种因果链之收缩至少有三项动机,以纯真度递减之序:其一,临床上有用:一位 FLDS 虐待之幸存者可以在不要求治疗师对摩门教神学持立场之情况下被治疗创伤,这保留治疗师之专业中立性,并避免疏远那些希望保留宗教身份之来访者。其二,学术上更安全:一位治疗与摩门教相关之患者的临床心理学家,负担不起被看作指控摩门教神学,因为如此将意味着失去转介与主流摩门教机构在研究上之合作。其三,它保留一种更普遍的制度舒适:即"主流宗教在根本上是健康的、唯有'高控制分支'是病态的"之隐含暗示,而这与广泛的美国自由派宗教建制相投合。

此收缩之代价由幸存者承担。一位离开 FLDS 但保留对"恢复福音"——即对 Joseph Smith 包括 教义与圣约 132 在内之奠基性启示——之信仰的年轻女性,在临床学派之框架下,并非处于概念错误。她仅仅离开了一个偏离分支并回归合法宗教。但在教义底层视角下,她只离开了操作性延伸;使她之被虐待获神学授权之教义之门,仍在她继续居住之传统中敞开。她需要结构性词汇,使她得以命名的不仅是 Jeffs 所做之事,亦是教义架构所授权 Jeffs 所为之事。临床学派对因果链之收缩否认她此种词汇。这是第二重诠释学不正义,在形式上平行于 NRM 学派之第一重,虽然由于其行为者将自己视为幸存者之盟友而较不显眼。

Third Avoidance: Mainstream Religious Studies Outsources the Problem

第三重回避:主流宗教学外包问题

The third avoidance is institutional and structural. Mainstream religious studies departments do not, as a rule, treat cult production as an internal problem within the study of major traditions. The question "what doctrinal features of Tradition X make it cult-susceptible?" is not a standard research question within Mormon studies, Buddhist studies, Islamic studies, or Christian theology. It is outsourced to a separate subfield — "new religious movements" or "cultic studies" — which is in turn dominated by either the NRM-school avoidance (Barker et al.) or the clinical-school contraction (Singer et al.). The result is that no scholarly community has the question on its standard agenda: which features of mainstream traditions, including the one I study, are doctrinally pre-loaded for cultic offshoots?

This third avoidance is the most consequential of the three, because it ensures that the question is asked nowhere in the academy. It is not asked in cult studies (which has contracted the causal chain). It is not asked in religious studies proper (which has outsourced the question). It is not asked in theology (which is institutionally committed to the legitimacy of the traditions it studies). The question therefore survives only in three places: in journalism (Krakauer, Lawrence Wright, Janet Reitman, Sarah Hammel), in survivor memoir (Carolyn Jessop, Rebecca Musser, Sarah Edmondson, Jenna Miscavige Hill), and in occasional public-intellectual essays. It is brought back to something approaching scholarly form here, because the institutional locations that should host the question have, severally and jointly, declined to.

第三重回避是制度性与结构性的。主流宗教学系,作为规则,不将邪教产出作为主要传统研究内部之问题加以处理。"传统 X 的何种教义特征使其邪教易感?"这一问题,在摩门教研究、佛教研究、伊斯兰教研究、或基督教神学中,非标准研究问题。它被外包至一个分立子领域——"新兴宗教运动"或"邪教研究"——而该子领域反过来被 NRM 学派之回避(Barker 等)或临床学派之收缩(Singer 等)所主导。其结果是,没有一个学术共同体将此问题置于其标准议程上:我所研究之传统(包括其主流形式)的哪些特征,在教义上预装载为邪教式分支?

此第三重回避是三重中最严重者,因为它确保该问题在学界无处被提出。它不在邪教研究中被提出(后者已收缩因果链)。它不在严格意义之宗教学中被提出(后者已外包该问题)。它不在神学中被提出(后者在制度上承诺其所研究之传统之合法性)。故该问题只存活于三处:新闻业(Krakauer、Lawrence Wright、Janet Reitman、Sarah Hammel)、幸存者回忆录(Carolyn Jessop、Rebecca Musser、Sarah Edmondson、Jenna Miscavige Hill)、与偶发之公共知识分子文章。在此处以接近学术之形式将其带回,因为本应承载此问题之制度位置,分别与共同地,皆拒绝之。

II · 5 Han Yu and the Non-Western Tradition of Anti-Cult Critique 韩愈与非西方反邪教批判传统 +

A Predecessor the English Literature Has Forgotten

英文文献已遗忘之先驱

In 819 CE, the Tang dynasty official Han Yu (韓愈, 768–824) submitted to Emperor Xianzong a memorial protesting the imperial procession of a Buddha bone relic into the capital — the Lùn Fógǔ Biǎo (論佛骨表, "Memorial on the Buddha-Bone"). The memorial protested not only the specific procession but the broader phenomenon of mass enthusiasm it had provoked: ordinary people, Han Yu reported, were burning the tops of their heads, severing fingers, donating their entire fortunes, and abandoning their families in pursuit of merit from the relic. Han Yu's diagnosis was structural: the behaviour was pathological at a mass scale; the immediate cause was not the individuals' personal failings but the doctrinal framework of Buddhism, which authorised such acts as soteriologically meaningful; and the emperor's imperial procession of the relic legitimated the populace's extremes by giving them imperial sanction.

The memorial cost Han Yu his career — he was banished to Chaozhou — but his position is recognisably the same position taken here, eleven centuries earlier. He refused the comfortable dichotomy: "Buddhism is fine, only a few extremists go too far." He insisted instead on the link between the doctrinal structure and the mass phenomenon it produced. He insisted that imperial / institutional legitimation of the underlying doctrine bore part of the responsibility for the operational extremes. This is, in its structural form, exactly the move the contemporary academy has refused: trace the cultic phenomenon back to the doctrinal substrate, and refuse to let mainstream sanction insulate itself from operational consequence.
