Initiation 受戒 Empowerment (abhiṣeka) by qualified lineage-holder; gradual through study and meditation 由具格法脉持有者授予灌顶(abhiṣeka);经研习与禅修渐进 "Initiation" via electric-shock helmets, hallucinogens (LSD), and drinking Asahara's blood / bathwater for sale 通过电击头盔、致幻剂(LSD)、并出售麻原之血/洗澡水以供饮用之"受戒"
Heresy Status
异端判定

Buddhism does not have a formal heresiological apparatus comparable to the Christian conciliar tradition; the technical question "is Aum a Buddhist heresy" therefore requires translation. Within the Tibetan Vajrayāna and Mahāyāna Buddhist frame, three forms of doctrinal pathology are recognised: wrong view (mithyādṛṣṭi, 邪見), broken samaya (violation of tantric vows), and parasitic teaching (presenting non-Buddhist content under a Buddhist label). Aum is all three. Its Shiva-Asahara identification is not Buddhist; its poa doctrine licensing murder is broken samaya at the strongest possible degree; and its apocalyptic-science-fiction framing is parasitic on Vajrayāna vocabulary without Vajrayāna substance. By the criteria used inside the Buddhist tradition, Aum is unambiguously outside Buddhism.

佛教没有与基督教大公会议传统相当之正式异端学装置;故"奥姆是否佛教异端"之技术性问题需翻译。在藏传金刚乘与大乘佛教框架内,三种教义病理被识别:邪见(mithyādṛṣṭi,梵语)、破三昧耶(违反密戒)、与寄生性教导(以佛教之名呈现非佛教内容)。奥姆三者皆是。其湿婆-麻原之等同非佛教;其授权杀戮之颇瓦教义,是破三昧耶之最强可能程度;其末日科幻框架,是寄生于金刚乘词汇而无金刚乘实质。按佛教传统内部所使用之标准,奥姆毫无歧义地处于佛教之外。

Mainstream Position
主流定位

After the March 1995 Tokyo subway sarin attack, the Japan Buddhist Federation (全日本仏教会) issued statements distancing all Japanese Buddhist denominations from Aum and Asahara. The 14th Dalai Lama's office, embarrassed by the 1987 Dharamsala photograph, issued repeated clarifications that the meeting was a brief reception with no transmission of teachings or empowerments; Dalai Lama personally expressed regret. Mainstream Tibetan Buddhist authorities (the Karmapas, the Sakya Trizin, and others) have consistently treated Aum as a complete fabrication using Buddhist vocabulary, without Buddhist substance. Japanese state authorities classified Aum as a designated organisation under the Anti-Subversive Activities Law in 1995; its assets were liquidated; surviving members regrouped into Aleph (アレフ) and Hikari no Wa (ひかりの輪), which remain under government surveillance. The mainstream Buddhist response is, in this case, uncharacteristically unified and unambiguous: Aum was not us. The doctrinal-substrate analysis here does not contest this judgement, but argues that the specific doctrinal materials Asahara used (guru-yoga structure, antinomian licence via realisation, mappō framework) are genuinely Buddhist, and that the cleanness of the post-1995 disavowal should not obscure the lineage of Aum's doctrinal vocabulary.

1995 年 3 月东京地铁沙林事件后,全日本仏教会发表声明,使所有日本佛教宗派与奥姆和麻原划清界限。第十四世达赖喇嘛办公室因 1987 年达兰萨拉之合影而尴尬,反复澄清该会面只是简短接待,无任何教法传授或灌顶;达赖喇嘛本人表示遗憾。主流藏传佛教权威(各噶玛巴、萨迦法王等)一贯将奥姆视为完全使用佛教词汇而无佛教实质之伪造。日本国家当局 1995 年依《反破坏活动法》将奥姆列为指定团体;其资产被清算;存活成员重组为 Aleph(アレフ)与"光之轮"(ひかりの輪),至今仍受政府监视。本案中之主流佛教回应反常地统一且毫无歧义:奥姆不是我们。此处之教义底层分析不挑战此判断,但主张麻原所使用之具体教义材料(上师瑜伽结构、由证悟所授权之反律法主义、末法框架)确实属于佛教,而 1995 年后切割之干净,不应遮蔽奥姆教义词汇之法脉。

The Doctrinal Synthesis

教义合成

Shoko Asahara (born Chizuo Matsumoto) founded Aum Shinrikyo in 1984 as a yoga and meditation circle, registering it as a religious corporation in 1989. Its doctrinal synthesis was distinctive: Tibetan Buddhist tantra reinterpreted through a personal vision of Asahara as a final-age bodhisattva, fused with Hindu Shaivite imagery, Christian apocalyptic, and elements taken from the science fiction of Isaac Asimov and the novels of Philip K. Dick. The synthesis was not the work of doctrinal scholarship but of a charismatic figure constructing a comprehensive vocabulary in which all of human experience could be re-described as moves in a cosmic drama in which Aum, and Asahara, played the decisive role.

麻原彰晃(本名松本智津夫)1984 年创立奥姆真理教,初为瑜伽与冥想团体,1989 年作为宗教法人注册。其教义合成独具一格:对藏传佛教密宗之重新诠释,经麻原个人愿景——将其自身视为末法时代之菩萨——所过滤;与印度教湿婆派意象、基督教末世论、以及取自阿西莫夫科幻与菲利普·迪克小说之元素相融合。此合成非教义学术之产物,而是一位魅力型人物所建构的全覆盖性词汇,其中人类经验之全部皆可被重述为一出宇宙大剧中的着子,奥姆与麻原在其中扮演决定性角色。

The Escalation

升级

From 1989 onward, Aum killed perceived enemies inside and outside the organisation: a defecting member, a lawyer who represented members' families (and his wife and infant son), and members who failed to comply with internal discipline. By the early 1990s the leadership had acquired a substantial technical apparatus, including the production of sarin nerve agent at a compound near Mount Fuji. On 20 March 1995, five members released sarin on multiple lines of the Tokyo subway system during morning rush hour, killing 14 and injuring over a thousand. Asahara was arrested two months later, tried, convicted, and executed in 2018, alongside twelve other senior members.

1989 年起,奥姆杀害组织内外被视为敌人者:一名叛教成员;一位代表成员家属的律师(及其妻与婴儿之子);以及未能遵守内部纪律之成员。1990 年代初,领导层已获取相当之技术装备,包括在富士山附近一处院落内生产沙林毒气。1995 年 3 月 20 日清晨高峰,五名成员在东京地铁多条线路释放沙林,致 14 人死亡、千余人受伤。麻原两月后被捕,经审判定罪,2018 年与其他十二名高级成员一同被处决。

Doctrinal Anatomy

教义解剖

Asahara invented none of the doctrinal elements his organisation ran on. He combined them, weighted them in a particular way, and added a doomsday science-fiction overlay. Each underlying element is canonical to mainstream Mahāyāna esoteric practice. The guru-as-vehicle structure: Tibetan tantra explicitly teaches obedience to the root lama (samaya) as a soteriological precondition for tantric practice; breaking samaya is metaphysically punished. Transgressive antinomianism authorised by realisation: the doctrine that a sufficiently realised practitioner can perform acts that would be unethical for an unrealised practitioner — because the realised one acts from emptiness rather than delusion — appears in the canonical biographies of Padmasambhava and the trülshik and siddha lineages, and is in living circulation in any educated Vajrayāna context today. Mappō / latter-day Dharma: the doctrine that the present is a degenerate era in which ordinary religious practice is insufficient and extraordinary measures are required, is canonical East Asian Mahāyāna.

Asahara's distinctive contribution was the apocalyptic-science-fiction overlay (drawn from Asimov, from Philip K. Dick, from 1980s Japanese millenarian fiction) and the willingness to operationalise the antinomian licence at industrial scale, with sarin synthesis. The doctrinal substrate that authorised the operationalisation — guru-vehicle, antinomian licence, mappō — was Mahāyāna esoteric mainstream. Lifton, in Destroying the World to Save It, comes close to this point. He writes about Asahara's "guru bond" and about Aum's tap into authentic Vajrayāna structures. He stops short of saying that mainstream Vajrayāna therefore shares partial responsibility. That step is taken here.

麻原所使用之教义元素,他未发明一个。他将它们组合、以特定方式赋权、并加上一末日科幻外衣。每一底层元素皆是主流大乘密宗实践之经典。上师作为媒介之结构:藏传密宗明确教导对根本喇嘛之顺从(三昧耶)为密法修行之救赎前提;破坏三昧耶则受形而上学之惩罚。由证悟所授权之越轨反律法主义:即"充分证悟之修行者可行使对未证悟者而言不道德之行为——因证悟者由空性而非迷妄行事"之教义,出现于莲花生大士之经典传记与瑜伽士、成就者法脉中,且在今日任何受教育之金刚乘语境中皆活生生地流通。末法/末世:即"当下乃退化之时代,普通宗教修行不足,需非常手段"之教义,是经典之东亚大乘佛教。

麻原之独到贡献,是末日科幻外衣(取自阿西莫夫、菲利普·迪克与 1980 年代日本千禧年小说)与"将反律法主义之许可以工业规模操作化"之意愿——以沙林之合成。授权该操作化的教义底层——上师-媒介、反律法主义之许可、末法——是大乘密宗主流。Lifton 在《摧毁世界以救赎之》中接近此点。他写到麻原之"上师关系",以及奥姆如何接入真实金刚乘结构。他止步于不去说"主流金刚乘因而对此负有部分责任"。此步在此处迈出。

Why Aum Matters for the Four-Condition Definition

奥姆对四条件定义之意义

Aum is the central case for two purposes. First, it demonstrates the integration of cultic structure with high technical capability. The members who synthesised sarin were chemistry PhDs; the doctrinal frame had not eliminated their technical rationality, only re-targeted it. This rebuts the comfortable assumption that cult members are necessarily uneducated or unsophisticated. Second, Aum shows the four conditions operating at the limit of (3): exit-cost was not only metaphysical but physical, with murder of those who attempted to leave. The combination of metaphysical and physical exit-enforcement is the strongest possible realisation of the third condition. Aum is also the case Robert Jay Lifton chose to anchor his second major book on cults (Destroying the World to Save It, 1999), the work in which he made the strongest claims for the necessary continuity of his thought-reform framework into the analysis of religious cults.

奥姆对四条件定义有两重意义。其一,它展示邪教结构与高技术能力之整合。合成沙林之成员是化学博士;教义框架并未消除其技术理性,只是将其重新瞄准。这反驳了"邪教成员必然未受教育或不复杂"之舒适假设。其二,奥姆显示四条件在(三)之极限运作:出口成本不仅是形而上学的,也是物理的,试图离开者遭到谋杀。形而上学与物理出口强制之结合,是第三条件最强可能之实现。奥姆亦是 Robert Jay Lifton 选择作为其第二部邪教主要著作之锚点的案例(《摧毁世界以救赎之》,1999),在该书中他作出了其思想改造框架向宗教邪教分析连续延伸的最强主张。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • Robert Jay Lifton, Destroying the World to Save It: Aum Shinrikyo, Apocalyptic Violence, and the New Global Terrorism (Metropolitan Books, 1999).
  • Haruki Murakami, Underground: The Tokyo Gas Attack and the Japanese Psyche (Vintage, 2001; English trans. Alfred Birnbaum & Philip Gabriel).
  • Ian Reader, Religious Violence in Contemporary Japan: The Case of Aum Shinrikyo (University of Hawaii Press, 2000).
IV · 4 Scientology 山达基 +
Lineage 谱系
Parentage
母系

Scientology is not built on a personal God or on revealed scripture, and therefore does not belong to the family of religions in the strict sense that this page reserves for traditions grounded in belief in God. Its 1953 designation as a "religion" was a deliberate legal and tax move by Hubbard, formalised in a memorandum (the "Religion Angle" letter) that has subsequently surfaced in litigation. The proper lineage is a 20th-century American hybrid of new-spirituality traditions and popular-science self-help, with no theological core. Five tributaries: (1) Theosophy (Blavatsky 1875, with its "Masters" hierarchy, multiple subtle bodies, and ascending levels of spiritual development); (2) New Thought (Quimby, Eddy, late 19th-century — mind as the determinant of matter, illness as a mental defect to be corrected); (3) Freudian and post-Freudian depth psychology (the unconscious as repository of traumatic engrams to be uncovered and discharged — Hubbard's "engram" is a direct repurposing of Freudian Verdrängung); (4) Aleister Crowley's ceremonial magic (Hubbard participated in the 1946 Babalon Working rituals at Jack Parsons's Pasadena house, documented in Parsons's diaries and in subsequent biographies); (5) Golden-Age pulp science fiction (Hubbard was a prolific pulp author through the 1930s and 1940s; the Xenu cosmology of OT III is, in genre terms, a 1940s-style space opera). Dianetics (1950) was marketed as a science of the mind; Scientology (1953) added the spiritual layer (the thetan) and the religious branding.

山达基非建立于人格神或所启示之经文,故不属于本页所保留之"以对神之信仰为根基"严格意义上之宗教家族。其 1953 年被指定为"宗教",是 Hubbard 一个深思熟虑之法律与税务举措,正式化于一份备忘录("宗教角度"信函),后在诉讼中浮出。其恰当谱系是二十世纪美国之一种混合体,合新灵性传统与通俗科学自助,无神学核心。五条支流:(一)神智学(Blavatsky 1875,带其"大师"等级、多重微妙身体、与渐升之灵性发展层级);(二)新思想(Quimby、Eddy,十九世纪末——心智作为物质之决定者,疾病作为心理缺陷被纠正);(三)弗洛伊德与后弗洛伊德深度心理学(无意识作为待被揭示与释放之创伤性印痕之贮存所——Hubbard 之"印痕"是对弗洛伊德 Verdrängung 之直接重新挪用);(四)Aleister Crowley 之仪式魔法(Hubbard 1946 年参与 Jack Parsons 在 Pasadena 家中之 Babalon Working 仪式,记载于 Parsons 之日记与后续传记中);(五)黄金时代通俗科幻(Hubbard 是 1930-40 年代多产之通俗作家;OT III 之 Xenu 宇宙论,以体裁论之,即一 1940 年代之太空歌剧)。戴尼提(1950)以心智科学之名销售;山达基(1953)加上灵性层面(theta)与宗教品牌。

Doctrinal Sources
教义来源

The textual sources are Hubbard's own. The foundational text is Dianetics: The Modern Science of Mental Health (1950), which introduces the engram theory and the auditing procedure. The doctrine of the thetan appears in Scientology 8-8008 (1952) and is elaborated in the Phoenix Lectures (1954). The cosmological narrative culminating in Xenu and the volcanic-implant story is contained in the OT III materials, hand-written by Hubbard and revealed only to members at the appropriate level. The complete Hubbard corpus exceeds 500 books and lectures; all are treated as authoritative, with no internal mechanism for revision. The structural form of the doctrine — a trapped immortal self, layered cosmic history, esoteric knowledge progressively revealed — is recognisably Gnostic in pattern, although Hubbard rejected the comparison and presented Scientology as scientific.

文本来源是 Hubbard 自己之作品。奠基性文本是《戴尼提:现代心智健康科学》(1950),介绍印痕理论与听析程序。theta 之教义出现于《山达基 8-8008》(1952),并在《凤凰演讲》(1954)中加以阐发。以 Xenu 与火山植入故事告终之宇宙论叙事,载于 OT III 材料,由 Hubbard 亲笔写就,只向达到相应等级之成员揭示。Hubbard 之完整文集超过 500 本书与演讲;所有皆被视为权威,无内部修订机制。其教义之结构形式——被困之不朽自我、多层宇宙史、秘传知识渐进揭示——在模式上可识别地是灵知派的,虽然 Hubbard 拒绝此比较,并将山达基呈现为科学的。

Doctrinal Comparison
教义对照
Dimension New-Spirituality Traditions + Empirical Science Scientology 维度 新灵性传统 + 经验科学 山达基
Supreme being 至高存在 Either an impersonal absolute (Theosophy, New Thought) or no metaphysical claim (science) 或为非人格之绝对者(神智学、新思想),或无形而上学主张(科学) "Eighth Dynamic" — deliberately unspecified; no personal God "第八动力"——刻意未指定;无人格神
Knowledge model 知识模型 Science: open publication, peer review, falsifiability; New-spirituality: open inspiration accessible to all 科学:公开出版、同行评议、可证伪;新灵性:开放灵感,人人可及 Tiered esoteric secrets (OT levels), released only after payment and verified loyalty; non-disclosure required 分层之秘传秘密(OT 等级),只在付款并经验证忠诚后释出;要求保密

Heresy Status
异端判定

Not applicable in the strict religious sense, since Scientology is not built on belief in God. There is no theological parent tradition that could classify it as heresy. Two parallel judgements can however be made. From science: Dianetics's claims about engrams, auditing efficacy, and the E-meter's diagnostic function were tested in the early 1950s by mainstream psychology and medicine and found to be unfalsifiable or false; the American Psychological Association issued a formal warning in 1950. Scientology's epistemic posture — its refusal to submit OT-level claims for external verification, its treatment of internal scrutiny as suppressive — is incompatible with scientific norms. From the new-spirituality traditions Scientology descends from: Theosophical and New Thought communities have generally regarded Scientology as a commercialised, hierarchically authoritarian distortion of their open-spiritual tradition. The pattern of secrecy, payment-gated access, and policy-driven harassment of critics has no antecedent in Theosophical or New Thought practice. By the standards of either parent — empirical science or open new-spirituality — Scientology is doctrinally and behaviourally deviant.

在严格之宗教意义上不适用,因山达基不建立于对神之信仰。无任何神学母传统能将其归类为异端。然两项平行判断可作。从科学:戴尼提关于印痕、听析效力、与 E-meter 诊断功能之主张,1950 年代初被主流心理学与医学检验,被认定为不可证伪或假;美国心理学会 1950 年发出正式警告。山达基之认识论姿态——拒绝将 OT 等级主张提交外部验证、将内部审查视作抑制性——与科学规范不兼容。从其所源出之新灵性传统:神智学与新思想共同体,普遍将山达基视为对其开放灵性传统之商业化、等级专制之扭曲。保密、付款门控访问、与政策驱动之骚扰批评者之模式,在神智学或新思想实践中并无前例。按任一母系——经验科学或开放新灵性——之标准,山达基在教义上与行为上皆是偏离的。

Mainstream Position
主流定位

Scientology's legal status as a religion varies by jurisdiction. United States: recognised as a tax-exempt religion since 1993, after sustained litigation against the IRS. Germany: classified as a commercial enterprise rather than a religion; placed under federal intelligence (Bundesamt für Verfassungsschutz) observation 1997–2008. France: classified as a sect (secte) by the 1995 Guyard Report; convicted of organised fraud in 2009 (case upheld in 2013). Belgium: criminal investigations 1997–2016 on fraud, extortion, and violations of privacy laws. The 1953 self-designation as a religion has held in some jurisdictions and failed in others, exactly as one would expect from a movement whose religious status is the product of legal positioning rather than doctrinal continuity with any prior religious tradition.

山达基作为宗教之法律地位因司法辖区而异。美国:1993 年起经对国税局之持续诉讼,被承认为免税宗教。德国:被归类为商业企业而非宗教;1997-2008 年置于联邦宪法保卫局(Bundesamt für Verfassungsschutz)之监察下。法国:1995 年 Guyard 报告将其归类为宗派(secte);2009 年被裁定为有组织诈骗罪(2013 年终审维持)。比利时:1997-2016 年因诈骗、勒索与违反隐私法接受刑事调查。1953 年之宗教自我指定,在某些司法辖区被认可,在另一些被驳回——这正符合"一个其宗教地位是法律定位之产物、而非与任何先前宗教传统具教义连续性"之运动之预期。

Origin and Self-Presentation

起源与自我呈现

L. Ron Hubbard, a pulp science-fiction writer, founded Dianetics in 1950 as a self-help system based on the proposed clearing of negative engrams from the human mind through a procedure he termed auditing. By 1953 the system had been re-presented as a religion, with the term Scientology and the doctrine of the thetan — an immortal spiritual being whose passage through countless lifetimes is the subject of Scientology practice. The organisation acquired tax-exempt religious status in the United States after a sustained legal campaign culminating in 1993, has substantial real estate holdings worldwide, and is among the most disciplined of large cultic organisations in its public messaging.

L. Ron Hubbard,一位通俗科幻作家,1950 年创立 Dianetics(戴尼提)——一个自助系统,基于将负面"印痕"(engrams)从人类心智中"清除"之程序,他将该程序命名为"听析"(auditing)。1953 年,该系统被重新呈现为一种宗教,带有"山达基"之名与"theta"(thetan)之教义——一个不朽的灵性存在,其穿越无数世之旅程,即山达基修行之主题。该组织经持续法律运动于 1993 年在美国获得宗教免税地位,在全球拥有可观的房地产,且在大型邪教组织中,其公共讯息纪律性最强者之一。

Doctrinal Anatomy

教义解剖

Hubbard's stated frame is technological self-help and a science of the mind. The underlying structure is recognisably Gnostic: a true self (the thetan) trapped in matter (MEST: Matter, Energy, Space, Time); salvation through esoteric knowledge progressively revealed only to initiated members; the highest knowledge (the OT levels including the Xenu cosmology) kept secret and represented as metaphysically dangerous to those not prepared. This recapitulates, in 20th-century vocabulary, the central move of Valentinian and Sethian Gnosticism c. 150–250 CE. Hubbard's specifically modern contributions are the secular-technological idiom (the E-meter, "auditing," engineering-style level numbering) and the legal-corporate infrastructure that made the system commercially scalable.

Two doctrinal doors carry the system. D-c (Gnostic dualism) in strong form: ordinary epistemic access is insufficient; only Scientology's inner pathway reaches the truth about reality. This pre-loads epistemic closure: any external evidence against Scientology can be reframed as the unenlightened world's predictable resistance to thetan-liberation. D-d (esoteric initiation) in strong form: the doctrine that the higher OT levels are dangerous to the uninitiated converts hierarchical knowledge asymmetry into a soteriological virtue, and binds members to the organisation by the very fact of their having paid for and received the higher materials. The category of the Suppressive Person — defined as an individual whose criticism is, by definition, evidence of his own pathology — is the operational expression of (c). The Bridge to Total Freedom, the tiered ladder of OT levels, is the operational expression of (d).

Hubbard 所声称之框架是技术性自助与心智科学。其底层结构则可识别地是灵知派:一真我(theta)困于物质(MEST:物质、能量、空间、时间);救赎在于通过仅渐进地向已受戒成员揭示之秘传知识所得之解脱;最高知识(OT 等级,包括 Xenu 宇宙论)被保密,且被表述为对未准备者形而上学地危险。这在二十世纪词汇中重演了瓦伦丁派与塞特派灵知主义(约公元 150–250 年)之核心移动。Hubbard 具体的现代贡献,是世俗-技术词语(E-meter、"听析"、工程式之等级编号)与使该系统具商业可扩展性之法律-公司基础设施。

两道教义之门承载该系统。D-c(灵知二元论)之强形式:普通认识论途径不足;唯山达基之内部路径达至关于实相之真理。这预装了认识论闭合:对山达基不利之任何外部证据,皆可被重述为"未开悟之世界对 theta 解脱之可预测抵抗"。D-d(密法授受)之强形式:"较高 OT 等级对未受戒者危险"之教义,将等级性知识不对称转为一种救赎论美德,并通过成员已支付并接受较高材料这一事实本身,将其束缚于组织。"抑制性人物"这一范畴——按定义,其批评即其自身病理之证据——是(c)之操作性表达。"通往完全自由之桥"——OT 等级之分层阶梯——是(d)之操作性表达。

The Four Conditions in Scientology

山达基中的四条件

(1) Closure: the doctrine includes the category of the Suppressive Person (SP), an individual whose criticism of Scientology is, by definition, evidence of his own pathology. Once one is classified an SP, his speech is filtered through the doctrine that he cannot tell the truth about Scientology. (2) Centralisation: after Hubbard's death in 1986, authority was concentrated in David Miscavige, Chairman of the Board of the Religious Technology Center. The texts left by Hubbard supply the doctrinal corpus, but Miscavige's role in interpreting them and revoking earlier interpretations is functionally identical to that of a living prophet — and at sufficient distance from doctrinally fixed scripture that no critical interpretation can be sustained against his pronouncement. (3) Exit-cost: the policy of Disconnection requires members in good standing to sever contact with any family member or friend declared an SP. The metaphysical exit-cost is the loss of progress along the "Bridge to Total Freedom" — the ladder of thetan development across lifetimes; the social exit-cost is the loss of one's family, since family members within the church will be required to disconnect. (4) Coverage: Scientology has procedures for ethics, marriage, child-rearing, work, dispute resolution, illness ("auditing" is presented as therapy for psychological conditions), and ultimate metaphysical destiny.

(一)闭合:教义包含"抑制性人物"(SP)之范畴——一个对山达基提出批评者,按定义为其自身病理之证据。一旦被归为 SP,其言说被通过"他无法说出关于山达基之真相"之教义所过滤。(二)单一化:Hubbard 1986 年身亡后,权威集中于宗教技术中心董事长 David Miscavige。Hubbard 所遗文本提供教义语料,但 Miscavige 在诠释这些文本与撤销既往诠释中的角色,在功能上等同于一位在世先知——且与教义上固定之经文存在足够距离,使得任何批判性诠释都无法对抗他的宣告。(三)出口成本:"切断"(Disconnection)政策要求在职成员与任何被宣告为 SP 之家人或朋友断绝接触。形而上学出口成本是丧失沿"通往完全自由之桥"之进展——多世 theta 发展的阶梯;社会出口成本是丧失家庭,因为教会内之家庭成员将被要求切断。(四)覆盖:山达基有伦理、婚姻、育儿、工作、纠纷解决、疾病("听析"被呈现为对心理状况之治疗)以及终极形而上学命运之程序。

The Legal Dimension

法律维度

Scientology is the case in which cultic structure has been combined with sustained legal sophistication. The organisation has pursued critics through extensive litigation; has been recognised as a religion in the United States, Australia, and Italy; has been classified as a commercial enterprise rather than a religion in Germany and a totalitarian sect in France's MIVILUDES reports. The legal asymmetry partly explains why Scientology has been able to use academic NRM literature in its own favour: where Scientology has obtained classification as a religion, the NRM framework has provided the academic vocabulary in which that classification is at home. This is the cleanest example of the practical consequence of the NRM-versus-cult vocabulary choice: the choice is not value-neutral, it favours the well-resourced organisation.

山达基是邪教结构与持续法律精明结合之案例。该组织通过广泛诉讼追究批评者;在美国、澳大利亚、意大利被承认为宗教;在德国被归类为商业企业而非宗教,在法国 MIVILUDES 报告中被列为极权宗派。法律层面之不对称部分解释了:山达基为何能够利用学界 NRM 文献为己所用——在山达基已获宗教分类之处,NRM 框架为该分类提供了学术词汇之归宿。这是 NRM 与邪教词汇选择之实际后果最清晰之例:这一选择并非价值中立的,它有利于资源丰厚的组织。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • Lawrence Wright, Going Clear: Scientology, Hollywood, and the Prison of Belief (Alfred A. Knopf, 2013).
  • Janet Reitman, Inside Scientology: The Story of America's Most Secretive Religion (Houghton Mifflin Harcourt, 2011).
  • Hugh B. Urban, The Church of Scientology: A History of a New Religion (Princeton University Press, 2011).
  • Leah Remini with Rebecca Paley, Troublemaker: Surviving Hollywood and Scientology (Ballantine Books, 2015).
IV · 5 NXIVM: The Secular Case NXIVM:世俗案例 +
Lineage 谱系
Parentage
母系

NXIVM, like Scientology, is not built on belief in God or on revealed scripture, and therefore does not belong to the strict religious-tradition family. Its lineage is entirely within 20th-century American secular thought: (1) Objectivism (Ayn Rand 1957 onward — rational egoism, the legitimacy of merit-based hierarchy, the "rational inquiry method" as an ethical absolute; Raniere cited Rand extensively in NXIVM training materials); (2) the human-potential movement (Esalen Institute 1962, EST / Werner Erhard 1971, Landmark Forum 1991 — tiered multi-weekend courses, confrontational therapy, "breakthrough" rhetoric, financial commitment as proof of commitment); (3) NLP and applied behavioural conditioning (Bandler and Grinder 1970s — Raniere's pre-NXIVM background was in the related "Consumers' Buyline" multi-level marketing); (4) Multi-level marketing structure (the inverted-pyramid recruitment model where each member is incentivised to recruit downstream); (5) Sadomasochistic sexual literature (the inner DOS or "Vow" structure of branding and master-slave bonds shows formal resemblance to Pauline Réage's Story of O (1954), though no direct citation from Raniere is documented). Raniere founded Executive Success Programs in 1998 with Nancy Salzman; reorganised as NXIVM (pronounced "Nexium") shortly after; created DOS as a secret women-only inner circle in 2015–17.

NXIVM 与山达基相似,不建立于对神之信仰或所启示之经文,故不属于严格之宗教传统家族。其谱系完全在二十世纪美国世俗思想内:(一)客观主义(Ayn Rand 1957 年起——理性利己主义、按功绩之等级合法性、"理性探究方法"作为伦理绝对者;Raniere 在 NXIVM 培训材料中广泛引用 Rand);(二)人类潜能运动(Esalen 研究所 1962、EST/Werner Erhard 1971、Landmark Forum 1991——分层多周末课程、对抗性治疗、"突破"修辞、以财务投入证明承诺);(三)NLP 与应用行为条件化(Bandler 与 Grinder 1970 年代——Raniere 在 NXIVM 之前的背景是相关之"Consumers' Buyline"传销);(四)传销结构(倒金字塔招募模型,每位成员被激励招募下线);(五)施虐受虐之性文学(内部 DOS 即"誓约"结构之烙印与主奴关系,在形式上与 Pauline Réage 之《O 的故事》(1954)相似,虽未发现 Raniere 之直接引用文献)。Raniere 1998 年与 Nancy Salzman 共同创立 Executive Success Programs;不久后重组为 NXIVM(发音"Nexium");2015-17 年创立 DOS 为秘密之只限女性内圈。

Doctrinal Sources
教义来源

NXIVM had no scripture proper. Its operative materials were tiered training modules (called "intensives"), proprietary, internally generated by Raniere with Salzman, and protected by copyright and non-disclosure agreement. Recurrent concepts in the training: integration (the resolution of internal psychological splits, framed as the goal of human development); limiting beliefs (false convictions inherited from family, society, or trauma that must be identified and dissolved); parasites (people whose unintegrated state drains others' energy — a category used to justify cutting contact); the curriculum (the body of NXIVM training as the path to integration). The DOS inner-circle materials added the soteriological reframing of submission: "collateral" (compromising personal information held by the master as guarantee of obedience) was described as a "sacrifice of attachment"; branding (Raniere's initials cauterised into the pelvic area of female DOS members) was described as a "commitment ceremony"; sexual submission to Raniere was described as a developmental opportunity to overcome internal limits. The transformation of ordinary words — "sacrifice", "commitment", "growth" — into operative cult-vocabulary is a textbook case of Lifton's loading the language (see III.2 in Chapter IV).

NXIVM 无严格意义之经文。其运作材料是分层之培训模块(称"密集课"),为专有的、由 Raniere 与 Salzman 在内部生成的、受版权与保密协议保护的。培训中之反复出现概念:整合(内在心理分裂之解决,被框定为人发展之目标);限制性信念(从家庭、社会、或创伤继承之假信念,需被识别与溶解);寄生虫(其未整合状态消耗他人能量之人——一被用以justifying断绝接触之范畴);课程(NXIVM 培训之全体,作为通往整合之路径)。DOS 内圈材料增加了对服从之救赎论重新框定:"抵押物"(由女主作为顺从保证而持有之毁损性私人信息)被描述为"对依恋之牺牲";烙印(Raniere 之姓名首字母被烧灼于 DOS 女性成员之骨盆区)被描述为"承诺仪式";对 Raniere 之性服从,被描述为克服内在限制之发展机会。普通词汇——"牺牲"、"承诺"、"成长"——被转化为运作性邪教词汇,是 Lifton 语言改装之教科书案例(见第四章 III.2)。

Doctrinal Comparison
教义对照
Dimension New-Spirituality + Mainstream Self-Development NXIVM 维度 新灵性 + 主流自我发展 NXIVM
Supreme being 至高存在 Open: spiritual traditions may posit absolute; self-development is agnostic 开放:灵性传统或设立绝对者;自我发展为不可知论 No metaphysical absolute; Raniere functions as the de facto highest authority 无形而上学绝对者;Raniere 作为事实上之最高权威
Knowledge access 知识获取 Mainstream self-development: courses scaled by complexity, materials available in print, criticisable in public 主流自我发展:课程按复杂度分级,材料以书面形式可得,可在公开场合被批评 Tiered "stripes" levels; inner DOS materials secret; all materials NDA-protected; external criticism = "parasite" behaviour 分层"条纹"等级;内部 DOS 材料保密;所有材料受保密协议保护;外部批评 = "寄生虫"行为
Treatment of body 对身体之处理 Body work: voluntary, reversible, regulated by professional ethics 身体工作:自愿、可逆、受职业伦理规范 Branding of female members with leader's initials; sleep restriction; calorie restriction 用首领姓名首字母烙印女性成员;睡眠限制;热量限制
Sexuality 性 Therapeutic context: zero sexual contact between facilitator and participant; ethical violation if breached 治疗语境:辅导者与参与者间零性接触;违反即伦理违规 DOS inner circle: sexual service to Raniere framed as developmental practice; coercion structurally built in via "collateral" DOS 内圈:对 Raniere 之性服务被框定为发展性修行;强制通过"抵押物"在结构上嵌入
Exit 退出 Participant ends programme at will; no continuing obligation 参与者随意结束课程;无持续义务 Departure means "collateral" can be released; financial, social, and reputational annihilation as exit-cost 离开意味着"抵押物"可能被释出;财务、社会、与声誉之毁灭作为出口成本
Heresy Status
异端判定

Not applicable. NXIVM never claimed to be a religion, never claimed metaphysical revelation, and has no theological parent tradition. The parallel judgements made for Scientology — that NXIVM departs from both its proximate parent (the human-potential movement) and the empirical-rational standards it loudly invoked — apply here as well. From its self-claimed standard of "rational inquiry": NXIVM's actual practice (NDA-gated curriculum, ad-hominem treatment of critics, refusal of external scrutiny) is the operational opposite of rational inquiry. From the human-potential movement it descends from: ESTalen, Landmark, and comparable training organisations have never branded participants, never operated secret inner circles requiring "collateral," and never institutionalised sexual access to the founder. NXIVM is, by the standards of its actual lineage, deviant. The fact that it had no religious claim does not insulate it from the structural analysis; it confirms (per the Chapter II argument) that cultic structure is realisable in secular as well as religious vocabulary.

不适用。NXIVM 从未宣称为宗教,从未宣称形而上学启示,亦无神学母传统。为山达基所作之平行判断——它既偏离其近端母系(人类潜能运动),亦偏离其大声援引之经验-理性标准——在此处同样适用。按其自称之"理性探究"标准:NXIVM 实际之做法(以保密协议门控之课程、对批评者之人身攻击式处理、拒绝外部审查)是理性探究之操作性反面。按其所源出之人类潜能运动:Esalen、Landmark 与类似培训组织,从未烙印参与者、从未运作需要"抵押物"之秘密内圈、从未将对创始人之性接触制度化。NXIVM 按其实际谱系之标准,是偏离的。它无宗教主张这一事实,并不使其免于结构性分析;它(按第二章之论证)证实邪教结构可在世俗与宗教词汇中皆得实现。

Mainstream Position
主流定位

Mainstream coverage of NXIVM after the 2017 New York Times exposé and the 2018 federal indictment has been uniformly negative. The human-potential movement and the broader self-development industry have generally treated NXIVM as a cautionary tale, though without a great deal of structural reflection on the family resemblances. Cult-studies academic responses (Janja Lalich's commentary, the HBO documentary The Vow) have framed NXIVM as a paradigm contemporary case. The 2020 federal sentencing of Raniere to 120 years on counts including racketeering, sex trafficking, forced labour conspiracy, and possession of child pornography settled the matter at the operational level. The deeper structural question — whether the human-potential movement contains doctrinal-substrate elements that make NXIVM-type emergence possible — remains, as Chapter II argues, largely unaddressed.

2017 年《纽约时报》披露与 2018 年联邦起诉之后,主流媒体对 NXIVM 之报道一致负面。人类潜能运动与更广泛之自我发展产业,普遍将 NXIVM 视为警示故事,但少有对家族相似性之结构性反思。邪教研究之学术回应(Janja Lalich 之评论、HBO 纪录片《誓约》)将 NXIVM 框定为当代典范案例。2020 年联邦判决 Raniere 120 年监禁,罪名包括敲诈勒索、性贩运、强制劳动合谋、与持有儿童色情物品,在操作层面结案。更深之结构性问题——人类潜能运动是否包含使 NXIVM 式浮现成为可能之教义底层元素——按第二章之论证,大体仍未被处理。

A Cult Without Religion

无宗教外衣之邪教

NXIVM (pronounced Nexium), founded by Keith Raniere and Nancy Salzman in 1998, was presented externally as a personal-development and executive-coaching organisation. Its public offerings — Executive Success Programs — were structured as multi-level training seminars not unlike many in the human-potential industry. The cultic structure was concealed within an inner organisation, "DOS" or "The Vow," disclosed only to selected female members, in which they were branded with Raniere's initials, required to provide "collateral" (compromising personal material to be released if they left or spoke), and subjected to coerced sexual relations with Raniere. Raniere was arrested in Mexico in 2018 and sentenced to 120 years in 2020. Allison Mack, Clare Bronfman, Nancy Salzman, Lauren Salzman, and others received sentences ranging from probation to fourteen years.

NXIVM(发音如 Nexium),由 Keith Raniere 与 Nancy Salzman 于 1998 年创立,对外呈现为个人发展与高管教练组织。其公共课程——"高管成功项目"——在结构上是多层次培训研讨会,与人类潜能产业中许多类似课程无异。邪教结构隐藏于一个内部组织"DOS"或"誓约"(The Vow)之中,仅对选定之女性成员揭示——她们被烙上 Raniere 之姓名首字母,被要求提供"抵押物"(若离开或发声则会被释放之毁损性私人材料),并被迫与 Raniere 发生性关系。Raniere 2018 年在墨西哥被捕,2020 年被判 120 年。Allison Mack、Clare Bronfman、Nancy Salzman、Lauren Salzman 等人被判从缓刑到 14 年不等之刑罚。

Doctrinal Anatomy

教义解剖

NXIVM had no afterlife, no scripture, no claim of divine revelation. Its public idiom was the human-potential industry — executive coaching, NLP-style rational training, integration psychology. The underlying structure was nevertheless Gnostic, transposed into a secular register: a true self (the "integrated" person, freed from "limiting beliefs") trapped in a fallen condition (ordinary human emotional and cognitive patterns); salvation through esoteric knowledge ("rational inquiry method") progressively revealed only to those who proved themselves through the tiered system of "stripes"; the highest knowledge, in the inner DOS/Vow circle, kept secret and operationally dangerous to those who tried to leave.

Raniere's specifically modern contribution was the substitution of secular salvation-language for theological salvation-language. D-c (Gnostic dualism) appears as the distinction between "integrated" persons and ordinary humans — a metaphysical hierarchy disguised as a psychological diagnosis. D-d (esoteric initiation) appears as the master-disciple lineage of stripes, with the inner DOS slavery as the highest "initiation." D-f (sacralised marriage / sexuality) appears in DOS as the soteriological framing of submission to Raniere: women branded with his initials, required to provide "collateral," and required to submit sexually were doing so within a framework that described these acts as personal-development achievements. The case is important precisely because the metaphysical claim was absent. The four organisational conditions were filled by a secular Gnostic-initiatory structure rather than a religious one. The metaphysical claim is not necessary; what is necessary is the construction of exit-cost as infinite within the system's terms, and Gnostic-initiatory grammar can do this without any reference to a god.

NXIVM 没有来世、没有经文、没有神圣启示之主张。其公开词语是人类潜能产业——高管教练、NLP 式理性训练、整合心理学。然而其底层结构仍是灵知派的,被移调入一种世俗语域:一真我("已整合者",从"限制性信念"中得释)被困于一堕落处境(普通人之情感与认知模式);救赎在于通过秘传知识("理性探究方法")——只渐进地向那些通过"条纹"分层系统证明自身者揭示——所得之解脱;最高知识——在内部 DOS/誓约圈中——被保密,且对试图离开者操作上危险。

Raniere 之具体现代贡献,是以世俗救赎语言取代神学救赎语言。D-c(灵知二元论)呈现为"已整合者"与普通人之区分——伪装为心理学诊断的形而上学等级。D-d(密法授受)呈现为"条纹"之师徒法脉,以内部 DOS 之奴役为最高"受戒"。D-f(神圣化的婚姻与性)在 DOS 中呈现为对 Raniere 之服从之救赎论框架:女性被烙上其姓名首字母、被要求提供"抵押物"、被要求性服从,皆是在一个将这些行为描述为"个人发展成就"之框架内行之。本案重要正因为形而上学主张缺席。四组织条件由一世俗灵知-受戒结构填充,而非宗教结构。形而上学主张并非必要;必要者是在系统内将出口成本建构为无限,而灵知-受戒之语法可在不涉及任何神之情况下做到此点。

Why the Secular Case Confirms the Definition

世俗案例为何确证此定义

NXIVM had no doctrine of an afterlife, no claims of divine revelation, no metaphysical cosmology. Yet it satisfied all four conditions. (1) Closure: Raniere's "rational inquiry method" was presented as the only valid system of reasoning; critics were dismissed as failing the method. (2) Centralisation: Raniere was the "Vanguard," holder of all genuine insight; Salzman was his second-in-command. (3) Exit-cost: the metaphysicalisation operated in secular terms — leaving meant the destruction of one's potential, the failure of one's life project, the loss of true human flourishing — and was reinforced by the threat of collateral being released. (4) Coverage: NXIVM members underwent thousands of hours of curricular training, applied to relationships, diet, professional choices, sleep, sexual expression.

The NXIVM case is therefore important to the present definition: the metaphysical claim is not necessary; what is necessary is the construction of exit-cost as infinite within the system's framework. A secular doctrine of self-actualisation can perform the same role as a religious doctrine of damnation, if the doctrine is configured so that departure means the negation of everything the system has trained the member to value. This is also why the four-condition definition does not commit the methodological move of treating "religion" and "cult" as adjacent species of the same genus. The genus is ideological community, of which religious and secular forms are both members.

NXIVM 既无来世教义、亦无神圣启示之主张、亦无形而上学宇宙论。然而它满足四条件。(一)闭合:Raniere 之"理性探究方法"被呈现为唯一有效之推理系统;批评者被斥为未掌握该方法。(二)单一化:Raniere 为"先锋"(Vanguard),所有真正洞见之持有者;Salzman 为其副手。(三)出口成本:形而上学化以世俗方式运作——离开意味着自身潜能之毁灭、人生项目之失败、真正之人之繁荣的丧失——且被"抵押物将被释放"之威胁所强化。(四)覆盖:NXIVM 成员经历数千小时课程训练,应用于关系、饮食、职业选择、睡眠、性表达。

NXIVM 因此对本定义重要:形而上学主张非必要;必要者是在系统框架内将出口成本建构为无限。一个世俗的自我实现教义可扮演与宗教永罚教义相同之角色,只要该教义被配置为:离开意味着对系统所训练成员去珍视之一切的否定。这亦说明为何四条定义不犯方法论错误,即把"宗教"与"邪教"视作同一属下的相邻种。其属是意识形态共同体(ideological community),宗教与世俗形式同为其成员。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • Sarah Edmondson with Kristine Gasbarre, Scarred: The True Story of How I Escaped NXIVM (Chronicle Prism, 2019).
  • Catherine Oxenberg, Captive: A Mother's Crusade to Save Her Daughter from a Terrifying Cult (Gallery Books, 2018).
  • United States v. Raniere et al., Case No. 1:18-cr-00204, U.S. District Court for the Eastern District of New York.
  • Mark Vicente, Sarah Edmondson et al., The Vow (HBO documentary series, two seasons, 2020 and 2022).
V · 6 The Church of Almighty God 全能神教会 +
Lineage 谱系
Parentage
母系

The Church of Almighty God (CAG) has a doubly inherited doctrinal substrate. Its primary parent is Chinese house-church evangelical Pentecostalism of the 1980s and 1990s — itself descended from Western Pentecostal-Charismatic missions to China (most influentially the China Inland Mission and the Norwegian Pentecostal mission of the early 20th century, plus later Hong Kong / Taiwan / Korean influence). Founder Zhao Weishan (赵维山) was active in the Shouters (呼喊派, Witness Lee's offshoot of the Local Churches movement of Watchman Nee, itself a Plymouth-Brethren-derived Chinese restorationist tradition) before founding CAG in Henan c. 1991. The secondary parent is the Chinese folk-religious substrate of female millenarian figures — most directly the Eternal Venerable Mother (无生老母, Wúshēng Lǎomǔ) of the White Lotus and Yellow Sky (黄天) traditions, which run from the Ming through the Qing and reappear in early 20th-century Yiguandao (一贯道). The female embodiment of CAG's "Almighty God" — a woman named Yang Xiangbin (杨向斌) — sits at the precise intersection of these two parent streams: a female Christ-returned, intelligible to evangelical converts as the Second Coming and intelligible to folk-religious converts as the latest manifestation of the Eternal Venerable Mother. Zhao and Yang fled to the United States c. 2000; the movement continues to operate transnationally from Korea, the US, and Italy, with active membership in China that internal documents estimate in the millions.

全能神教会(CAG)具双重继承之教义底层。其首要母系是 1980-90 年代之中国家庭教会福音派五旬节运动——后者本身源出于西方五旬节-灵恩派对华传教(影响最大者为中国内地会与二十世纪初挪威五旬节传教,加之后来香港/台湾/韩国之影响)。创办人赵维山在创立 CAG 之前(约 1991 年河南),曾活跃于呼喊派(李常受所分立之倪柝声地方教会运动支派,而地方教会本身是源出于普利茅斯弟兄会之中国复原主义传统)。其次要母系是中国民间宗教中女性千禧年人物之底层——最直接者为白莲教与黄天传统中之无生老母,该线索从明至清贯穿,并于二十世纪初重现于一贯道。CAG"全能神"——一位名为杨向斌之女性——之女身道成肉身,恰处于这两条母系河流之精确交会处:一位女身基督再临,对福音派改信者可作为"再来"被理解,对民间宗教改信者可作为无生老母之最新显现被理解。赵杨二人约 2000 年逃至美国;该运动自韩国、美国、与意大利跨国运作,中国境内之活跃成员据内部文件估计在数百万。

Doctrinal Sources
教义来源

CAG's primary scripture is The Word Appears in the Flesh (话在肉身显现), a continuously-expanding corpus of utterances attributed to Almighty God (Yang Xiangbin), now exceeding several thousand pages across multiple volumes. The Bible is held to be authoritative but preparatory: it records the first two stages (Jehovah / Age of Law and Jesus / Age of Grace) but is now superseded by the third stage (Almighty God / Age of Kingdom). The Three-Stage doctrine has an obvious structural parallel to Joachim of Fiore's 12th-century schema (Father / Son / Spirit), though CAG does not appear to cite Joachim directly. The specific evangelical-Pentecostal sources include: standard end-times preaching (Mark 13, 1 Thessalonians 4, Revelation); the doctrine of continuing prophetic revelation (drawn from Pentecostal and especially Watchman Nee / Witness Lee positions on the Holy Spirit's contemporary speech); and the Plymouth-Brethren-derived ecclesiology of the faithful remnant in tension with the institutional church. The specific folk-religious sources include the Eternal Venerable Mother literature (e.g., the Long-flowering Sūtra, Jiulian Baojuan, and other Ming-Qing precious-scroll literature), in which a maternal cosmic deity sends three Buddhas (the third being Maitreya) to gather her children at the end-time. CAG's Three-Stage doctrine maps formally onto this folk schema: three sendings, three salvations, with the present being the third and final.

CAG 之首要经文是《话在肉身显现》,一持续扩充之文集,内容是归于全能神(杨向斌)之口谕,现已横跨多卷,超过数千页。圣经被持为有权威但仅为预备:它记录头两阶段(耶和华/律法时代与耶稣/恩典时代),但现已被第三阶段(全能神/国度时代)所超越。"三阶段"教义在结构上明显平行于费奥雷的若亚敬之十二世纪图式(圣父/圣子/圣灵),虽然 CAG 看来不直接引用若亚敬。具体之福音派-五旬节派来源包括:标准末世讲道(《马可福音》13、《帖撒罗尼迦前书》4、《启示录》);持续先知启示之教义(取自五旬节派,尤其是倪柝声/李常受对圣灵当代说话之立场);与源出于普利茅斯弟兄会之教会论——信徒余民与制度性教会之张力。具体之民间宗教来源包括无生老母文学(如《长生宝卷》、《九莲宝卷》与其他明清宝卷文献),其中一位母系宇宙神祇在末世派遣三位佛(第三位为弥勒)聚集其儿女。CAG 之"三阶段"教义在形式上与此民间图式对应:三度派遣、三度救赎,而当下即为第三亦即最终之一。

Doctrinal Comparison
教义对照
