Canon 正典 Bible (66 books) closed and supreme; no new scripture 圣经(66 卷)封闭且至高;无新经文 Bible preparatory; The Word Appears in the Flesh is the present authoritative revelation 圣经仅为预备;《话在肉身显现》为当下权威启示
Christ 基督 One historical incarnation (Jesus); his return is future, visible, glorious (1 Thess. 4) 一次历史道成肉身(耶稣);其再临在未来,可见,荣耀(《帖前》4) Two completed incarnations (Jesus + Almighty God / Yang Xiangbin); the second has occurred in China in female form 两次已完成之道成肉身(耶稣 + 全能神/杨向斌);第二次已在中国以女身发生
Soteriology 救赎论 Salvation by faith in Christ's atoning death and resurrection; available to all who believe 通过对基督赎罪之死与复活之信而得救赎;一切相信者皆可得 Salvation requires recognition of Almighty God in her present form; mere belief in Jesus is now insufficient 救赎要求承认全能神之当下形式;仅信仰耶稣现已不足
Heresiological self-position 异端学自我定位 "Once for all delivered to the saints" (Jude 3) — no new dispensations "一次交付圣徒"(《犹大书》3)——无新安排 Three Ages: prior dispensations were partial and superseded; CAG holds the final dispensation 三时代:先前安排部分且被超越;CAG 持守最终安排
Outsiders 外人 Unbelievers are objects of evangelism and prayer; not to be harmed 不信者是传福音与代祷之对象;不应被伤害 Those refusing recognition of Almighty God are "evil spirits" facing imminent destruction; rare cases of operational violence (Zhaoyuan 2014) 拒绝承认全能神者是"邪灵",面临即将到来之毁灭;偶有操作性暴力案例(招远 2014)
Heresy Status
异端判定

CAG is unambiguously a Christian heresy by every classical and contemporary evangelical standard. The relevant criteria — closure of the canon (Revelation 22:18–19), uniqueness of the Christ-incarnation (1 Tim 2:5), the once-for-all character of the gospel (Jude 3), and the prohibition of "another gospel" (Galatians 1:6–9) — are violated frontally. Within the standard Reformed-evangelical heresiological taxonomy (developed in works such as Walter Martin's Kingdom of the Cults, 1965, and ongoing in the Christian Research Journal), CAG matches the criteria for what is termed "Christ-displacement cult": a movement claiming a new central authority that displaces Christ as the unique mediator. CAG itself accepts this classification only in the sense that it regards mainstream Christianity as having been left behind; the substance of the heresy judgement — that the canon is closed and Christ is the unique incarnation — it rejects.

CAG 按一切古典与当代福音派标准皆毫无歧义为基督教异端。相关标准——正典之封闭(《启示录》22:18-19)、基督道成肉身之独一性(《提摩太前书》2:5)、福音"一次交付"之性质(《犹大书》3)、与"另一福音"之禁令(《加拉太书》1:6-9)——皆被正面违反。在标准之改革宗-福音派异端学分类法(发展于 Walter Martin 之《邪教王国》(1965)与持续出版之《基督教研究期刊》等著作)内,CAG 符合所谓"基督-取代邪教"之标准:一个宣告新中心权威以取代基督独一中保地位之运动。CAG 自身仅在其将主流基督教视为已被超越这一意义上接受此分类;其对异端判决之实质——正典封闭且基督是独一道成肉身——则予以拒绝。

Mainstream Position
主流定位

CAG occupies an unusual position in that both Chinese state-sanctioned Christianity (the Three-Self Patriotic Movement and the China Christian Council) and the underground house-church movement — which usually treat one another with mutual suspicion — have publicly and repeatedly condemned CAG as a heresy (异端). This rare alignment across Chinese Protestant Christianity is itself doctrinal evidence: it suggests CAG transgresses something both sides treat as fundamental, namely the closure of the canon and the uniqueness of Christ. The CCC's Tianfeng (天风) magazine and the underground-church-aligned ChinaSource have both published detailed refutations. International evangelical organisations (the Lausanne Movement, the World Evangelical Alliance) treat CAG as a heretical movement. The PRC state classifies CAG as an 邪教 (cult) under Article 300 of the Criminal Law and has prosecuted thousands of members; following the 2014 Zhaoyuan McDonald's murder of Wu Shuoyan (吴硕艳), the prosecution intensified. The complication, addressed in Chapter IX, is that PRC state action against CAG is heavy-handed in ways that have drawn international criticism from religious-liberty bodies, even where those same bodies recognise CAG's structural pathology. Both judgements — CAG is a heretical cult; the PRC response is sometimes disproportionate — can be true simultaneously.

CAG 占据一个不寻常之位置:中国官方基督教(三自爱国运动与中国基督教协会)与地下家庭教会运动——通常彼此互怀疑虑——双方皆公开且反复将 CAG 谴责为异端。中国新教基督教内部之此种罕见对齐,本身即教义证据:它暗示 CAG 跨越了双方皆视为根本之物,即正典之封闭与基督之独一性。中国基督教协会之《天风》杂志与与地下教会有关联之 ChinaSource,皆已出版详细驳斥。国际福音派组织(洛桑运动、世界福音派联盟)将 CAG 视为异端运动。中国国家依《刑法》第 300 条将 CAG 归类为邪教,已起诉数千名成员;2014 年招远麦当劳杀害吴硕艳事件后,起诉强度增加。第九章所处理之复杂性在于:中国国家对 CAG 之行动以某些方式过于严厉,以致连承认 CAG 结构性病理之宗教自由机构亦提出过国际批评。两种判断——CAG 是异端邪教;中国之回应有时不成比例——可同时为真。

Origin and Theology

起源与神学

The Church of Almighty God (全能神教会), also known as Eastern Lightning (东方闪电) after a phrase in Matthew 24:27, emerged in the early 1990s in Henan Province. Its founding teacher Zhao Weishan (赵维山) declared that a woman in his circle — Yang Xiangbin (杨向斌), referred to in the movement's literature simply as "Almighty God" — was the second incarnation of Christ, returned in female form to perform the third and final stage of God's work: a stage that completes what was insufficient in the first stage (Jehovah, the Age of Law) and the second stage (Jesus, the Age of Grace). The new stage is the Age of Kingdom; only those who recognise Almighty God in her present incarnation are saved; the rest, including ordinary Christians who continue to await Christ's return in the conventional form, face imminent divine annihilation. Zhao and Yang fled to the United States in the early 2000s and have continued to operate the movement from there. Internal estimates put membership in China at several million by the mid-2010s, though figures are contested.

全能神教会(亦称"东方闪电",取自《马太福音》24:27)于 1990 年代初在河南兴起。其创始教师赵维山宣告其圈中之一位女性——杨向斌,在教内文献中径称"全能神"——为基督之第二次道成肉身,以女身归来执行神之工作之第三亦即最终阶段:此阶段完成第一阶段(耶和华,律法时代)与第二阶段(耶稣,恩典时代)所未尽之事。此新阶段为国度时代;唯有承认全能神为其此世之化身者得救;其余之人,包括继续按传统形式等待基督再临之普通基督徒,皆面临即将到来之神圣毁灭。赵杨二人 2000 年代初出逃美国,自此在美国境外继续运作该运动。教内估算 2010 年代中期之中国境内成员数在数百万,但具体数字有争议。

Doctrinal Anatomy

教义解剖

The Church of Almighty God is, doctrinally, a near-textbook example of how an evangelical Christian doctrinal substrate can be operationalised into a cult by activating four of the six susceptible structures (D-a, D-b, D-e, plus implicit D-f) simultaneously. D-a (continuing revelation): the movement rejects the Protestant sola scriptura closure of the canon and posits a new authoritative revelation given through Almighty God's spoken utterances, now compiled in a continuously-expanding corpus titled The Word Appears in the Flesh. The Bible's authority is not denied; it is subsumed under Almighty God's interpretive supremacy, which exposes the earlier scripture as preparatory and incomplete. D-b (end-times eschatology) in its strongest possible form: we are at the very threshold of the Age of Kingdom; refusing to recognise Almighty God incurs imminent divine punishment; this-worldly action is required (recruitment, separation from unbelieving family). D-e (mystical theosis / divine embodiment) in its strongest possible form: a specific living woman is literally God incarnate. The female embodiment is itself an opportunistic theological move within the Chinese evangelical context — it draws on Pentecostal-Charismatic charismatic-prophetess traditions present in 1980s–90s Chinese underground Christianity, and on the rural-folk substrate of female-divine figures (Guanyin, Eternal Venerable Mother in White Lotus traditions). Almighty God is doctrinally positioned as both the Christian Christ-returned and the figure the Chinese folk-religious imagination was already prepared to receive.

The genealogical relation to mainstream evangelical Christianity is not "external corruption." It is doctrinal extension. House-church evangelical Christianity in China in the 1980s and 90s held: that the canon's authority is supreme but the Holy Spirit continues to speak; that Christ's return is imminent; that the official Three-Self Patriotic Church is compromised and only the underground remnant is faithful; that emotional charismatic experience and prophetic speech are normative. Each of these positions, taken to its internal extreme, generates Almighty God. The new revelation simply identifies who specifically is now speaking with the authority the substrate had pre-licensed. The Three Stages doctrine (Jehovah → Jesus → Almighty God) is a structural parallel to Joachim of Fiore's medieval Three Ages (Father → Son → Spirit); like Joachim's schema, it relativises the previous dispensations by subordinating them to a third and final one that requires recognition of a new specific historical agent.

全能神教会在教义上是近乎教科书式的范例,展示一个福音派基督教教义底层如何通过同时激活六个易感结构中之四个而被操作化为邪教。D-a(持续启示):该运动拒绝新教 sola scriptura 对正典之封堵,设立由全能神之口谕给出之新权威启示——现已被编纂为一持续扩充之文集《话在肉身显现》。圣经之权威并未被否定;它被纳入全能神之诠释至上权之下,后者揭示先前经文为预备性的、不完整的。D-b(末世论)之最强可能形式:我们正处于国度时代之门槛;拒绝承认全能神即招致即将到来之神圣惩罚;需要此世之行动(发展成员、与不信家人分离)。D-e(神秘合一与神化)之最强可能形式:一位具体之在世女性即神之肉身道成。女身化身本身,在中国福音派语境内即一机会主义之神学举措——它取材于 1980-90 年代中国地下基督教中之五旬节派/灵恩派女先知传统,亦取材于女神形象(观音、白莲教传统中之无生老母)之乡土民间底层。全能神在教义上被定位为既是基督教之"基督再临",又是中国民间宗教想象本已预备接收之那位形象。

与主流福音派基督教之谱系关系不是"外部败坏"。它是教义延伸。1980-90 年代之中国家庭教会福音派持守:正典之权威至上,但圣灵继续说话;基督再临迫近;官方三自爱国教会已堕,唯有地下余民忠贞;情感性灵恩经验与先知性言说为常规。每一条立场,推至其内部极致,即生出全能神。新启示只是辨认出:谁现在以底层早已预先授权之权威在说话。"三阶段"教义(耶和华→耶稣→全能神)在结构上平行于费奥雷的若亚敬之中世纪"三时代"图式(圣父→圣子→圣灵);如若亚敬之图式,它通过将前述之神圣安排从属于一个第三亦即最终之安排,而使其相对化——而这第三阶段要求承认一位新的具体历史能动者。

The Four Conditions in Operation

四条件之运作

(1) Epistemic closure: members are trained to read all external information — official PRC reports, media coverage, even mainstream Christian denial of Almighty God's status — as the predicted persecution of the faithful at the end of the age, which simply confirms the doctrine. (2) Centralisation: Almighty God, through Zhao Weishan's administrative authority, is the sole interpretive source; the doctrine is internally self-modifying via her continued utterances. (3) Exit-cost metaphysicalisation: departure means rejection of the only path to salvation in the Age of Kingdom, i.e., eternal destruction at the imminent judgement. (4) Concept-frame coverage: the doctrine pronounces on family relations (members are taught to disconnect from unbelieving relatives, including spouses and parents), marriage, sexuality, work, political allegiance, and the ultimate metaphysical structure of history. The 2014 McDonald's murder case in Zhaoyuan (招远), Shandong, in which six Almighty God members beat a woman to death in a McDonald's restaurant for refusing to give her phone number when approached for evangelism, is a paradigm instance of the doctrine licensing operational extremity: from inside the frame, the victim was identified as an "evil spirit" who, by refusing the message, had marked herself for destruction; from outside the frame, she was a thirty-five-year-old mother named Wu Shuoyan (吴硕艳).

(一)认识论闭合:成员被训练将所有外部信息——中国官方报告、媒体报道、乃至主流基督教对全能神身份之否认——读作末世对信徒之被预言之迫害,这反而证实教义。(二)单一化:全能神通过赵维山之行政权威,为唯一诠释源头;教义通过她之持续口谕在内部自我修订。(三)出口成本之形而上学化:离开意味着拒绝国度时代之唯一救赎途径,即在迫近的审判中永恒被毁灭。(四)概念框架覆盖:教义对家庭关系(成员被教导与不信亲属——包括配偶与父母——切断关系)、婚姻、性、工作、政治效忠、以及历史之终极形而上结构皆予以裁定。2014 年山东招远麦当劳血案——六名全能神成员在麦当劳店内因传教时一位女子拒绝给出电话号码而将其殴打致死——是教义授权操作性极端化之典范实例:在框架内,该受害者被认定为"邪灵",因拒绝信息而自标毁灭;在框架外,她是一位三十五岁、名叫吴硕艳的母亲。

Why Almighty God Matters for the Definition

全能神对此定义之意义

Almighty God matters here for three reasons. First, it shows the four-condition structural definition working symmetrically across cultural contexts: the case is not Western, the doctrinal substrate is Chinese-evangelical rather than American, and yet the structural features and the doctrinal-substrate analysis apply with no modification. Second, it shows the doctrinal substrate as doubly inherited — from Western evangelical Christianity (the Three Stages, the imminent return, the continuing prophetic voice) and from Chinese folk-religious traditions of millenarian female-divine figures (the White Lotus / Eternal Venerable Mother substrate documented by ter Haar). Third, it exposes a complication in the PRC legal apparatus: Almighty God is the central contemporary target of the post-1999 anti-邪教 regime, and the legal apparatus's response — mass arrests, criminal sentences under Article 300, the official reframing of victim Wu Shuoyan as a martyr for Chinese state secularism — is itself a partisan use of the structural category. The four-condition definition correctly identifies Almighty God as a cult; the PRC legal apparatus correctly identifies the same. Whether the PRC's coercive response is therefore justified is a separate question, treated in Chapter IX, and the answer is not yes-by-default.

全能神在此处之重要性有三重。第一,它显示四条结构性定义在跨文化语境中对称地起效:本案非西方,其教义底层是中国福音派的而非美国的,然而结构性特征与教义底层分析无需任何修正即适用。第二,它显示其教义底层是双重继承的——继承自西方福音派基督教(三阶段、迫近之再临、持续之先知之声)与继承自中国民间宗教中千禧年女性神祇形象之传统(ter Haar 所记录之白莲教/无生老母底层)。第三,它揭示中国法律装置中之一项复杂性:全能神是 1999 年后反邪教体制之当代核心目标,而该法律装置之回应——大规模逮捕、依《刑法》300 条之刑事判决、官方将受害者吴硕艳重新框定为中国国家世俗主义之殉道者——本身即对结构性范畴之党派性运用。四条定义正确地将全能神识别为邪教;中国法律装置正确地识别同一物。中国之强制性回应是否因此合理则是另一问题,在第九章中处理,而答案并非默认为是。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • Emily Dunn, Lightning from the East: Heterodoxy and Christianity in Contemporary China (Brill, 2015).
  • Massimo Introvigne, Inside The Church of Almighty God: The Most Persecuted Religious Movement in China (Oxford University Press, 2020).
  • David Ownby, "The Church of Almighty God and the Pluralisation of Religion in Contemporary China" in The Journal of CESNUR 3, no. 1 (2019).
  • B. J. ter Haar, The White Lotus Teachings in Chinese Religious History (E. J. Brill, 1992).
  • 招远市人民法院,《张立冬等故意杀人案一审刑事判决书》(2014 年)。
VII. Chapter Seven 第 七 章

Religion / Cult: The Boundary Problem 宗教与邪教:边界问题

The principal objection to the cult/religion distinction, repeated since the 1980s by Eileen Barker and her successors, is that there is no sharp line: every "religion" was once a small heterodox movement, every "cult" is somebody's religion, and the apparent line between them tracks social respectability rather than structural difference. This chapter takes that objection seriously and answers it from within the ontology of vagueness — a tradition with which any geographer who works on vague regional boundaries is well acquainted.

对邪教/宗教区分之主要反对意见,自 1980 年代起由 Eileen Barker 及其继承者反复提出:其间无清晰界线;每个"宗教"曾经都是小型异端运动,每个"邪教"都是某些人之宗教,且二者之间表观的界线,跟踪的是社会体面性而非结构性差异。本章认真对待此反对意见,并从模糊性本体论之传统中加以回答——任何研究模糊地区边界的地理学者,对此传统皆熟稔。

V · 1 Vagueness Without Obliteration 模糊不等于消解 +

The Sorites Argument and Its Limits

堆垛论证及其局限

The standard structure of the NRM objection is a sorites: at the early Christian Church one can find epistemic closure, centralised authority in apostolic succession, exit constructed as eternal damnation, and frame-coverage of the entire moral life — and yet the early Church is not "a cult" in the contemporary sense. By inducting from one borderline case to another, one arrives at the conclusion that no specific instance of the four-condition structure suffices to license calling an organisation a cult. This is the classical sorites move: from "a single grain is not a heap" and "if n grains is not a heap, then n+1 is not a heap" to "no number of grains is a heap." The conclusion is, of course, false — there are heaps — and the philosophical literature on vagueness (Williamson, Keefe, Smith) is the literature on what is wrong with the inductive step. The four leading responses are epistemicism (there is a precise but unknown line), supervaluationism (the predicate is true under all admissible precisifications), degree theory (truth values are continuous), and contextualism (the line shifts with conversational context). All four agree, against the sorites, that the existence of borderline cases does not entail the absence of a distinction.

NRM 反对意见的标准结构是堆垛论证(sorites):在早期基督教会中,可以找到认识论闭合、使徒传承中之集中权威、被建构为永罚之离开、以及对全部道德生活之框架覆盖——然而早期教会并非当代意义上之"邪教"。从一个边缘案例归纳至另一个,人到达"四条件结构之任何具体实例皆不足以使一个组织被称为邪教"之结论。这是经典堆垛之移动:从"一粒沙不构成一堆"与"若 n 粒不是堆,则 n+1 粒亦不是堆"推出"无论多少粒皆不是堆"。该结论当然为假——堆是存在的——而关于模糊性的哲学文献(Williamson、Keefe、Smith)正是关于"归纳步骤为何错误"的文献。四个主要回应是:认识论主义(存在精确但不可知之界线)、超赋值主义(谓词在一切可接受之精确化下皆为真)、程度理论(真值是连续的)、语境主义(界线随对话语境变动)。四者皆同意:与堆垛相反,边缘案例之存在并不蕴涵区分之缺失。

An Ontology of Vague Boundaries

模糊边界之本体论

Geographic ontology offers an instructive parallel. A "mountain" is a geographical kind without sharp boundaries: there is no precise contour-line height at which a hill becomes a mountain, and the transition is gradient. Yet mountains are not the same as hills, and a definition of "mountain" that admits the gradient (mountains have certain structural features — prominence, isolation, relief — to a sufficient degree) is a useful, testable, and ontologically defensible definition. The same applies to "valley," "city," "wetland," "forest." Vague regional ontologies are a well-developed research area within geographic information science (Smith and Mark, 1998; Bennett, 2001) precisely because the categories are real, the boundaries are vague, and the operational needs of legal, ecological, and planning systems require definitions that handle the vagueness without collapsing the categories.

Cults, as an ontological category, are vague in exactly the same way. The four conditions admit of degree, the borderline cases are real, and the underlying structure is real. The job of an ontology of cults is not to find the sharp line — there is none — but to specify the structural features that explain why the paradigm cases are paradigm cases and why the borderline cases are borderline. This is what the four-condition definition attempts. The NRM framework, by contrast, mistakes the absence of a sharp line for the absence of a structural distinction, which is a basic error in the ontology of vagueness.

地理本体论提供一个有教益的平行。"山"是一种无清晰边界的地理种类:无某一精确等高线高度,使丘变为山,且过渡是渐变的。然而山与丘不同,且一个接纳渐变之"山"定义(山以足够程度具备某些结构特征——突起度、孤立度、起伏度)是有用、可检验、且本体论上可辩护的定义。这同样适用于"谷"、"城"、"湿地"、"林"。模糊地区本体论是地理信息科学中一个发展成熟的研究领域(Smith and Mark, 1998;Bennett, 2001),原因正在于:范畴是真实的,边界是模糊的,而法律、生态、规划系统的运作需要,要求一种能处理模糊性而不消解范畴的定义。

邪教作为本体论范畴,以完全相同的方式是模糊的。四条件允许程度变化,边缘案例真实存在,底层结构真实。邪教本体论之任务,不是找到清晰界线——并无此线——而是刻画那些解释"为何典型案例是典型案例、为何边缘案例是边缘案例"的结构特征。这是四条定义所尝试者。与此相反,NRM 框架将清晰界线之缺失误认为结构性区分之缺失,这是模糊性本体论中的一个基本错误。

The Historical Religion Counter-Example, Diagnosed

历史宗教反例之诊断

Was the early Christian Church a cult on the four-condition definition? At certain moments — particular Pauline communities, certain proto-orthodox cells under persecution — it is plausible that the four conditions were satisfied to a substantial degree. The honest answer is therefore: some early Christian communities were structurally cult-like in some periods. This is not an embarrassment for the four-condition definition; it is what the definition correctly predicts. The history of religions includes movements that drifted across the threshold in both directions: a cult-like origin that institutionalised, accommodated external authority, and stabilised at a non-cult equilibrium (the Latter-Day Saints between 1830 and 1900 is the textbook case); and an established religion that, at moments of stress, regressed toward cult-like structure in some of its parts (counter-Reformation Catholicism in certain Inquisitorial offices). The four-condition definition is not a static taxonomy but a structural description that applies to organisations at moments of their history, and the fact that organisations move is not a defect of the definition but a feature of its truthful application.

早期基督教会按四条定义是邪教吗?在某些时刻——特定保罗派共同体、迫害下某些原始正统小组——四条件被相当程度地满足是有可能的。诚实的回答因此是:某些早期基督教共同体,在某些时期,在结构上是邪教式的。这对四条定义不是难堪;这正是该定义正确预测者。宗教史包含双向跨越阈值之运动:从邪教式起源出发,通过制度化、接纳外部权威、于非邪教均衡处稳定下来(1830 至 1900 年间之后期圣徒教会是教科书案例);以及一个既立宗教在压力时刻,其某些部分朝邪教式结构回退(反宗教改革中天主教某些宗教裁判所办公室)。四条定义不是一个静态分类法,而是一个结构性描述,适用于一个组织其历史之具体时刻;而组织会移动这一事实,不是定义之缺陷,而是其诚实应用之特征。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • Timothy Williamson, Vagueness (Routledge, 1994).
  • Rosanna Keefe, Theories of Vagueness (Cambridge University Press, 2000).
  • Barry Smith & David M. Mark, "Ontology and Geographic Kinds" Proceedings of the Eighth International Symposium on Spatial Data Handling (1998): 308–320.
  • Brandon Bennett, "What is a Forest? On the Vagueness of Certain Geographic Concepts" Topoi 20 (2001): 189–201.
VIII. Chapter Eight 第 八 章

The Phenomenology of Leaving 离开的现象学

Most people who join cults eventually leave them. The long-term retention rate of even the most successful cults is well below half; the modal cult member exits within a decade. The structural barriers to departure are formidable but not absolute. This chapter examines what is known about the phenomenology of leaving — what it is like, how it happens, what the post-exit period involves, and what the historical controversy around "deprogramming" can tell us about both the structural reality of the cult and the corresponding risks of intervention.

加入邪教者多数最终会离开。即便最成功的邪教,其长期保留率亦远低于半数;邪教成员中之众数在十年内退出。结构性的离开障碍虽强大,但非绝对。本章考察关于"离开之现象学"的已知者——它是什么样子、它如何发生、离开后阶段包含什么、以及围绕"去编程"(deprogramming)的历史争议能告诉我们关于邪教结构现实与相应干预风险的何种信息。

VI · 1 Modes of Exit 离开的方式 +

Drift, Crisis, Expulsion, Rescue

漂离、危机、被驱逐、被救出

Sociological research on cult exit (Stuart Wright, David Bromley, Janja Lalich) distinguishes several modes. Drift is the gradual loosening of commitment, typically over several years, in which the member's effective participation declines, peripheral involvements expand, and exit becomes possible because the metaphysical exit-cost has been quietly eroded. Crisis exit is precipitated by a triggering event: a doctrinal contradiction the member cannot reconcile (an unfulfilled prophecy, a leadership scandal), a personal disaster (illness, the death of a child, abuse that exceeds the member's tolerance), or a moment of external contact that ruptures the closure (an unfiltered conversation with an ex-member, exposure to material the member was not supposed to see). Expulsion is exit imposed by the organisation: members who have been declared apostate or suppressive, members who have lost utility, members whose continued presence threatens the leader. Rescue is exit through external intervention — historically including the contested practice of deprogramming.

关于邪教离开的社会学研究(Stuart Wright、David Bromley、Janja Lalich)区分若干模式。漂离是承诺之逐渐松弛,通常历时数年,在其中成员之有效参与下降、外围牵连扩展、且离开成为可能,因为形而上学出口成本已被悄然侵蚀。危机离开由一个触发事件促成:一个成员无法调和之教义矛盾(未应验之预言、领导层丑闻)、一个个人灾难(疾病、孩子之死、超过成员忍受力之虐待)、或一个打破闭合之外部接触时刻(与前成员之未经过滤的对话、接触到本不应看到之材料)。被驱逐是组织所强加之离开:被宣告为叛教或抑制性之成员、失去效用之成员、其继续在场会威胁领袖之成员。被救出是通过外部干预之离开——历史上包括"去编程"这一受争议之实践。

The Deprogramming Controversy

"去编程"之争议

From the early 1970s through the mid-1980s, a controversial practice known as deprogramming emerged in the United States: members of cultic organisations were forcibly removed by family members or hired specialists (Ted Patrick being the most prominent), held in confinement, and subjected to extensive counselling intended to break the cult's hold on their cognition. The practice produced some genuine exits but also caused significant harm: it was, in operational terms, a kidnapping; some subjects were physically restrained for days; some emerged worse off; and the practice supplied the cultic movements with a public-relations counter-narrative in which families and "anti-cult" actors were the aggressors. The legal pushback (notably Eilers v. Coy, 1984) effectively ended forcible deprogramming. It was replaced by exit counselling, voluntary intervention by the family with the member's tacit or active cooperation, which is the contemporary standard.

The deprogramming era is important for two reasons. First, it is one of the historical episodes most cited by NRM scholars to justify their preference for the neutral term: the abuses of deprogramming, they argue, were enabled by anti-cult rhetoric, and dropping the rhetoric should reduce the harm. The argument has weight as a critique of the rhetoric of the 1970s, but it is non-sequitur as a critique of the structural definition: deprogramming was wrong because forcible detention is wrong, not because cults do not exist. Second, the rapid replacement of forcible deprogramming by voluntary exit counselling, with comparable rates of successful exit, suggests that the structural hold of the cult is real (intervention is sometimes needed) but is not so absolute that physical force is required to break it (cooperation suffices). This is consistent with what the four-condition definition predicts: the closure is sufficient to prevent rational exit from inside the system, but does not survive sustained contact with material that the system cannot reframe.

从 1970 年代初至 1980 年代中期,一种名为去编程(deprogramming)的争议性实践在美国出现:邪教组织成员被家人或受雇专家(Ted Patrick 为最著名者)强行带走,被拘禁,并接受旨在打破邪教对其认知掌控之广泛咨询。该实践产生了一些真正的离开,但也造成显著伤害:在操作上,它是绑架;一些对象被人身限制达数日;一些情况变得更糟;且该实践为邪教运动提供了公关反叙事——家人与"反邪教"行动者反成施暴方。法律反弹(尤其 Eilers v. Coy, 1984)有效终结了强制性去编程。它被退出咨询(exit counselling)所取代——家人在成员之默许或主动配合下进行的自愿干预,此为当代标准。

去编程时代之重要,有两重原因。其一,它是 NRM 学者最常引用以为其偏好中立术语辩护的历史插曲之一:他们论证,去编程之滥用乃由反邪教修辞所致,放弃修辞应能减少危害。该论证作为对 1970 年代修辞之批判有分量,但作为对结构性定义之批判则是非随贯(non sequitur):去编程之所以错,因为强制拘禁是错的,而非因为邪教不存在。其二,强制性去编程被自愿退出咨询迅速取代——成功离开率相当——这暗示邪教的结构性掌控是真实的(有时需要干预),但并非绝对到必须以物理强制才能打破(协作即可)。这与四条定义所预测者一致:闭合足以阻止从系统内部之理性离开,但不能在持续接触系统无法重述之材料后存续。

Post-Exit Recovery

退出后之恢复

The clinical literature on post-exit recovery (Singer, Lalich and Tobias, Hassan, Goldberg) identifies several characteristic challenges. Identity reconstruction: the member's identity has been built within the cult's vocabulary and roles, which no longer apply outside; rebuilding requires categories the cult never supplied. Decision-making: members who left cults that micro-managed daily life often experience paralysis when faced with ordinary choices that the cult would have decided for them. Trust: having been deceived once, often by people who professed extraordinary love and concern, ex-members experience difficulty trusting any subsequent relationship. Residual phobias: cult-installed fears about leaving (damnation, ontological annihilation, betrayal of the cause) persist for years and can produce panic responses to mundane situations. Floating: episodes in which the post-exit member finds herself, often suddenly, re-experiencing the cult's framework as if from inside, with the same emotional weight, before the post-exit perspective reasserts itself. The recovery period is typically measured in years, not months.

关于退出后恢复的临床文献(Singer、Lalich 与 Tobias、Hassan、Goldberg)识别几个特征性挑战。身份重建:成员之身份被建构于邪教词汇与角色之中,在外部不再适用;重建需要邪教从未提供之范畴。决策制定:离开过度管控日常生活之邪教的成员,在面对邪教本会替他们决定的普通选择时,常经历瘫痪。信任:曾被欺骗——常被那些声称怀有非凡爱与关怀之人——前成员在任何后续关系中难以信任。残余恐惧:邪教植入之关于离开之恐惧(永罚、本体论消亡、对事业之背叛)持续数年,可对日常情境产生恐慌反应。漂浮:退出后成员发现自己常突然地,以与从内部相同的情感分量,重新体验邪教框架,直至退出后视角再次复位。恢复期通常以年而非月为单位计算。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • Stuart A. Wright, Leaving Cults: The Dynamics of Defection (Society for the Scientific Study of Religion Monograph, 1987).
  • Janja Lalich & Madeleine Tobias, Take Back Your Life: Recovering from Cults and Abusive Relationships (Bay Tree Publishing, 2006).
  • Lorna Goldberg, "Guidelines for Therapists Working with Former Cult Members" in Recovery from Cults, ed. Michael Langone (W. W. Norton, 1993).
  • David Bromley (ed.), The Politics of Religious Apostasy (Praeger, 1998).
IX. Chapter Nine 第 九 章

The NRM Debate NRM 之争

This chapter sets out, as fairly as the partisan framing of this page will permit, the case for the New Religious Movements paradigm — for the academic reader's benefit, and so that the present position can be tested against it. The chief defenders (Eileen Barker, J. Gordon Melton, Massimo Introvigne) made arguments of substance, and a serious working position should be able to state them with their full force before responding.

本章在本页面偏向性框架所允许的范围内,尽量公正地陈述"新兴宗教运动"范式之主张——为学术读者计,亦为使此处所采取之立场能在与之对照中受到检验。主要辩护者(Eileen Barker、J. Gordon Melton、Massimo Introvigne)提出了实质性论证,严肃的工作立场,理当能以其全力陈述这些论证,而后再加以回应。

VII · 1 The Case for NRM NRM 一方的主张 +

The Methodological Argument

方法论论证

Eileen Barker, whose The Making of a Moonie (1984) is the foundational study, argued that the academic study of unconventional religious movements requires methodological neutrality. The term cult, she observed, had become a term of public abuse by the late 1970s — used to mobilise hostility, to justify intervention, and to deny the religious character of practices that, on closer examination, exhibited continuities with religious traditions deemed respectable. To preserve the scholarly capacity to study these movements as social and religious phenomena, the field needed a vocabulary that did not pre-judge them. New Religious Movement, neutrally meaning a religious movement of relatively recent origin, was that vocabulary.

Eileen Barker,其 1984 年著作《Moonie 之造就》为奠基性研究,主张:对非传统宗教运动的学术研究要求方法论中立。她观察到,至 1970 年代末,邪教一词已成为公众辱骂用语——用以动员敌意、为干预辩护、并否认那些(仔细审视后)与被视为体面之宗教传统具备连续性之实践的宗教性。为保留对这些运动作为社会与宗教现象之学术研究能力,该领域需要一种不预先判定它们的词汇。新兴宗教运动——中立地指相对晚近起源之宗教运动——即此词汇。

The Sociological Argument

社会学论证

J. Gordon Melton's argument, developed across multiple encyclopedic works on American religion, was historical: every major religious tradition has, in its origin, exhibited features that observers of the time called cultic. Early Christianity, early Mormonism, early Seventh-day Adventism, early Pentecostalism were all, in their day, denounced in terms structurally similar to contemporary anti-cult rhetoric. The historical record therefore licenses a precautionary principle: scholars should be wary of using a term that has, repeatedly, turned out to have been applied prematurely to movements that subsequently institutionalised into recognised traditions.

J. Gordon Melton 的论证——展开于其关于美国宗教之多部百科全书著作中——是历史性的:每一主要宗教传统在其起源时,皆展现出当时观察者所称为邪教式之特征。早期基督教、早期摩门教、早期复临安息日会、早期五旬节派,在其时代皆被以结构上类似当代反邪教修辞之措辞所斥责。因此,历史记录为审慎原则提供了正当性:学者应警惕使用一个反复被证明过早地应用于"其后制度化为公认传统的运动"的术语。

The Religious-Liberty Argument

宗教自由论证

Massimo Introvigne, founder of CESNUR (Centro Studi sulle Nuove Religioni), has made the most explicitly civil-liberties-grounded argument: state action against "cults," from French MIVILUDES classifications to Chinese suppression of Falun Gong, has frequently been disproportionate, has frequently targeted minority religious groups whose practices the majority finds objectionable for non-cultic reasons, and has frequently relied on academic legitimation of the cult label. The NRM framework, by withholding that legitimation, can blunt the most coercive forms of state response. The argument applies most pointedly in jurisdictions where religious minorities have been subject to state hostility on cultural rather than structural grounds.

CESNUR(新兴宗教研究中心)创办人 Massimo Introvigne 提出了最明确地以公民自由为根据之论证:针对"邪教"之国家行动——从法国 MIVILUDES 之分类到中国对法轮功之压制——常不成比例、常以多数群体出于非邪教原因觉得反感之少数宗教群体为对象、且常依赖学界对"邪教"标签之合法化。NRM 框架通过不提供此合法化,可挫钝国家回应之最强制形式。该论证在那些宗教少数群体因文化而非结构理由受国家敌视之司法辖区中,最为切中。

The Response from the Doctrinal-Substrate Position

从教义底层立场出发之回应

Each of these three arguments has weight. Each also fails as a justification for the categorical abandonment of the structural distinction. The methodological argument is right that pejorative vocabulary is inadmissible in scholarship; it is wrong that any term that has carried pejorative use must be abandoned. Cult could be re-disciplined to a structural meaning, as this page attempts. The sociological argument is right that some movements once called cults later institutionalised into something else; it is wrong that this falsifies the structural definition for the movements that did not. The four-condition definition handles institutional change explicitly: an organisation moves into and out of the category as its structure changes. The religious-liberty argument is right that state action against "cults" has often been illegitimate; it is wrong that the appropriate response is to deny the structural reality. The appropriate response is to be precise about what state action is justified — namely, action against specific harms (child abuse, fraud, confinement) — and to insist that the structural label does not by itself license state response. Scientology is, on the four-condition definition, a cult; it is also a constitutionally protected organisation in the United States, and these two facts are compatible.

三种论证各具分量。每一种作为对结构性区分之categorical 放弃的辩护亦皆失败。方法论论证正确地指出贬义词汇在学术中不可接受;它错误地推断任何曾被贬义使用之词皆须放弃。邪教一词可被重新规训以达至一种结构性含义,这正是本页所尝试者。社会学论证正确地指出某些曾被称为邪教之运动后来制度化为他物;它错误地推断这证伪了对未如此者的结构性定义。四条定义明确处理制度变迁:一个组织随其结构变化而进出该范畴。宗教自由论证正确地指出针对"邪教"之国家行动常不合法;它错误地推断恰当回应是否认结构性现实。恰当回应是,对"何种国家行动是合理的"保持精确——即针对具体伤害之行动(虐童、欺诈、拘禁)——并坚持:结构性标签本身不为国家回应提供正当性。山达基按四条定义是邪教;它在美国亦是宪法保护之组织。这两个事实可同时成立。

Principal Sources 主要文献
  • Eileen Barker, The Making of a Moonie: Choice or Brainwashing? (Blackwell, 1984).
  • Eileen Barker, New Religious Movements: A Practical Introduction (HMSO, 1989).
  • J. Gordon Melton, Encyclopedic Handbook of Cults in America (Garland, 1986; revised editions thereafter).
  • Massimo Introvigne, "The Future of Religion and the Future of New Religions" CESNUR, 2001. CESNUR
  • Stephen A. Kent, "Scientific Evaluation of the Dangers Posed by Religious Groups: A Partial Model" Cultic Studies Review 3(2-3) (2004): 101–134.
NRM defenders' rejoinder to the four-condition definition
NRM 阵营对四条定义之再驳

A defender of the NRM framework might respond that the four-condition definition is itself susceptible to the same critique it makes of the legal-political definitions: that its application is value-laden, that "epistemic closure" or "exit-cost metaphysicalisation" are themselves judgements that smuggle in normative preferences (in favour of open inquiry, in favour of metaphysical naturalism), and that applying the definition will track the same in-group/out-group distinctions that the older anti-cult literature tracked, only with more sophisticated vocabulary.

NRM 框架之辩护者或许会回应:四条定义本身可被它对法律-政治定义所做之批评所反击——即其应用是价值负载的,"认识论闭合"或"出口成本之形而上学化"本身即是夹带规范性偏好(偏向开放探究、偏向形而上学自然主义)之判断,且应用此定义所追踪者,与较早的反邪教文献所追踪者一致,只是术语更精细。

Rejoinder
再再驳

The critique is partly correct: any definition of any social-ontological category is value-inflected at some point. The relevant question is not whether the four-condition definition is value-free (it is not) but whether the values it presupposes are defensible. The presupposed values are: that organisations should not engineer their members' epistemic capacities so that escape from internal manipulation is impossible; that authority should not be unaccountable to any external reference point; that members should not be threatened with infinite cost for departure; that conceptual frameworks should not foreclose alternative ways of describing experience. These are not merely first-person preferences; they are conditions for the very possibility of the consent on which the NRM framework's own civil-liberties argument depends. A defender of NRM cannot, without contradiction, ground religious liberty in the value of free choice while denying that the same value licenses the structural distinction the four-condition definition draws.

该批评部分正确:对任何社会本体论范畴之任何定义,皆在某一点上是价值负载的。相关的问题不是四条定义是否价值无涉(它不是),而是它所预设之价值是否可辩护。所预设之价值是:组织不应工程化其成员的认识论能力以致"逃离内部操纵"成为不可能;权威不应不对任何外部参照点负责;成员不应因离开而被以无限代价相威胁;概念框架不应封闭描述经验的替代方式。这些不仅是第一人称偏好;它们是同意之可能性条件,而 NRM 框架自身的公民自由论证正依赖于这一同意。NRM 之辩护者不能在不自相矛盾的情况下,既以自由选择之价值为根据为宗教自由辩护,又否认同一价值为四条定义所作结构性区分提供正当性。

X. Chapter Ten 第 十 章

Legal and Institutional Responses 法律与制度回应

Three jurisdictions display the principal contemporary models for institutional response to organisations that satisfy the four-condition definition (or, in NRM vocabulary, "New Religious Movements with high control characteristics"). The People's Republic of China criminalises the category itself. The United States declines to recognise the category and acts only against discrete criminal conduct. France occupies a middle position, with a state monitoring body that does not criminalise the category but tracks organisations against an enumerated list of structural risk factors. Each model has known costs and benefits, and none is straightforwardly applicable across regime types.

三个司法辖区展示了针对"满足四条定义之组织"(或在 NRM 词汇中,"具高度控制特征之新兴宗教运动")的当代制度回应之主要模式。中华人民共和国将该范畴本身入罪化。美国不承认该范畴,只对具体之犯罪行为采取行动。法国占据中间立场:有一国家监测机构,不将范畴入罪化,但根据一份列明之结构性风险因素清单监察组织。每种模式皆有已知之代价与收益,且皆非可直接跨政体适用。

VIII · 1 Three Models: China, the United States, France 三种模式:中国、美国、法国 +

China: Categorical Criminalisation

中国:范畴入罪化

PRC Criminal Law Article 300 criminalises the use of an "邪教组织" (cult organisation) to undermine national law, with the judicial interpretation specifying the definitional criteria summarised earlier. The model offers a high-resolution legal apparatus for action against the category itself, including criminal sanctions for organisers and for active members. Its operational target since 1999 has included Falun Gong, the Church of Almighty God (全能神教会), and several smaller groups. The model's strength is operational: it permits state action without the difficulty of building a separate criminal case for each violation a cult commits. Its weakness, considered as ontology, is that the definition embeds the political relationship of the organisation to the state in the constitutive criteria (clauses about "endangering society" and "undermining the implementation of national laws"). This makes the category functionally a political-legal category rather than a purely structural one. An organisation that satisfies the four structural conditions but does not threaten the state's interests would not, in practice, be prosecuted under Article 300; an organisation that does threaten the state's interests but does not cleanly satisfy the four structural conditions might be.

中华人民共和国《刑法》第 300 条将利用"邪教组织"破坏国家法律之实施入罪化,其司法解释指明前述总结之定义标准。该模式提供针对范畴本身行动之高分辨率法律装置,包括对组织者与积极成员之刑事制裁。其运作目标自 1999 年起包括法轮功、全能神教会与若干小规模团体。该模式之长处在于操作性:它允许国家行动,而无需为邪教所行之每一违法行为分别立案。其作为本体论之弱点在于:定义将组织与国家之政治关系嵌入构成性标准之中("危害社会"、"破坏国家法律实施"等条款)。这使该范畴在功能上是一个政治-法律范畴,而非纯结构性的。一个满足四条结构条件但不威胁国家利益之组织,在实践中不会依第 300 条被诉;一个威胁国家利益但不干净地满足四条结构条件之组织,则或许会被诉。

United States: Conduct-Based Enforcement

美国:基于行为之执法

In the United States, the First Amendment's Religion Clauses prevent the government from classifying any organisation as a "cult" with legal consequences attached to the classification. Action against cultic organisations therefore proceeds entirely through ordinary criminal law applied to specific conduct: child sexual abuse (FLDS prosecutions, Bateman), tax fraud and money laundering (NXIVM), domestic violence (numerous), human trafficking (FLDS, Bateman, NXIVM), murder and conspiracy (Aum operations abroad and various individual cases), assault (Scientology in selected cases), wage-and-hour violations (numerous). The model's strength is principled: religious liberty is robustly protected, and state action requires the burden of proving a specific crime rather than the burden of proving a contested classification. Its weakness, considered from the perspective of victims, is that the structural harm of cultic membership — the systematic re-engineering of the member's epistemic and decisional capacities — is not itself a cognisable injury, even when it is the source of every cognisable injury that the prosecution can establish. The lawyer who litigated against Jeffs cannot make "constructing infinite exit-cost" a count in the indictment, only the specific child sexual abuse that the structure facilitated.

在美国,《第一修正案》之宗教条款阻止政府将任何组织归类为"邪教"并赋予该分类以法律后果。因此,针对邪教组织之行动完全通过适用于具体行为之普通刑法进行:儿童性虐待(FLDS 诉讼、Bateman)、税务欺诈与洗钱(NXIVM)、家庭暴力(众多)、人口贩运(FLDS、Bateman、NXIVM)、谋杀与共谋(奥姆海外行动及各种个案)、人身攻击(山达基在选定案件中)、工资工时违规(众多)。该模式之长处在原则性:宗教自由受到稳健保护,且国家行动需承担证明具体犯罪之举证责任,而非证明一个有争议之分类之举证责任。从受害者视角考察,其弱点是:邪教成员身份之结构性伤害——对成员之认知与决策能力的系统性再工程——本身不构成可诉之伤害,即便它是检方所能证立之每一可诉伤害的源头。对 Jeffs 提起诉讼之律师,无法将"构造无限出口成本"作为起诉书之一项罪名,只能援引该结构所促成之具体儿童性虐待。

France: Monitoring without Categorical Criminalisation

法国:不带范畴入罪化的监测

France has, since 2002, operated MIVILUDES (Mission interministérielle de vigilance et de lutte contre les dérives sectaires), a state inter-ministerial mission tasked with monitoring and reporting on what French legal vocabulary calls dérives sectaires — "sectarian aberrations." MIVILUDES does not criminalise sectarian status; it identifies organisations against a list of structural risk indicators (very similar in content to the four-condition definition: mental destabilisation, exorbitant financial demands, rupture with the family environment, threats to physical or moral integrity, indoctrination of children, anti-social discourse, breach of public order, judicial action against the organisation, exfiltration of traditional economic circuits, attempts to infiltrate public authorities). It publishes an annual report, supports victims, and refers specific cases to ordinary law enforcement. The 2001 About-Picard Law also created the criminal offence of "abuse of a state of weakness," targeting the structural exploitation of members regardless of the organisation's religious status. The French model is the closest operational counterpart to the four-condition definition: it gives state action a defensible structural target without making religious classification itself a crime.

法国自 2002 年起设立 MIVILUDES(部际宗派偏离警惕与抵制使命),为国家跨部门机构,负责监测并报告法国法律词汇中所谓之dérives sectaires——"宗派偏离"。MIVILUDES 不将宗派身份入罪化;它根据一份结构性风险指标清单(内容与四条定义高度相似:心理失稳、过度经济索求、与家庭环境断裂、对身体或道德完整性之威胁、对儿童之灌输、反社会话语、违反公共秩序、对组织之司法行动、规避传统经济循环、渗透公共机关之企图)识别组织。它发布年度报告、支持受害者、并将具体案件转介普通执法。2001 年之《About-Picard 法》亦设立"滥用脆弱状态"之刑事罪名,针对对成员之结构性剥削,不论组织之宗教身份。法国模式是与四条定义最接近之运作对应物:它为国家行动提供一个可辩护的结构性目标,而不将宗教分类本身作为犯罪。

Toward a Comparative Assessment

朝向一种比较评估

No model is clean. The Chinese model is operationally effective but cannot be transplanted because its constitutive politics is incompatible with religious liberty as understood in liberal democracies. The American model preserves religious liberty but produces hermeneutic injustice as a side-effect, since the structural harm cannot be named in law. The French model is the closest to a workable balance but depends on a degree of state administrative competence and on a settled political consensus around laicité that does not exist everywhere. The honest conclusion is that the legal-institutional problem of cults is one of the genuinely hard problems in contemporary regulatory theory, and that the question of the right response cannot be settled by decisions about vocabulary alone. The vocabulary, however, is upstream of the response: if "cult" is not a category, the state cannot articulate a response to it; if it is a category, the response is contestable but it is at least articulable. The argument is that the category should be retained, at the structural level, and that the institutional response is then a separate question to be settled within the constraints of each polity's constitutional order.

无一模式干净。中国模式运作有效,但因其构成性政治与自由民主国家所理解之宗教自由不兼容,不可移植。美国模式保留了宗教自由,但产生诠释学不正义为副作用,因结构性伤害无法在法律中被命名。法国模式最接近可行平衡,但依赖一定的国家行政能力与围绕世俗主义(laïcité)的既定政治共识,而后者并非处处皆有。诚实的结论是:邪教之法律-制度问题是当代规制理论中真正的难题之一,正确回应之问题不能仅由词汇决定来解决。然而,词汇位于回应之上游:若"邪教"不是一个范畴,国家无法表达对它的回应;若它是一个范畴,回应是可争议的,但至少是可表达的。所主张者是:该范畴应在结构层面予以保留,而制度性回应则是一个独立的问题,需在每一政体之宪政秩序的约束之内予以解决。

  • 最高人民法院、最高人民检察院,《关于办理组织和利用邪教组织犯罪案件适用法律若干问题的解释(二)》(法释〔2017〕3 号)。
  • MIVILUDES, Rapports annuels (2002 onwards; available via the French government's official portal). miviludes.gouv.fr

XI. Chapter Eleven 第 十一 章

A Catalogue of Cults 邪教志

Where Chapter VI gives depth (six cases worked through in detail), this chapter gives breadth. The catalogue lists movements that satisfy Cult(G) by the four-condition definition O1–O4, organised by doctrinal lineage. Each entry gives only what fits a single line: founder and year, primary region, estimated membership, current status, and the key doctrinal deviation. For depth on any case marked V.x, see the corresponding section of Chapter VI.

第六章给深度(六个案例细致考察);本章给广度。本邪教志列出按四条件定义 O1–O4 满足 Cult(G) 之运动,按教义谱系组织。每条目仅给一行所能容纳之信息:创办者与年份、主要地区、估计成员数、当前状态、以及关键教义偏离。任何标有 V.x 之案例,详见第六章对应章节。

What this catalogue includes. Movements satisfying the four-condition organisational definition O1 + O2 + O3 + O4 (Chapter I, Def 3), with sufficient public academic, journalistic, or legal documentation for an independent judgement.

What this catalogue excludes. (i) New Religious Movements proper — traditions heretical from their host tradition but not satisfying O1–O4. Mainline LDS (Mormonism), the Bahá'í Faith, Unitarian Universalists, Christian Science, mainstream Seventh-day Adventists, Soka Gakkai International, and Ahmadiyya belong to this category, not to the catalogue. Heresy is not cult. See Chapter I, Th 1. (ii) Mainstream world religions and their accepted denominations. (iii) Movements that fall into NRM ↔ cult dispute and that the author has not personally examined. See deferred-cases note below.

本志收录何者。满足四条件组织性定义 O1 + O2 + O3 + O4(第一章 Def 3)之运动,且有充分之公开学术、新闻或法律文献以做独立判断。

本志排除何者。(一)严格意义之新兴宗教运动——相对其母传统为异端但不满足 O1–O4 之传统。主流 LDS(摩门教)、巴哈伊信仰、Unitarian Universalist、基督科学派、主流七日复临会、创价学会国际、艾哈迈底亚派属于此类,不属于本志。异端不等于邪教。详见第一章 Th 1。(二)主流世界宗教及其被接受之宗派。(三)处于 NRM ↔ 邪教争议中且作者未亲身考察之运动。详见下面之搁置条目说明。

Markers used. DS indicates date-setting heresy (Chapter III, D-b): the movement set a specific year or sign for Christ’s return or equivalent eschatological event. V.1 through V.6 link to depth case studies in Chapter VI.

所用标记。DS 表示设日期异端(第三章 D-b):该运动为基督再临或等价末世事件设定了具体年份或标志。V.1 至 V.6 链接至第六章之深度案例研究。

I · Christian-Derivative I · 基督教衍生
Movements that emerged from within Christianity and remain identifiable as Christian or post-Christian in idiom. Many activate D-b (end-times eschatology) in its date-setting form — a structurally inherited heresy by Matthew 24:36 and Acts 1:7. All entries here are Heretic(G, Nicene Christianity) by classical orthodoxy unless otherwise noted. 源出于基督教内部、且在语汇上仍可被认作基督教或后基督教的运动。其中许多以“设日期化”形式激活 D-b(末世论)——按《马太福音》24:36 与《使徒行传》1:7,这本身已是异端。除非另有说明,本组所有条目按古典正统皆 Heretic(G, 尼西亚基督教)。

II · Mormon-Derivative II · 摩门教衍生
Movements descending from the LDS tradition that diverge from Salt Lake’s post-1890 mainstream and retain the pre-Manifesto plural-marriage doctrine. All carry the doubly-heretical position discussed in Chapter VI.1: heretical by Nicene Christianity, and schismatic from mainline LDS. 源出于 LDS 传统、在 1890 年后与盐湖城主流分歧、并保留宣言前多妻教义之运动。所有条目皆持双重异端之立场(参第六章第 1 节):按尼西亚基督教为异端,且对主流 LDS 为分裂派。

III · Buddhist-Derivative III · 佛教衍生
Movements drawing on Buddhist (especially Vajrayāna and Mahāyāna) doctrinal vocabulary, often combined with apocalyptic or political content. Buddhism has no conciliar heresiology, but each entry violates one or more of mithyādṛṣṭi (wrong view), broken samaya (tantric vow violation), or parasitic teaching. 源出于佛教教义词汇(尤其是金刚乘与大乘),常与末世或政治内容相混合之运动。佛教无大公会议式异端学,但每条目皆违反邪见、破三昧耶、或寄生性教导中之一或多项。

IV · Hindu-Derivative IV · 印度教衍生
Guru-centred movements within or adjacent to Hindu tradition. Hindu orthodoxy is itself loosely defined; the criterion here is satisfaction of the O-set rather than departure from a fixed creed. 印度教传统内部或邻近之古鲁中心运动。印度教正统本身界定宽松;此处标准是 O 集之满足,而非偏离固定信经。

V · Islamic-Derivative V · 伊斯兰衍生
Movements originating within Islamic tradition (Sunni, Shia, Sufi) and crossing into cult structure typically through D-b (Mahdist eschatology) plus D-e (mystical incarnation), often combined with armed political dimension. 源出于伊斯兰传统(逊尼、什叶、苏菲)、通过 D-b(马赫迪末世论)叠加 D-e(神秘道成肉身)而跨入邪教结构之运动,常与武装政治维度结合。

VI · East Asian / Chinese Folk-Derivative VI · 东亚 / 中国民间衍生
Movements drawing on Chinese folk-religious substrate (especially the Eternal Venerable Mother / White Lotus tradition) or Korean / Japanese folk-Buddhist substrates. Several couple Christian conversion content with this older substrate (CAG, Shouters, World Mission Society). 源出于中国民间宗教底层(尤其无生老母 / 白莲教传统)或韩日民间-佛教底层之运动。其中数个将基督教改信内容与此较古老之底层耦合(全能神、呼喊派、世界传道会)。

VII · Secular / Thought-History VII · 世俗 / 思想史衍生
Movements without religious doctrinal substrate; emerging from secular intellectual traditions (Theosophy, New Thought, human-potential movement, Objectivism, Marxism, nationalism). For these, the heresy predicate is undefined (Th 2); only the cult predicate applies. 无宗教教义底层之运动;源出于世俗思想史传统(神智学、新思想、人类潜能运动、客观主义、马克思主义、民族主义)。对这些运动,异端谓词未定义(Th 2);仅邪教谓词适用。

Deferred cases. Several movements often raised in cult discussions are not listed because their classification is contested in serious scholarship and the author has had personal contact or interviews with several of them but has not yet completed systematic study. These include: Falun Gong (法轮功) — central to PRC anti-cult enforcement since 1999, central to international religious-liberty discourse since 2000; ISKCON / Hare Krishna; Brahma Kumaris; Shincheonji (新天地, Lee Man-hee’s Korean movement); contemporary Soka Gakkai International. Each requires more direct examination than the author has yet brought to bear. Entries will be added on completion of the relevant fieldwork.

搁置条目。邪教讨论中常被提及之若干运动未列入,因其分类在严肃学界本身存在争议,且作者对其中数个有亲身接触或访谈,但尚未完成系统研究。这些包括:法轮功——1999 年起为中国反邪教执法之中心,2000 年起为国际宗教自由话语之中心;ISKCON / 哈瑞奎师那;Brahma Kumaris;新天地(李万熙之韩国运动);当代创价学会国际。每一者皆需作者尚未做出之更直接考察。相关田野工作完成后,条目将被补入。

Diagnostic Checklist · Christian-Derivative (provisional) 日常诊断清单 · 基督教衍生(临时版)
Three doctrinal-layer tests against the Nicene-Christian host tradition. Each question corresponds to a hard scriptural or conciliar rule; any "yes" already constitutes heresy on that axis. The test identifies Heretic(B, T), not Cult(B). To diagnose cult status the organisational test O1–O4 must be applied separately (Chapter I §4 Diagnostic Matrix). 针对尼西亚基督教母传统的三个教义层测试。每一问题对应一条硬性经文或大公会议规则;任一"是"即已在该轴构成异端。本测试识别 Heretic(B, T),非 Cult(B)。诊断邪教须另行做组织测试 O1–O4(第一章 §4 诊断矩阵)。
Q 1 — Canon Q 1 — 正典
Does the movement accord any scripture outside the Bible the same authority as the Bible? 该运动是否将圣经之外的任何经典视为与圣经同等之权威?
Tests D-a (continuing revelation). Mainline Christianity holds the canon closed (Revelation 22:18–19; Jude 3). Texts triggering “yes”: Book of Mormon, Doctrine & Covenants, The Word Appears in the Flesh, Hubbard's lectures, Eddy's Science and Health, Ahn Sahng-hong's writings, the founder's prophetic utterances. 测试 D-a(持续启示)。主流基督教持正典封闭(《启示录》22:18–19;《犹大书》3)。触发“是”的文本:摩尔门经、《教义与圣约》、《话在肉身显现》、Hubbard 之演讲、Eddy 之《科学与健康》、Ahn Sahng-hong 之著作、创办人之先知性口谕。
Q 2 — Date-Setting Q 2 — 设日期
Does the movement set a specific date, year, or identifying sign for the return of Christ (or an equivalent eschatological event)? 该运动是否设定了基督再临(或等价末世事件)之具体日期、年份或识别标志?
Tests D-b (end-times eschatology) in its date-setting form. The prohibition is hard: Matthew 24:36 (“of that day and hour knoweth no man”), Acts 1:7 (“it is not for you to know the times or seasons”); Augustine, De Civitate Dei 18:53. Triggers: Millerites (1844), JW (1914/1925/1975), Branch Davidians, Heaven's Gate (1997), Camping (2011), Dami Mission (1992), CAG (“Age of Kingdom has begun”). 测试 D-b(末世论)之设日期形式。经文禁令是硬性的:《马太福音》24:36("但那日子,那时辰,没有人知道")、《使徒行传》1:7("父凭着自己的权柄所定的时候、日期,不是你们可以知道的");奥古斯丁《上帝之城》18:53。触发者:米勒派(1844)、JW(1914/1925/1975)、Branch Davidians、天堂之门(1997)、Camping(2011)、Dami Mission(1992)、全能神("国度时代已开始")。
Q 3 — Trinity Q 3 — 三位一体
Does the movement reject the Nicene doctrine of the Trinity — that the Father, Son, and Holy Spirit are three consubstantial (homoousios) persons of one God? 该运动是否拒绝尼西亚之三位一体教义——即圣父、圣子、圣灵是一神之三同质(homoousios)位格?
Tests Christology against the Nicene-Constantinopolitan Creed (325/381) and Chalcedonian Definition (451). Rejection forms: social-trinitarian polytheism (LDS), Arian-style subordination of the Son (JW, Christadelphians), modalist absorption (Oneness Pentecostals, JW), replacement by a different incarnation (CAG, Unification Church). Catholic, Eastern Orthodox, and mainstream Reformed bodies all treat this as the load-bearing test. 测试基督论是否符合尼西亚-君士坦丁堡信经(325/381)与迦克墩定义(451)。拒绝之形式:社会三位一体多神论(LDS)、亚流式之圣子从属(JW、Christadelphians)、形态论之吸收(Oneness Pentecostals、JW)、以另一道成肉身取代(全能神、统一教)。天主教、东正教与主流改革宗皆持此为承重测试。
Live result 实时结果

How the levels map. The classical heresiological tradition treats any one of these violations as sufficient for heresy; the three-question protocol gives diagnostic precision rather than a single threshold. Three "yes" indicates a movement near the centre of the heretical space (heavy heresy + standard cult candidate); a single "yes" indicates a movement on the periphery (heretical but possibly an institutionalised New Religious Movement). The cult question is separate: it requires the O1–O4 organisational test, not represented in this checklist.

Other host traditions. Equivalent diagnostic questions for Buddhist, Hindu, Islamic, and secular-derivative movements have not been formulated here. Designing such questions requires the same depth of familiarity with the host tradition’s orthodox standards (canon, conciliar tradition, authoritative interpretation) that Christianity supplies for the questions above. The author has not yet brought that depth to bear on the other traditions. Until then, this section is deliberately limited to the Christian-derivative case.

诊断分级如何映射。古典异端学传统视任何一条违反皆足以构成异端;三问协议给出诊断精度,而非单一阈值。三个“是”表示该运动处于异端空间之中心(重度异端 + 标准邪教候选);单个“是”表示该运动处于边缘(异端,但可能是已机构化之新兴宗教)。邪教问题是另一回事:它需要 O1–O4 组织测试,本清单不予表示。

其他母传统。对应于佛教、印度教、伊斯兰、与世俗衍生运动之诊断问题,此处尚未拟出。设计此类问题,需要与基督教问题所基于之同等深度——对该母传统正统标准(正典、大公会议传统、权威诠释)之熟悉。作者尚未对其他传统投入此深度。在此之前,本节有意地限定于基督教衍生情形。

Colophon 版本

Notes on the ontology of cults: organisational and doctrinal layers, the principal theorists, central case studies, the boundary problem, the phenomenology of leaving, the terminological politics of the New Religious Movements paradigm, and legal-institutional responses. The position is partisan along two axes — the kind cult is real (Chapter I), and certain doctrinal substrates produce it more readily than others (Chapter II).

A working document. Revisions and additions are expected as new cases are documented, as new theoretical work appears, and as the four-condition definition is tested against further material.

关于邪教本体论的笔记:组织层与教义层、主要理论家、核心案例、边界问题、离开之现象学、"新兴宗教运动"范式之术语政治、以及法律-制度回应。立场沿两轴具偏向性——邪教这一种类是真实的(第一章),且某些教义底层比另一些更易产出它(第二章)。

工作文档。随新案例之记录、新理论工作之出现,以及四条定义被进一步材料所检验,将持续修订与扩充。
